// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Text Size Helper
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
f_tsize(string s) =>
    s == "tiny" ? size.tiny : s == "normal" ? size.normal : size.small

// MOS ASCII strength bar (0-100 -> 10-cell filled/empty bar).
f_mosBar(float _pct) =>
    int _n = math.round(math.min(math.max(_pct, 0.0), 100.0) / 10.0)
    str.repeat("█", _n) + str.repeat("░", 10 - _n)

// Dynamic per-TF wave progress: distance consumed from that TF's origin toward its
// target (0-100). Physics/distance based — never a static phase-count lookup.
f_tfProg(float _orig, float _tgt) =>
    (not na(_orig) and not na(_tgt) and math.abs(_tgt - _orig) > 1e-10) ? math.min(100.0, math.abs(close - _orig) / math.abs(_tgt - _orig) * 100.0) : na

// NOTE (v17): the lossy on-chart phase helpers f_phaseAbbr (LQW/EXP·LQ/…) and
// f_chartPhaseLabel (collapsed Liquidation/Pre-Convexity/Induction) were REMOVED.
// They discarded the liquidation title + substate and forced every leg to read
// "Liquidation". The chart now renders the single Engine-1A authority string
// `currentDisplayPhase` verbatim as a persistent REGION label (see Section "DIE
// region-based display authority" below). Do not reintroduce a collapse layer.

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 2 — CORE PHYSICS ENGINE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ── Core physics on the FIXED L0 timeframe (M5) — v90 root-cause fix. ────────
// Computed INSIDE request.security so every history reference ([1],[3]) resolves
// on M5 bars (not chart bars). This makes all downstream physics-derived scores
// (beliefs, obs scores, direction probability, geometry, ERF dimensions)
// timeframe-independent. Returns current values AND every history-based flag.
f_phys(simple int _atrL, simple int _effL, simple float _effT, simple float _dispT, simple float _convM) =>
    float _atr = ta.atr(_atrL)
    float _vel = ta.ema(close - close[1], 3)
    float _acc = _vel - _vel[1]
    float _cvx = _acc - _acc[1]
    float _csm = ta.ema(_cvx, 3)
    float _mv  = math.abs(close - close[_effL])
    float _ps  = math.sum(math.abs(close - close[1]), _effL)
    float _eff = _ps > 0 ? _mv / _ps : 0.0
    float _dsp = (high - low) / math.max(_atr, 1e-10)
    float _cth = _atr * _convM
    bool  _bCS = _csm >  _cth and _csm[1] <=  _cth
    bool  _rCS = _csm < -_cth and _csm[1] >= -_cth
    bool  _bImp = _eff > _effT and _vel > _vel[1] and _acc > 0 and close > open and _dsp > _dispT
    bool  _rImp = _eff > _effT and _vel < _vel[1] and _acc < 0 and close < open and _dsp > _dispT
    bool  _bDec = math.abs(_acc) < math.abs(_acc[1]) * 0.8 and _vel > 0
    bool  _rDec = math.abs(_acc) < math.abs(_acc[1]) * 0.8 and _vel < 0
    bool  _bMic = _eff > _effT * 0.80 and _vel > _vel[1] and _acc > 0 and close > open and _dsp > _dispT * 0.50
    bool  _rMic = _eff > _effT * 0.80 and _vel < _vel[1] and _acc < 0 and close < open and _dsp > _dispT * 0.50
    bool  _vd70   = math.abs(_vel) < math.abs(_vel[1]) * 0.7
    bool  _vd50   = math.abs(_vel) < math.abs(_vel[1]) * 0.5
    bool  _vd85   = math.abs(_vel) < math.abs(_vel[1]) * 0.85
    bool  _vd55x3 = math.abs(_vel) < math.abs(_vel[3]) * 0.55
    float _mom    = _vel - _vel[1]
    bool  _accDec = math.abs(_acc) < math.abs(_acc[1])
    [_atr, _vel, _acc, _cvx, _csm, _eff, _dsp, _bCS, _rCS, _bImp, _rImp, _bDec, _rDec, _bMic, _rMic, _vd70, _vd50, _vd85, _vd55x3, _mom, _accDec]

// ── HTF MEMORY GUARD ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// On charts ABOVE H1 (H4 / Daily / Weekly …) a request.security() to a LOWER
// timeframe pulls a massive intrabar count and blows the indicator's memory
// limit. f_safeTF clamps any requested timeframe UP to the chart timeframe when
// (and only when) the chart is above H1, so HTF charts request NO lower-TF data.
// Intraday charts (<= H1) are untouched and keep full M1 / M3 / M5 granularity.
bool _htfMemGuard = timeframe.in_seconds() > 3600
f_safeTF(simple string _tf) => _htfMemGuard and timeframe.in_seconds(_tf) < timeframe.in_seconds() ? timeframe.period : _tf

[atr, velocity, acceleration, convexity, convSmooth, efficiency, displacement, bullConvShift, bearConvShift, bullImpulse, bearImpulse, bullMomDecay, bearMomDecay, bullMicroImpulse, bearMicroImpulse, phys_vd70, phys_vd50, phys_vd85, phys_vd55x3, phys_mom, phys_accDec] = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("5"), f_phys(atrLen, effLen, effThresh, dispThresh, convMult), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)

float convThreshold = atr * convMult
float atrSma     = ta.sma(atr, 20)
float volRatio   = atr / math.max(atrSma, 1e-10)
string volRegime = volRatio > 1.5 ? "HIGH" : volRatio < 0.7 ? "LOW" : "NORMAL"
float volMult    = math.max(0.5, math.min(volRatio, 2.5))

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 3 — HTF BELIEF ENGINE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

f_htfBeliefs(float _open, float _high, float _low, float _close,
             float _effT, float _dispT,
             int   _acceptB, float _convMult,
             int   _obLook) =>
    float _atr_htf  = ta.atr(atrLen)
    float _vel_htf  = ta.ema(_close - _close[1], 3)
    float _acc_htf  = _vel_htf - _vel_htf[1]
    float _conv_htf = _acc_htf - _acc_htf[1]
    float _convSm   = ta.ema(_conv_htf, 3)
    float _convTh   = _atr_htf * _convMult
    float _move     = math.abs(_close - _close[_obLook])
    float _pathSum  = math.sum(math.abs(_close - _close[1]), _obLook)
    float _eff      = _pathSum > 0 ? _move / _pathSum : 0.0
    float _disp     = (_high - _low) / math.max(_atr_htf, 1e-10)

    float _expScore  = math.min(_eff / math.max(_effT, 1e-10) * 50.0 + _disp / math.max(_dispT, 1e-10) * 50.0, 100.0)
    float _decayScr  = math.abs(_acc_htf) < math.abs(_acc_htf[1]) * 0.8 ? math.min(math.abs(_conv_htf) / math.max(_convTh, 1e-10) * 50.0, 100.0) : 0.0
    float _curvScr   = math.min(math.abs(_convSm) / math.max(_convTh, 1e-10) * 50.0, 100.0)
    float _abScr     = (_eff < _effT * 0.7 and math.abs(_vel_htf) < math.abs(_vel_htf[1]) * 0.6) ? 60.0 + _curvScr * 0.4 : _curvScr * 0.3
    float _liqScr    = (math.abs(_convSm) > _convTh * 1.5 and _disp > _dispT) ? math.min(_curvScr * 1.2, 100.0) : _curvScr * 0.5

    bool  _bullImp   = _eff > _effT and _vel_htf > _vel_htf[1] and _acc_htf > 0 and _close > _open and _disp > _dispT
    bool  _bearImp   = _eff > _effT and _vel_htf < _vel_htf[1] and _acc_htf < 0 and _close < _open and _disp > _dispT
    int   _dir       = _bullImp ? 1 : _bearImp ? -1 : 0

    [_dir, _expScore, _decayScr, _curvScr, _abScr, _liqScr]

[raw_dir_tf1, raw_expScr_tf1, raw_decScr_tf1, raw_curvScr_tf1, raw_abScr_tf1, raw_liqScr_tf1] = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF(tf1),
    f_htfBeliefs(open, high, low, close, effThresh, dispThresh, acceptBars, convMult, obLookback),
    lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)

[raw_dir_tf2, raw_expScr_tf2, raw_decScr_tf2, raw_curvScr_tf2, raw_abScr_tf2, raw_liqScr_tf2] = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF(tf2),
    f_htfBeliefs(open, high, low, close, effThresh, dispThresh, acceptBars, convMult, obLookback),
    lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)

int   dir_tf1     = nz(raw_dir_tf1)
int   dir_tf2     = nz(raw_dir_tf2)
float expScr_tf1  = nz(raw_expScr_tf1)
float expScr_tf2  = nz(raw_expScr_tf2)
float decScr_tf1  = nz(raw_decScr_tf1)
float decScr_tf2  = nz(raw_decScr_tf2)
float curvScr_tf1 = nz(raw_curvScr_tf1)
float curvScr_tf2 = nz(raw_curvScr_tf2)
float abScr_tf1   = nz(raw_abScr_tf1)
float abScr_tf2   = nz(raw_abScr_tf2)
float liqScr_tf1  = nz(raw_liqScr_tf1)
float liqScr_tf2  = nz(raw_liqScr_tf2)

// ── Phase 1 (visualization) — HTF / ITF / M1 zone ranges ─────────────────────
// Reuses the SAME tf1 / tf2 timeframes (and "1" = M1) already defined above for
// the belief engines. This does not add new detection logic — it simply reads
// Helper to return [highest, lowest] over 20 bars for zone visualization
f_zoneRange() => [ta.highest(high, 20), ta.lowest(low, 20)]

// each timeframe's recent price range so the L2/L1/L3 layers can be SHOWN
// spatially on the chart instead of only as numeric dashboard readouts.
[l2_zoneHigh, l2_zoneLow] = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF(tf2),
     f_zoneRange(), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)

[l1_zoneHigh, l1_zoneLow] = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF(tf1),
     f_zoneRange(), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)

[l3_zoneHigh, l3_zoneLow] = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("3"),
     f_zoneRange(), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)

// M1 ("1") and H4 ("240") price ranges — fixed timeframes (match se1 / se240
// structure engines) so their trace bands always represent M1 and H4 regardless
// of the tf1/tf2 bias inputs.




var int htfBias1  = 0
var int htfBias2  = 0
if expScr_tf1 > 60 and dir_tf1 != 0
    htfBias1 := dir_tf1
if expScr_tf2 > 60 and dir_tf2 != 0
    htfBias2 := dir_tf2
if decScr_tf1 > 70 and dir_tf1 == htfBias1
    htfBias1 := 0
if decScr_tf2 > 70 and dir_tf2 == htfBias2
    htfBias2 := 0

int htfAlign = (htfBias1 == 1  and htfBias2 == 1)  ?  1 :
               (htfBias1 == -1 and htfBias2 == -1) ? -1 : 0

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 4 — MARKET STRUCTURE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

float structPivH = ta.pivothigh(high, structLen, structLen)
float structPivL = ta.pivotlow (low,  structLen, structLen)

var float lastPivHigh = na
var float prevPivHigh = na
var float lastPivLow  = na
var float prevPivLow  = na
var int   structBias  = 0

if not na(structPivH)
    prevPivHigh := lastPivHigh
    lastPivHigh := structPivH
if not na(structPivL)
    prevPivLow  := lastPivLow
    lastPivLow  := structPivL

bool isHH = not na(lastPivHigh) and not na(prevPivHigh) and lastPivHigh > prevPivHigh
bool isLH = not na(lastPivHigh) and not na(prevPivHigh) and lastPivHigh < prevPivHigh
bool isHL = not na(lastPivLow)  and not na(prevPivLow)  and lastPivLow  > prevPivLow
bool isLL = not na(lastPivLow)  and not na(prevPivLow)  and lastPivLow  < prevPivLow

var float prevSwingHigh = na
var float prevSwingLow  = na
var float currSwingHigh = na
var float currSwingLow  = na

float swPivH = ta.pivothigh(high, pivotLen, pivotLen)
float swPivL = ta.pivotlow (low,  pivotLen, pivotLen)

if not na(swPivH)
    prevSwingHigh := na(currSwingHigh) ? swPivH : currSwingHigh
    currSwingHigh := swPivH
if not na(swPivL)
    prevSwingLow  := na(currSwingLow)  ? swPivL : currSwingLow
    currSwingLow  := swPivL

bool bullBOS = not na(prevSwingHigh) and close > prevSwingHigh
bool bearBOS = not na(prevSwingLow)  and close < prevSwingLow

// Buffered CHoCH used to flip wave DIRECTION (per-TF wave dirs + Engine 1A spawn).
// Requires close to CLEAR the swing by chochBufferATR*ATR — filters minor
// counter-swings in choppy ranges that were whipsawing the wave direction.
chochBufferATR = input.float(0.75, "Direction CHoCH Buffer (ATR)", group=GRP_STRUCT, minval=0.0, maxval=3.0, step=0.05)
bool bullCHoCH = not na(prevSwingHigh) and close > prevSwingHigh + atr * chochBufferATR
bool bearCHoCH = not na(prevSwingLow)  and close < prevSwingLow  - atr * chochBufferATR

if useStrictStructure
    if isHH and isHL
        structBias := 1
    if isLH and isLL
        structBias := -1
else
    if bullBOS
        structBias := 1
    if bearBOS
        structBias := -1

bool _structLabelsOK = displayMode != "Execution"
if showStruct and _structLabelsOK and useStrictStructure and not na(structPivH) and ecvShow_Highs
    label.new(bar_index[structLen], structPivH, isHH ? "HH" : "LH",
         style=label.style_label_down,
         color=isHH ? color.new(color.lime, 55) : color.new(color.red, 55),
         textcolor=color.white, size=size.tiny)

if showStruct and _structLabelsOK and useStrictStructure and not na(structPivL) and ecvShow_Lows
    label.new(bar_index[structLen], structPivL, isHL ? "HL" : "LL",
         style=label.style_label_up,
         color=isHL ? color.new(color.lime, 55) : color.new(color.red, 55),
         textcolor=color.white, size=size.tiny)

if showStruct and _structLabelsOK and not useStrictStructure and bullBOS and ecvShow_Highs
    label.new(bar_index, low - atr * 0.3, "BOS ▲",
         style=label.style_label_up, color=color.new(color.lime, 40), textcolor=color.black, size=size.tiny)

if showStruct and _structLabelsOK and not useStrictStructure and bearBOS and ecvShow_Lows
    label.new(bar_index, high + atr * 0.3, "BOS ▼",
         style=label.style_label_down, color=color.new(color.red, 40), textcolor=color.white, size=size.tiny)

bool structLongOK  = not requireStruct or (useStrictStructure and structBias ==  1 and isHH) or (not useStrictStructure and structBias ==  1)
bool structShortOK = not requireStruct or (useStrictStructure and structBias == -1 and isLL) or (not useStrictStructure and structBias == -1)


// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// FIXED-TIMEFRAME STRUCTURE ENGINE  (ROOT-CAUSE FIX — v90)
// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// PROBLEM SOLVED: Previously L3/L0/L1/L2 inherited the CHART timeframe through
// chart-native open/high/low/close/bar_index/ta.pivot*/ta.atr in Sections 2/4/5/6/8
// and Engine 1A. Switching the chart timeframe therefore moved every structure.
//
// FIX: One self-contained structure engine — f_se() — computes ALL nine structural
// components (Swings, BOS, CHoCH, Direction, Lifecycle, Point4, Invalidation,
// Targets, FRZ) using ONLY the series of the timeframe it is requested on. It is
// then instantiated ONCE PER FIXED TIMEFRAME via request.security:
//
//     M1  → "1"     (micro structure — new engine)
//     L3  → "3"     (was wrongly bound to M1 "1")
//     L0  → "5"     (was the CHART timeframe — the primary leak)
//     L1  → "15"
//     L2  → "60"
//
// Because every value below is produced inside request.security on a FIXED tf, the
// chart viewport can no longer change any structural interpretation. There is no
// hierarchy and no primary wave: five independent structures, each on its own tf.
// f_se() performs NO drawing (illegal inside request.security); only numeric/bool
// state is returned and drawn later in the chart context at TF-independent prices.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

f_se(simple int _pvLen, simple int _stLen, simple int _atrL, simple float _effT,
     simple float _dispT, simple float _convM, simple float _impM, simple float _chBuf,
     simple int _effL) =>
    // ── PHYSICS (this tf only) ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    float _atr  = ta.atr(_atrL)
    float _vel  = ta.ema(close - close[1], 3)
    float _acc  = _vel - _vel[1]
    float _conv = _acc - _acc[1]
    float _csm  = ta.ema(_conv, 3)
    float _mv   = math.abs(close - close[_effL])
    float _ps   = math.sum(math.abs(close - close[1]), _effL)
    float _eff  = _ps > 0 ? _mv / _ps : 0.0
    float _disp = (high - low) / math.max(_atr, 1e-10)
    bool  _bullImp = _eff > _effT and _vel > _vel[1] and _acc > 0 and close > open and _disp > _dispT
    bool  _bearImp = _eff > _effT and _vel < _vel[1] and _acc < 0 and close < open and _disp > _dispT
    bool  _bullDec = math.abs(_acc) < math.abs(_acc[1]) * 0.8 and _vel > 0
    bool  _bearDec = math.abs(_acc) < math.abs(_acc[1]) * 0.8 and _vel < 0

    // ── SWINGS (this tf only) ───────────────────────────────────────────────
    float _pH = ta.pivothigh(high, _pvLen, _pvLen)
    float _pL = ta.pivotlow (low,  _pvLen, _pvLen)
    var float _curSH = na
    var float _curSL = na
    var float _prSH  = na
    var float _prSL  = na
    if not na(_pH)
        _prSH := na(_curSH) ? _pH : _curSH
        _curSH := _pH
    if not na(_pL)
        _prSL := na(_curSL) ? _pL : _curSL
        _curSL := _pL

    // ── PIVOT MEMORY (for impulse + order-block origin) ─────────────────────
    var float _lastP = na
    var int   _lastD = 0
    var float _prevP = na
    var int   _prevD = 0
    float _eP = na
    int   _eD = 0
    if not na(_pH)
        _eP := _pH
        _eD := 1
    else if not na(_pL)
        _eP := _pL
        _eD := -1
    if _eD != 0
        _prevP := _lastP
        _prevD := _lastD
        _lastP := _eP
        _lastD := _eD

    // ── BOS / CHoCH (this tf only) ──────────────────────────────────────────
    bool _bullBOS = not na(_prSH) and close > _prSH
    bool _bearBOS = not na(_prSL) and close < _prSL
    bool _bullCH  = not na(_prSH) and close > _prSH + _atr * _chBuf
    bool _bearCH  = not na(_prSL) and close < _prSL - _atr * _chBuf

    // ── IMPULSE ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    bool _eLong  = not na(_pH) and _prevD == -1 and (_pH - _prevP) > _atr * _impM
    bool _eShort = not na(_pL) and _prevD == 1  and (_prevP - _pL) > _atr * _impM

    // ── DIRECTION / POINT4 / INVALIDATION / TARGET (state machine) ──────────
    var int   _dir   = 0
    var float _ft    = na
    var float _fb    = na
    var float _p4h   = na
    var float _p4l   = na
    var float _inv   = na
    var float _tgt   = na
    var float _cycH  = na
    var float _cycL  = na
    bool _hasCtx = _dir != 0 and not na(_ft)
    bool _flipDn = _dir == 1  and _bearCH
    bool _flipUp = _dir == -1 and _bullCH
    bool _isRev  = (_eLong and _dir == -1) or (_eShort and _dir == 1) or _flipUp or _flipDn
    bool _spawn  = (_eLong or _eShort or _flipUp or _flipDn) and (not _hasCtx or _isRev)
    if _spawn
        int   _nd   = _eLong ? 1 : _eShort ? -1 : _flipUp ? 1 : -1
        float _obT  = _nd == 1 ? _lastP : _prevP
        float _obB  = _nd == 1 ? _prevP : _lastP
        _dir := _nd
        _ft  := _obT
        _fb  := _obB
        _p4h := _obT
        _p4l := _obB
        _cycH := high
        _cycL := low
        _inv := _nd == 1 ? _obB : _obT
        float _rng = not na(_prSH) and not na(_prSL) ? math.abs(_prSH - _prSL) : _atr * 5.0
        _tgt := _nd == 1 ? nz(_obT, close) + _rng : nz(_obB, close) - _rng
    if _dir == 1
        _cycH := na(_cycH) ? high : math.max(_cycH, high)
    if _dir == -1
        _cycL := na(_cycL) ? low : math.min(_cycL, low)

    int _bosOut = _bullBOS ? 1 : _bearBOS ? -1 : 0
    int _chOut  = _bullCH  ? 1 : _bearCH  ? -1 : 0

    // ── LIFECYCLE (canonical, self-contained, this tf only) ─────────────────
    var bool  _bos1 = false
    var bool  _bos2 = false
    var float _protSw  = na
    var float _protSw2 = na
    var float _indOrig = na
    var float _indExt  = na
    var bool  _indBrk  = false
    var int   _lastDirSeen = 0
    bool _reset = _dir != _lastDirSeen
    _lastDirSeen := _dir
    if _reset
        _bos1   := false
        _bos2   := false
        _protSw := na
        _protSw2:= na
        _indOrig:= na
        _indExt := na
        _indBrk := false
    if _dir == 1 and not na(_pL)
        _protSw2 := _protSw
        _protSw  := _pL
    if _dir == -1 and not na(_pH)
        _protSw2 := _protSw
        _protSw  := _pH
    bool _oppBOS = (_dir == 1 and not na(_protSw) and close < _protSw) or (_dir == -1 and not na(_protSw) and close > _protSw)
    if not _bos1 and _oppBOS
        _bos1   := true
        _indOrig := _dir == 1 ? nz(_cycH, high) : nz(_cycL, low)
    if _bos1 and not _bos2 and _oppBOS and not na(_protSw2) and (_dir == 1 ? close < _protSw2 : close > _protSw2)
        _bos2 := true
    if _bos1 and _dir == 1
        _indExt := na(_indExt) ? close : math.min(_indExt, close)
    if _bos1 and _dir == -1
        _indExt := na(_indExt) ? close : math.max(_indExt, close)
    if _bos2 and not na(_indOrig)
        if _dir == 1 and close > _indOrig
            _indBrk := true
        if _dir == -1 and close < _indOrig
            _indBrk := true

    float _convScore = math.min(math.abs(_csm) / math.max(_atr * _convM, 1e-10) * 50.0, 100.0)
    float _expScore  = math.min(_eff / math.max(_effT, 1e-10) * 50.0 + _disp / math.max(_dispT, 1e-10) * 50.0, 100.0)
    float _absScore  = (_eff < _effT * 0.7 and math.abs(_vel) < math.abs(_vel[1]) * 0.6) ? 60.0 + _convScore * 0.4 : _convScore * 0.3
    bool  _momExpStrong = _eff > _effT * 0.75 and (_dir == 1 ? _vel > 0 : _vel < 0)
    bool  _momDecaying  = _dir == 1 ? _bullDec : _bearDec
    bool  _momCounter   = _dir == 1 ? _bearImp : _bullImp
    bool  _momExhaust   = _eff < _effT * 0.65 and _absScore > 40.0
    // PHYSICS behaviour (bar-level orderflow observed inside this tf's engine) — these
    // are the physics dimension that must CONFIRM each structural event before the
    // lifecycle phase may advance (no structure-only shortcuts remain).
    bool  _physConvexDevel = _convScore > 35.0                        // convexity developing
    bool  _physTransfer    = _convScore > 48.0 or _absScore > 40.0    // participation/energy transfer
    bool  _physCapacityLow = _absScore > 45.0 or _eff < _effT * 0.6   // geometric capacity collapsing

    // Monotonic lifecycle STATE MACHINE — advances and HOLDS within a wave, and
    // resets only on a new wave spawn (direction flip). This is the fix for the
    // phase collapsing back to "Point 4 Origin" on quiet bars: once the wave has
    // expanded / broken structure, the phase progresses forward and stays there.
    var int _phaseState = 0
    if _reset
        _phaseState := 0
    if _dir != 0
        bool _expanding = _momExpStrong or _eLong or _eShort or (_dir == 1 ? _bullImp : _bearImp)
        if _phaseState < 1 and _expanding and not _physTransfer and not _physCapacityLow
            _phaseState := 1                          // Expansion (structure ∧ momentum ∧ physics: integrity preserved, no transfer, capacity available)
        if _phaseState < 2 and _bos1 and _momDecaying and _physConvexDevel
            _phaseState := 2                          // Expansion Pre-Convexity
        if _phaseState < 3 and _bos1 and _momCounter and _physTransfer
            _phaseState := 3                          // Expansion Induction
        if _phaseState < 4 and _bos2 and (_momDecaying or _momCounter) and _physTransfer
            _phaseState := 4                          // Expansion Liquidity
        if _phaseState < 5 and _indBrk and _momExpStrong and not _physCapacityLow
            _phaseState := 5                          // New High/Low (origin reclaimed ∧ accel restored ∧ capacity/energy available)
        if _phaseState >= 5 and _momExhaust and _physCapacityLow
            _phaseState := 7                          // Absorption
        if _phaseState >= 5 and _momCounter and not _momExhaust and _physTransfer
            _phaseState := 8                          // Retracement (turning)
    // EXPORTED phase = LIVE behavioural read so the label tracks the CURRENT
    // lifecycle (expansion / absorption / retracement) every bar, instead of
    // latching on "Point 4 Origin" / "Expansion". The monotonic _phaseState
    // (untouched) still drives the wave-progress %.
    // MEGATRON 8C/8D (v18) — SPATIAL INDUCTION: counter-momentum that occurs
    // BEFORE an objective (_phaseState < 5) is the inducement at the target
    // flip zone, so it now exports Expansion Induction (3) at the first
    // counter-BOS (_bos1) and Expansion Liquidity (4) once price breaks deeper
    // (_bos2) — instead of mislabelling a pre-objective reversal as Retracement
    // (8/9/10). Post-objective counter-momentum still maps to the Retracement
    // family. This is why "Induction" almost never appeared before.
    int _phase = _phaseState
    if _dir != 0
        _phase := _momExhaust and _physCapacityLow ? 7 :
                  _momCounter and _physTransfer    ? (_phaseState >= 5 ? (_convScore > 40.0 ? 10 : _momDecaying ? 9 : 8) : (_bos2 ? 4 : 3)) :
                  _momExpStrong ? (_phaseState >= 5 ? _phaseState : (_bos2 and _physTransfer) ? 4 : (_bos1 and _physConvexDevel) ? 2 : 1) :
                  _momDecaying  ? (_phaseState >= 5 ? _phaseState : 4) :
                  _phaseState == 0 ? 1 :
                  _phaseState
    if _phase == 5 and _dir == -1
        _phase := 6                                   // New Low (bear wave)

    float _wp = _phaseState == 0 ? 10.0 : _phaseState == 1 ? 25.0 : _phaseState == 2 ? 40.0 : _phaseState == 3 ? 55.0 : _phaseState == 4 ? 68.0 : _phaseState == 5 ? 80.0 : _phaseState == 7 ? 92.0 : 85.0
    float _cm = math.min(_convScore, 100.0)
    float _mf = math.min(math.max(_expScore, math.max(_absScore, _convScore)) * 0.70 + (_dir != 0 ? 30.0 : 0.0), 100.0)

    // ── FRZ candidate (origin order-block of this tf's structure) ───────────
    float _frzS = math.min((_eLong or _eShort ? 50.0 : 0.0) + _expScore * 0.30 + _convScore * 0.20, 100.0)

    // Reported wave direction = which side of its ORIGIN price sits on. The engine
    // above already detects each wave and stores its origin in _inv (bull wave =
    // launch low, bear wave = launch high). Per spec: price above origin -> Bullish,
    // below -> Bearish. _dir stays internal (drives spawn/lifecycle unchanged); only
    // the EXPORTED direction reflects price vs origin so the label can't stay stale.
    int _dirLabel = not na(_inv) ? (close > _inv ? 1 : close < _inv ? -1 : _dir) : _dir

    [_dirLabel, _phase, _curSH, _curSL, _prSH, _prSL, _bosOut, _chOut, _p4h, _p4l, _inv, _tgt, _ft, _fb, _frzS, _wp, _cm, _mf]

// ── Phase-code → canonical lifecycle string (shared by all layers) ───────────
f_phaseStr(int _c) =>
     _c == 1  ? "Expansion"                 :
     _c == 2  ? "Expansion Pre-Convexity"   :
     _c == 3  ? "Expansion Induction"       :
     _c == 4  ? "Expansion Liquidity"       :
     _c == 5  ? "New High"                  :
     _c == 6  ? "New Low"                   :
     _c == 7  ? "Absorption"                :
     _c == 8  ? "Retracement"               :
     _c == 9  ? "Retracement Pre-Convexity" :
     _c == 10 ? "Retracement Induction"     :
     _c == 11 ? "Retracement Liquidity"     :
     _c == 12 ? "Demand Return"             :
     _c == 13 ? "Supply Return"             : "Point 4 Origin"

// ── canonical phase → hypothesis-family string (L0 dominantPhase vocabulary) ─
f_hypFam(string _ph) =>
     _ph == "Expansion"                 ? "EXPANSION"           :
     _ph == "Expansion Pre-Convexity"   ? "CONVEXITY FORMING"   :
     _ph == "Expansion Induction"       ? "CONVEXITY FORMING"   :
     _ph == "Expansion Liquidity"       ? "CONVEXITY FORMING"   :
     _ph == "New High"                  ? "CREATION FORMING"    :
     _ph == "New Low"                   ? "CREATION FORMING"    :
     _ph == "Absorption"                ? "ABSORPTION"          :
     _ph == "Demand Return"             ? "DEMAND/SUPPLY RETURN":
     _ph == "Supply Return"             ? "DEMAND/SUPPLY RETURN": "RETRACEMENT"

// ── lifecycle family int → simple L1/L2 vocabulary (parent-child engine) ─────
f_famSimple(int _f) =>
     _f == 1 ? "Expansion"     :
     _f == 2 ? "Pre-Convexity" :
     _f == 4 ? "Absorption"    :
     _f == 5 ? "Liquidity"     :
     _f == 6 ? "Absorption"    : "Expansion"

// ── lifecycle family int → L3 micro vocabulary (fusion / dominance engines) ──
f_famMicro(int _f) =>
     _f == 2 ? "M1 Convexity"  :
     _f == 4 ? "M1 Absorption" :
     _f == 5 ? "M1 Liquidity"  : "M1 Expansion"

// ── next-phase prediction from canonical phase code ──────────────────────────
f_nextPhase(int _c) =>
     _c == 1 ? "Expansion Pre-Convexity" :
     _c == 2 ? "Expansion Induction"     :
     _c == 3 ? "Expansion Liquidity"     :
     _c == 4 ? "New High / New Low"      :
     _c == 5 or _c == 6 ? "Absorption"   :
     _c == 7 ? "Retracement"             :
     _c == 8 ? "Retracement Pre-Convexity" : "Expansion"

// ── phase code → lifecycle family int (matches f_phaseFamily numbering) ──────
f_phaseFamilyCode(int _c) =>
     _c == 1 ? 1 :
     (_c == 2 or _c == 3 or _c == 4) ? 2 :
     (_c == 5 or _c == 6) ? 3 :
     _c == 7 ? 4 :
     (_c == 8 or _c == 9 or _c == 10 or _c == 11) ? 5 :
     (_c == 12 or _c == 13) ? 6 : 0

// These are the ONLY source of structure for M1 / L3 / L0 / L1 / L2 from here on.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
[se1_dir, se1_ph, se1_sh, se1_sl, se1_psh, se1_psl, se1_bos, se1_ch, se1_p4h, se1_p4l, se1_inv, se1_tgt, se1_ft, se1_fb, se1_fs, se1_wp, se1_cm, se1_mf] =
     request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("1"),  f_se(pivotLen, structLen, atrLen, effThresh, dispThresh, convMult, impulseAtrMult, chochBufferATR, effLen), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)
[se3_dir, se3_ph, se3_sh, se3_sl, se3_psh, se3_psl, se3_bos, se3_ch, se3_p4h, se3_p4l, se3_inv, se3_tgt, se3_ft, se3_fb, se3_fs, se3_wp, se3_cm, se3_mf] =
     request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("3"),  f_se(pivotLen, structLen, atrLen, effThresh, dispThresh, convMult, impulseAtrMult, chochBufferATR, effLen), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)
[se5_dir, se5_ph, se5_sh, se5_sl, se5_psh, se5_psl, se5_bos, se5_ch, se5_p4h, se5_p4l, se5_inv, se5_tgt, se5_ft, se5_fb, se5_fs, se5_wp, se5_cm, se5_mf] =

[se15_dir, se15_ph, se15_sh, se15_sl, se15_psh, se15_psl, se15_bos, se15_ch, se15_p4h, se15_p4l, se15_inv, se15_tgt, se15_ft, se15_fb, se15_fs, se15_wp, se15_cm, se15_mf] =
     request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("15"), f_se(pivotLen, structLen, atrLen, effThresh, dispThresh, convMult, impulseAtrMult, chochBufferATR, effLen), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)
[se60_dir, se60_ph, se60_sh, se60_sl, se60_psh, se60_psl, se60_bos, se60_ch, se60_p4h, se60_p4l, se60_inv, se60_tgt, se60_ft, se60_fb, se60_fs, se60_wp, se60_cm, se60_mf] =
     request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("60"), f_se(pivotLen, structLen, atrLen, effThresh, dispThresh, convMult, impulseAtrMult, chochBufferATR, effLen), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)
[se240_dir, se240_ph, se240_sh, se240_sl, se240_psh, se240_psl, se240_bos, se240_ch, se240_p4h, se240_p4l, se240_inv, se240_tgt, se240_ft, se240_fb, se240_fs, se240_wp, se240_cm, se240_mf] =
     request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("240"), f_se(pivotLen, structLen, atrLen, effThresh, dispThresh, convMult, impulseAtrMult, chochBufferATR, effLen), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)

// ── Canonical phase strings per fixed layer ──────────────────────────────────
string m1_phaseCanon = f_phaseStr(int(nz(se1_ph)))
string l3_phaseCanon = f_phaseStr(int(nz(se3_ph)))
string l0_phaseCanon = f_phaseStr(int(nz(se5_ph)))
string l1_phaseCanon = f_phaseStr(int(nz(se15_ph)))
string l2_phaseCanon = f_phaseStr(int(nz(se60_ph)))
string l4_phaseCanon = f_phaseStr(int(nz(se240_ph)))   // L4 = H4 context

// ── Per-layer structural objects (Direction / Swings / BOS / CHoCH / Point4 /
//    Invalidation / Targets / FRZ) — ALL fixed-tf, none chart-dependent ───────
// ── Canonical wave DIRECTION per fixed timeframe ─────────────────────────────
// A wave's direction is defined by where LIVE price sits relative to that wave's
// ORIGIN: price above the origin -> Bullish wave; once the origin is breached,
// price is now building a Bearish wave (and symmetrically for a bear wave whose
// origin is its launch high). The fixed-tf engine already detects each wave and
// exports both its origin (se*_inv) and an origin-based direction (se*_dir) that
// it computes from that timeframe's OWN close inside request.security. On higher
// timeframes that close lags (it only updates when the HTF bar closes), which
// left the labels stale after an intrabar origin breach. We therefore re-evaluate
// direction here in CHART context against the live `close`, so every timeframe's
// label tracks the CURRENT price vs its origin in real time. These six variables
// are the single source of wave direction for every dashboard panel, on-chart
// label, narrative and downstream score, so fixing them here fixes them all.
f_waveDirByOrigin(float _origin, int _fallbackDir) =>
    not na(_origin) ? (close > _origin ? 1 : close < _origin ? -1 : _fallbackDir) : _fallbackDir

int   m1_dir = f_waveDirByOrigin(se1_inv,   int(nz(se1_dir)))
int   l3_dir = f_waveDirByOrigin(se3_inv,   int(nz(se3_dir)))
int   l0_dir = f_waveDirByOrigin(se5_inv,   int(nz(se5_dir)))
int   l1_dir = f_waveDirByOrigin(se15_inv,  int(nz(se15_dir)))
int   l2_dir = f_waveDirByOrigin(se60_inv,  int(nz(se60_dir)))
int   l4_dir = f_waveDirByOrigin(se240_inv, int(nz(se240_dir)))
int   m1_bos = int(nz(se1_bos))
int   l3_bos = int(nz(se3_bos))
int   l0_bos = int(nz(se5_bos))
int   l1_bos = int(nz(se15_bos))
int   l2_bos = int(nz(se60_bos))

int   l0_choch = int(nz(se5_ch))

int   l2_choch = int(nz(se60_ch))

float l2_frzScore = nz(se60_fs)

string m1_dirLabel = m1_dir == 1 ? "Bullish Wave" : m1_dir == -1 ? "Bearish Wave" : "Neutral"
string l3_dirLabel = l3_dir == 1 ? "Bullish Wave" : l3_dir == -1 ? "Bearish Wave" : "Neutral"
string l0_dirLabel = l0_dir == 1 ? "Bullish Wave" : l0_dir == -1 ? "Bearish Wave" : "Neutral"
string l1_dirLabel = l1_dir == 1 ? "Bullish Wave" : l1_dir == -1 ? "Bearish Wave" : "Neutral"
string l2_dirLabel = l2_dir == 1 ? "Bullish Wave" : l2_dir == -1 ? "Bearish Wave" : "Neutral"
string l4_dirLabel = l4_dir == 1 ? "Bullish Wave" : l4_dir == -1 ? "Bearish Wave" : "Neutral"

// ── M1 & H4 display aliases (parity with L0/L1/L2/L3 targetWave/currentPhase) ─
// M1 and H4 do not flow through the L1/L2/L3 belief classifier, so expose the
// same trio (targetWave / currentPhase / dominance) directly from their own
// fixed-tf engine outputs.

// ── FRACTAL STACK ALIGNMENT (v90) ────────────────────────────────────────────
// How unified the five FIXED structure layers are. Feeds the scores
// (buyScore/sellScore), the V72 consensus, and trade-quality grade so the
// contextual waves actually weight the decision — not just draw on the chart.
// Higher layers (L2 H1, L1 M15) carry more contextual weight than M3/M1.
int _stackBull = (m1_dir == 1 ? 1 : 0) + (l3_dir == 1 ? 1 : 0) + (l0_dir == 1 ? 1 : 0) + (l1_dir == 1 ? 1 : 0) + (l2_dir == 1 ? 1 : 0) + (l4_dir == 1 ? 1 : 0)
int _stackBear = (m1_dir == -1 ? 1 : 0) + (l3_dir == -1 ? 1 : 0) + (l0_dir == -1 ? 1 : 0) + (l1_dir == -1 ? 1 : 0) + (l2_dir == -1 ? 1 : 0) + (l4_dir == -1 ? 1 : 0)
int   fractalStackDir   = _stackBull > _stackBear ? 1 : _stackBear > _stackBull ? -1 : 0
float fractalStackScore = math.max(_stackBull, _stackBear) / 6.0 * 100.0

// ── Live directional references for DISPLAY engines (Bayesian / Direction Prob) ─
// These mirror the repaired live wave plumbing so display panels respond the
// instant the wave state changes. They intentionally do NOT touch the gated
// Engine-1A `direction` (execution state) or `htfAlign` (belief) used for trade
// firing — only the read-only probability/quality readouts consume them.
//   liveWaveDir   = M5 (L0) live origin-based wave direction (execution context)
//   liveHtfAlign  = live HTF consensus: +1/-1 only when H1 (l2) and H4 (l4) agree
int liveWaveDir  = l0_dir
int liveHtfAlign = (l2_dir != 0 and l2_dir == l4_dir) ? l2_dir : 0
float fractalCtxScore   = math.min(
     (l4_dir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? 30.0 : 0.0) +
     (l2_dir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? 26.0 : 0.0) +
     (l1_dir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (l0_dir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? 14.0 : 0.0) +
     (l3_dir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ?  6.0 : 0.0) +
     (m1_dir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ?  4.0 : 0.0), 100.0)

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 5 — MAX PIVOT MEMORY ENGINE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

float pivH = ta.pivothigh(high, pivotLen, pivotLen)
float pivL = ta.pivotlow (low,  pivotLen, pivotLen)

var float lastPivotPrice = na
var int   lastPivotBar   = na
var int   lastPivotDir   = 0
var float prevPivotPrice = na
var int   prevPivotBar   = na
var int   prevPivotDir   = 0

float pivotEventPrice = na
int   pivotEventBar   = na
int   pivotEventDir   = 0

if not na(pivH)
    pivotEventPrice := pivH
    pivotEventBar   := bar_index - pivotLen
    pivotEventDir   := 1
else if not na(pivL)
    pivotEventPrice := pivL
    pivotEventBar   := bar_index - pivotLen
    pivotEventDir   := -1

if pivotEventDir != 0
    prevPivotPrice := lastPivotPrice
    prevPivotBar   := lastPivotBar
    prevPivotDir   := lastPivotDir
    lastPivotPrice := pivotEventPrice
    lastPivotBar   := pivotEventBar
    lastPivotDir   := pivotEventDir

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 6 — MAX IMPULSE DETECTION
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

bool eliteShortImpulse = not na(pivL) and prevPivotDir == 1  and (prevPivotPrice - pivL) > atr * impulseAtrMult
bool eliteLongImpulse  = not na(pivH) and prevPivotDir == -1 and (pivH - prevPivotPrice) > atr * impulseAtrMult

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 7 — MAX INDUCEMENT / FLIPZONE PRICE FINDER
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

f_findInducPrice(int _anchorRefBar, float _anchorTop, float _anchorBot, int _lookback) =>
    float _best     = na
    float _bestDist = na
    int   _maxI     = math.min(_lookback, bar_index - _anchorRefBar)
    if _maxI >= 1
        for i = 1 to _maxI
            if high[i] < _anchorTop and low[i] > _anchorBot
                float _d = math.abs((bar_index - i) - _anchorRefBar)
                if na(_bestDist) or _d < _bestDist
                    _bestDist := _d
                    _best     := (high[i] + low[i]) / 2.0
    _best

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 8 — WAVE CONTEXT VARIABLES
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

var int   direction     = 0

var int   obBirthBar    = na

var float point4OriginLow  = na

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// PER-TIMEFRAME DISPLAY WAVE DIRECTION (v91 — no shared global)
// There is deliberately NO single global wave-direction master anymore. Each timeframe
// exposes its OWN origin-based wave direction (computed by f_waveDirByOrigin from
// live price vs that timeframe's origin), where:
//     +1 = price ABOVE that timeframe's wave origin -> Bullish Wave
//     -1 = price BELOW that timeframe's wave origin -> Bearish Wave
//      (price == origin -> previous direction preserved inside f_waveDirByOrigin)
// Every panel, label, narrative and downstream engine consumes the variable for
// ITS OWN timeframe. The execution/command engine is by design an M5 (L0) engine,
// so it explicitly references displayWaveDir_M5 (= l0_dir) — an EXPLICIT timeframe
// variable, never a hidden global that another timeframe could inherit.
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
int displayWaveDir_M1  = m1_dir   // M1  — fixed "1"   structure
int displayWaveDir_M3  = l3_dir   // M3  — fixed "3"   structure
int displayWaveDir_M5  = l0_dir   // M5  — fixed "5"   structure (execution TF)
int displayWaveDir_M15 = l1_dir   // M15 — fixed "15"  structure
int displayWaveDir_H1  = l2_dir   // H1  — fixed "60"  structure
int displayWaveDir_H4  = l4_dir   // H4  — fixed "240" structure


float _g_highestAB = ta.highest(high, acceptBars)
float _g_lowestAB  = ta.lowest (low,  acceptBars)

var array<float> cycleObTop        = array.new_float(4, na)
var array<float> cycleObBot        = array.new_float(4, na)
var array<float> cycleFlipTop      = array.new_float(4, na)
var array<float> cycleFlipBot      = array.new_float(4, na)
var array<float> cycleP4High       = array.new_float(4, na)
var array<float> cycleP4Low        = array.new_float(4, na)
var array<int>   cycleStartBar     = array.new_int  (4, na)
var array<int>   cycleDir          = array.new_int  (4, 0)
var array<box>   cycleHistoryBoxes = array.new<box> (4, na)

f_storeCycleState(int _cycle, float _obT, float _obB, float _fT, float _fB,
                  float _p4H, float _p4L, int _startBar, int _dir) =>
    int _idx = math.min(_cycle - 1, 3)
    array.set(cycleObTop,    _idx, _obT)
    array.set(cycleObBot,    _idx, _obB)
    array.set(cycleFlipTop,  _idx, _fT)
    array.set(cycleFlipBot,  _idx, _fB)
    array.set(cycleP4High,   _idx, _p4H)
    array.set(cycleP4Low,    _idx, _p4L)
    array.set(cycleStartBar, _idx, _startBar)
    array.set(cycleDir,      _idx, _dir)
    box _oldBox = array.get(cycleHistoryBoxes, _idx)
    if not na(_oldBox)
        box.delete(_oldBox)
    if showCycleHistory and not na(_p4H) and not na(_p4L)
        color _histCol    = _dir == 1 ? color.new(color.teal, 93) : color.new(color.red, 93)
        color _histBorder = _dir == 1 ? color.new(color.teal, 60) : color.new(color.red, 60)
        box _hb = box.new(left=_startBar, top=_p4H, right=bar_index + 200,
             bottom=_p4L, bgcolor=f_zoneFill(_histCol), border_color=_histBorder,
             border_style=line.style_dashed, border_width=1)
        array.set(cycleHistoryBoxes, _idx, _hb)

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// FORWARD DECLARATIONS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

var bool inductionEvidence  = false
var bool preConvEvidence    = false
var bool closeInside        = false
var bool m1AbsorptionEmer   = false
var bool m1ConvexityEmer    = false
var bool m1LiquidityEmer    = false

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 9 — PHYSICS OBSERVATION LAYER
// (Moved before Engine 1A — Engine 1A momentum/physics dimensions require
//  obs_* scores, convexityScore, and physicsConsensus at evaluation time.)
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

float velocityScore     = math.min(math.abs(velocity)     / math.max(atr * 0.1, 1e-10) * 50.0, 100.0)
float accelerationScore = math.min(math.abs(acceleration) / math.max(atr * 0.05,1e-10) * 50.0, 100.0)
float convexityScore    = math.min(math.abs(convSmooth)   / math.max(atr * convMult, 1e-10) * 25.0, 100.0)
float expansionScore    = math.min(displacement / math.max(dispThresh, 1e-10) * 50.0, 100.0)

float obs_ExpansionScore  = math.min(
     (efficiency > effThresh ? efficiency * 60.0 : efficiency * 30.0) +
     (displacement > dispThresh ? (displacement / math.max(dispThresh, 1e-10) - 1.0) * 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (velocity > 0 and acceleration > 0 ? velocityScore * 0.2 : velocity < 0 and acceleration < 0 ? velocityScore * 0.2 : 0.0),
     100.0)

float obs_DecayScore      = math.min(
     (bullMomDecay or bearMomDecay ? 40.0 : 0.0) +
     (convexityScore > 30 ? convexityScore * 0.5 : 0.0) +
     (phys_vd70 ? 30.0 : 0.0),
     100.0)

float obs_CurvatureScore  = convexityScore

float obs_AbsorptionScore = math.min(
     (efficiency < effThresh * 0.7 ? (1.0 - efficiency / math.max(effThresh, 1e-10)) * 50.0 : 0.0) +
     (phys_vd50 ? 30.0 : 0.0) +
     (displacement < dispThresh * 0.5 ? 20.0 : 0.0),
     100.0)

float obs_LiquidityScore  = math.min(
     obs_DecayScore * 0.4 +
     obs_CurvatureScore * 0.4 +
     (displacement > dispThresh * 1.2 and (bullMomDecay or bearMomDecay) ? 20.0 : 0.0),
     100.0)

float physicsMax  = math.max(obs_ExpansionScore, obs_DecayScore, obs_AbsorptionScore, obs_LiquidityScore)
float physicsDiff = physicsMax - math.min(obs_ExpansionScore, obs_DecayScore, obs_AbsorptionScore, obs_LiquidityScore)
float physicsConsensus = math.max(0.0, 100.0 - physicsDiff)

// ── Forward declarations for liqHeat, nearFlipzone, convexityMaturity ──────────
// These are fully computed in Sections 10–12 below. The var declarations here
// allow Engine 1A (which runs before those sections) to reference them safely.
// On bar 0 they hold their initialised defaults; from bar 1 onward the Section
// 10–12 assignments run first on the PREVIOUS bar, so the values are valid.
var float liqHeat         = 0.0
var bool  nearFlipzone    = false
var float convexityMaturity = 0.0

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ENGINE 1A — UNIFIED WAVE LIFECYCLE & PHASE DEFINITION ENGINE
// SOLE LIFECYCLE AUTHORITY — ALL DOWNSTREAM SYSTEMS CONSUME THIS OUTPUT ONLY.
//
// ARCHITECTURE:
//   Phase is determined by THREE DIMENSIONS SIMULTANEOUSLY:
//     DIMENSION 1 — STRUCTURE  : BOS events, swing violations, induction objects
//     DIMENSION 2 — MOMENTUM   : Expansion efficiency, decay, directional impulse
//     DIMENSION 3 — WAVE PHYSICS: Convexity development, geometric capacity,
//                                 liquidity formation, expansion integrity
//
//   A lifecycle phase becomes active ONLY when all three dimensions describe
//   the same market condition.  Structure alone, Momentum alone, Physics alone,
//   or any two-dimension combination is INVALID for phase assignment.
//
// CANONICAL LIFECYCLE (sole permitted vocabulary):
//   Point 4 Origin → Expansion → Expansion Pre-Convexity → Expansion Induction
//   → Expansion Liquidity → New High / New Low → Absorption → Retracement
//   → Retracement Pre-Convexity → Retracement Induction → Retracement Liquidity
//   → Demand Return / Supply Return
//
// OUTPUTS:
//   ie1a_waveDirection  : "Bullish Wave" | "Bearish Wave"
//   ie1a_currentPhase   : one of the 14 canonical lifecycle phases above
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ── ENGINE 1A OUTPUTS (v90): lifecycle is sourced from the M5 fixed engine.
// The legacy 3-dimension structural/momentum/physics apparatus was removed;
// its only remaining consumer (ie1a_phaseConfidence) is now an M5 model-fit proxy.
// (ie1a_waveDirection removed — unused; displayWaveDir_M5 / l0_dirLabel are the
//  origin-based M5 wave-direction source consumed by every panel and label.)
string ie1a_currentPhase   = l0_phaseCanon
float  ie1a_phaseConfidence = math.max(20.0, math.min(100.0, fractalCtxScore * 0.50 + nz(se5_mf) * 0.30 + nz(se5_wp) * 0.20))

// ── 1A-MAP: CANONICAL PHASE → HYPOTHESIS FAMILY MAP ─────────────────────────
// Maps IE1A phase back to the internal hypothesis vocabulary used by downstream
// belief engines (which remain as confidence providers, not phase assigners).
string ie1a_hypFamily =
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion"                  ? "EXPANSION"          :
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Pre-Convexity"    ? "CONVEXITY FORMING"  :
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Induction"        ? "CONVEXITY FORMING"  :
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Liquidity"        ? "CONVEXITY FORMING"  :
     ie1a_currentPhase == "New High"                   ? "CREATION FORMING"   :
     ie1a_currentPhase == "New Low"                    ? "CREATION FORMING"   :
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Absorption"                 ? "ABSORPTION"         :
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement"                ? "RETRACEMENT"        :
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Pre-Convexity"  ? "RETRACEMENT"        :
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Induction"      ? "RETRACEMENT"        :
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Liquidity"      ? "RETRACEMENT"        :
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return"              ? "DEMAND/SUPPLY RETURN" :
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return"              ? "DEMAND/SUPPLY RETURN" : "EXPANSION"

// Expansion-side flag (used by classifier for Retr Pre-Convexity/Induction/Liquidity mapping)
bool ie1a_isExpSide =
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion"               or
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Pre-Convexity" or
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Induction"     or
     ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Liquidity"     or
     ie1a_currentPhase == "New High"                or
     ie1a_currentPhase == "New Low"

// END ENGINE 1A
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ENERGY RESOLUTION FRAMEWORK (ERF)
// Combines: Energy Dissipation Engine (EDE) + Resolution Engine (RE) + Energy Attractor Engine (EAE)
// Architecture:  Price → EDE → RE → EAE → Intelligence Engine
//
// FUNDAMENTAL MARKET AXIOM
//   Market = Energy Generation System
//   Expansion       = Energy Creation
//   Pre-Convexity   = Initial Dissipation
//   Induction       = Secondary Dissipation
//   Liquidation     = Delivery Dissipation
//   Supply/Demand   = Potential Resolution Node
//   Zone Revisit    = Incomplete Resolution
//   Rotation        = Competing Energy System
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// EDE — ENERGY DISSIPATION ENGINE
// Answers: How is energy cleaning itself?
// Tracks:  Expansion Energy | Dissipation Progress | Cleaning State | Delivery State
// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// State 1-6 derived directly from IE1A canonical phase
// State 1: Energy Accumulation       → "Point 4 Origin" / "Expansion"
// State 2: Energy Release 1 (Pre-Conv)→ "Expansion Pre-Convexity"
// State 3: Energy Release 2 (Induction)→ "Expansion Induction"
// State 4: Energy Purge (Liquidation)→ "Expansion Liquidity"
// State 5: Objective Delivery        → "New High" / "New Low"
// State 6: Resolution Assessment     → "Absorption" onward

int ede_state =
     l0_phaseCanon == "Point 4 Origin"            ? 1 :
     l0_phaseCanon == "Expansion"                 ? 1 :
     l0_phaseCanon == "Expansion Pre-Convexity"   ? 2 :
     l0_phaseCanon == "Expansion Induction"       ? 3 :
     l0_phaseCanon == "Expansion Liquidity"       ? 4 :
     l0_phaseCanon == "New High"                  ? 5 :
     l0_phaseCanon == "New Low"                   ? 5 : 6

string ede_cleaningState =
     ede_state == 1 ? "Accumulating" :
     ede_state == 2 ? "Cleaning — Initial Release"  :
     ede_state == 3 ? "Cleaning — Secondary Release" :
     ede_state == 4 ? "Cleaning — Purge"            :
     ede_state == 5 ? "Delivering"                  : "Resolving"

// Expansion energy: proxy from physics score during expansion phase
float ede_expansionEnergy = math.min(
     obs_ExpansionScore * 0.50 +
     (bullImpulse or bearImpulse ? 30.0 : 0.0) +
     (efficiency * 20.0), 100.0)

// Dissipated energy: accumulates through pre-conv → induction → liquidation
float ede_dissipatedEnergy = math.min(
     (ede_state >= 2 ? obs_DecayScore * 0.40 : 0.0) +
     (ede_state >= 3 ? obs_CurvatureScore * 0.30 : 0.0) +
     (ede_state >= 4 ? obs_LiquidityScore * 0.30 : 0.0), 100.0)

// Dissipation progress 0-100
float ede_dissipationProgress = math.min(
     (ede_state >= 2 ? 25.0 : 0.0) +
     (ede_state >= 3 ? 25.0 : 0.0) +
     (ede_state >= 4 ? 25.0 : 0.0) +
     (ede_state >= 5 ? 25.0 : 0.0), 100.0)

// Delivery state: is the liquidation leg itself expanding (becoming a delivery wave)?
bool ede_liquidationBecomingDirectional =
     ede_state == 4 and (bullImpulse or bearImpulse) and efficiency > effThresh * 0.8

// Delivery space score: how much room remains before the objective?
// Uses convexityMaturity as inverse proxy — higher maturity = less space remaining
float ede_deliverySpaceScore = math.min(
     math.max(0.0, 100.0 - convexityMaturity) * 1.0, 100.0)

// Messy price action recognition — a core principle of EDE
// Messy ≠ Randomness; Messy = Energy Dissipation
bool ede_messyPriceIsDissipation =
     (ede_state >= 2 and ede_state <= 4) and
     obs_DecayScore > 30.0 and
     efficiency < effThresh * 0.9 and
     not (bullImpulse or bearImpulse)

// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// RE — RESOLUTION ENGINE
// Answers: Did the process actually finish?
// Tracks:  Resolution State | Recursive Completion | Residual Energy
// Key axiom: Objective Hit ≠ Process Complete
// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// Resolution states: RESOLVED | PARTIALLY_RESOLVED | UNRESOLVED
// Logic: reaching New High/Low (state 5) is objective delivery, but resolution
// requires the full absorption + retracement + demand return cycle.

// Expected recursive cycles based on wave generation depth
int re_expectedCycles = math.max(1, math.min(waveDepth + 2, 4))

// Completed cycles = entryCycle (each recursive wave = one completed dissipation cycle)
int re_completedCycles = math.max(0, math.min(entryCycle, re_expectedCycles))

// Recursive completion score 0-100
float re_recursiveCompletionScore =
     re_expectedCycles > 0 ?
     math.min(float(re_completedCycles) / float(re_expectedCycles) * 100.0, 100.0) : 0.0

// Residual energy = expansion energy minus what has been dissipated
float re_residualEnergy = math.max(0.0,
     ede_expansionEnergy - ede_dissipatedEnergy)

// Resolution state determination
// RESOLVED: delivery + full absorption + retracement + demand return completed
bool re_objectiveReached = ede_state >= 5
bool re_fullDissipation  = ede_dissipationProgress >= 75.0
float re_dissipationProgress = ede_dissipationProgress

bool re_absorbedAndReturned =
     (ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return") and
     recursiveComplete

string re_resolutionState =
     re_absorbedAndReturned and re_fullDissipation and re_recursiveCompletionScore >= 75.0 ?
          "RESOLVED" :
     re_objectiveReached and re_dissipationProgress >= 50.0 ?
          "PARTIALLY RESOLVED" : "UNRESOLVED"

// alias for local use in RE

// Residual energy score 0-100 (higher = more uncleaned energy remaining)
float re_residualEnergyScore = math.min(re_residualEnergy, 100.0)

// Node open/closed determination
bool re_nodeOpen   = re_resolutionState == "UNRESOLVED" or re_resolutionState == "PARTIALLY RESOLVED"
bool re_nodeClosed = re_resolutionState == "RESOLVED"

// Revisit probability (higher when open/unresolved)
float re_revisitProbability =
     re_resolutionState == "UNRESOLVED"         ? math.min(re_residualEnergyScore * 0.90, 95.0) :
     re_resolutionState == "PARTIALLY RESOLVED" ? math.min(re_residualEnergyScore * 0.60, 75.0) :
                                                   math.min(re_residualEnergyScore * 0.20, 25.0)

// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// EAE — ENERGY ATTRACTOR ENGINE
// Answers: Where is unresolved energy pulling price?
// New magnetism principle: Price attracted to unresolved energy (not just liquidity)
// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// Primary attractor: the most significant unresolved energy node
// Logic: if wave is unresolved, the current flipzone IS the primary attractor;
// if partially resolved, the demand/supply zone is the secondary attractor.
// Distance to attractor uses existing geometric calculations.

float eae_primaryAttractorPrice =
     direction == 0 ? na :
     re_resolutionState == "UNRESOLVED" ?
          (direction == 1 ? nz(flipBot, close - atr * 2.0) : nz(flipTop, close + atr * 2.0)) :
     re_resolutionState == "PARTIALLY RESOLVED" ?
          (direction == 1 ? nz(point4OriginLow, close - atr) : nz(point4OriginHigh, close + atr)) :
          na

float eae_secondaryAttractorPrice =
     direction != 0 and re_resolutionState == "UNRESOLVED" and not na(inducZoneLow) and not na(inducZoneHigh) ?
          (direction == 1 ? nz(inducZoneLow, na) : nz(inducZoneHigh, na)) : na

// Attractor scoring — weighted by residual energy, timeframe weight, termination strength
float eae_primaryAttractorScore = math.min(
     re_residualEnergyScore * 0.40 +
     (re_resolutionState == "UNRESOLVED" ? 30.0 :
      re_resolutionState == "PARTIALLY RESOLVED" ? 20.0 : 5.0) +
     (not na(eae_primaryAttractorPrice) ?
          math.max(0.0, 30.0 - math.abs(close - eae_primaryAttractorPrice) / math.max(atr, 1e-10) * 5.0)
          : 0.0),
     100.0)

float eae_secondaryAttractorScore = math.min(
     re_residualEnergyScore * 0.25 +
     (re_resolutionState == "PARTIALLY RESOLVED" ? 20.0 : 10.0) +
     (not na(eae_secondaryAttractorPrice) ?
          math.max(0.0, 20.0 - math.abs(close - eae_secondaryAttractorPrice) / math.max(atr, 1e-10) * 4.0)
          : 0.0),
     100.0)

// Primary attractor label for display
string eae_primaryAttractorLabel =
     re_resolutionState == "UNRESOLVED" ? "Flip Zone (High Residual)" :
     re_resolutionState == "PARTIALLY RESOLVED" ? "Origin Zone (Partial)" : "No Active Attractor"

// Energy state summary (for Intelligence Engine output)
string eae_energyState =
     ede_state == 1 ? "Accumulating" :
     ede_state >= 2 and ede_state <= 4 ? "Cleaning"     :
     ede_state == 5 ? "Delivering"                       :
     re_resolutionState == "RESOLVED"  ? "Exhausted"    : "Resolving"

// ── ERF: ROTATION ENGINE MODIFICATION ────────────────────────────────────────
// Old logic: Messy Structure = Rotation Risk
// New logic: Before rotation scoring, ask: Is active dissipation occurring?
//            If yes → suppress rotation because Cleaning ≠ Rotation

bool erf_activeDissipation = ede_messyPriceIsDissipation
bool erf_suppressRotation  = erf_activeDissipation and ede_state >= 2 and ede_state <= 4

// ERF Confidence: how well do EDE, RE, and EAE agree on market state?
float erf_confidence = math.min(
     (eae_energyState != "Accumulating" ? ie1a_phaseConfidence * 0.40 : 20.0) +
     (re_resolutionState == "RESOLVED"  ? 30.0 :
      re_resolutionState == "PARTIALLY RESOLVED" ? 20.0 : 10.0) +
     (eae_primaryAttractorScore * 0.30),
     100.0)

// ERF Dissipation Confidence (does the observed complexity match cleaning expectations?)
float erf_dissipationConfidence = math.min(
     (ede_messyPriceIsDissipation ? 50.0 : 0.0) +
     (ede_dissipationProgress * 0.50),
     100.0)

// ── V72 ERF INTEGRATION — TRADE READINESS + ENTRY GATE (Phase 1) ─────────────
// Spec Part 7. Elevates ERF from advisory to decision-influencing. All inputs
// are existing RE/EAE/ERF outputs computed above (compute order respected:
// IE1A -> EDE -> RE -> EAE -> ERF -> here). Readiness correction C10: a single
// tunable threshold replaces the paradoxical UNRESOLVED-dual-branch gate.
float erfReadyResW   = input.float(0.25, "ERF: Recursive Completion Weight", group=GRP_ERF, minval=0.0, maxval=1.0, step=0.05)
float erfReadyResidW = input.float(0.20, "ERF: Delivered Energy Weight",     group=GRP_ERF, minval=0.0, maxval=1.0, step=0.05)
float erfReadyConfW  = input.float(0.15, "ERF: Confidence Weight",           group=GRP_ERF, minval=0.0, maxval=1.0, step=0.05)
float erfEntryThreshold = input.float(45.0, "ERF: Entry Gate Threshold",     group=GRP_ERF, minval=0.0, maxval=100.0, step=1.0)
bool  erfGateEnabled    = input.bool(true,  "ERF: Enable Entry Gate on Signals", group=GRP_ERF)

float erf_tradeReadiness = math.min(
     (re_resolutionState == "RESOLVED"           ? 40.0 :
      re_resolutionState == "PARTIALLY RESOLVED" ? 25.0 : 10.0) +
     re_recursiveCompletionScore * erfReadyResW +
     (100.0 - re_residualEnergyScore) * erfReadyResidW +
     erf_confidence * erfReadyConfW,
     100.0)

// Single-threshold gate (C10). erf_tradeReadiness naturally scores low when
// UNRESOLVED and high when RESOLVED, so one threshold is sufficient and safe.
bool erf_entryGate = not erfGateEnabled or erf_tradeReadiness >= erfEntryThreshold

// END ENERGY RESOLUTION FRAMEWORK
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// HIGH-PROBABILITY ENTRY ZONE (Primary Attractor) — clean persistent chart marker
// One tidy band drawn at the primary attractor (the highest-probability
// return/entry level), always visible while a directional wave exists. This
// replaces the old supply/demand boxes and keeps the chart uncluttered.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
showEntryZone   = input.bool (true, "Show High-Probability Entry Zone", group=GRP_ERF)
entryZoneWidthA = input.float(0.15, "Entry Zone Half-Width (ATR)",      group=GRP_ERF, minval=0.02, step=0.01)

var box   ezBox = na
var label ezLbl = na
if barstate.islast
    if not na(ezBox)
        box.delete(ezBox)
    if not na(ezLbl)
        label.delete(ezLbl)
    if showEntryZone and direction != 0 and not na(eae_primaryAttractorPrice)
        float _ezMid = eae_primaryAttractorPrice
        float _ezH   = _ezMid + atr * entryZoneWidthA
        float _ezL   = _ezMid - atr * entryZoneWidthA
        color _ezBg  = direction == 1 ? color.new(#00ffcc, 82) : color.new(#ff2244, 82)
        color _ezBd  = direction == 1 ? color.new(#00ffcc, 15) : color.new(#ff2244, 15)
        ezBox := box.new(bar_index - 2, _ezH, bar_index + 40, _ezL,
             bgcolor=f_zoneFill(_ezBg), border_color=_ezBd, border_width=1, border_style=line.style_solid)
        ezLbl := label.new(bar_index + 40, _ezMid,
             "ENTRY ZONE  " + str.tostring(math.round(eae_primaryAttractorScore)) + "%  " + eae_primaryAttractorLabel,
             style=label.style_label_left,
             color=_ezBd, textcolor=color.white, size=size.small)

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 9 — PHYSICS OBSERVATION LAYER (declared before Engine 1A above)
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// obs_ExpansionScore, obs_DecayScore, obs_CurvatureScore, obs_AbsorptionScore,
// obs_LiquidityScore, physicsMax, physicsDiff, physicsConsensus,
// velocityScore, accelerationScore, convexityScore, expansionScore
// — all declared in the moved block above. No re-declaration needed here.

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 10 — LIQUIDITY HEATMAP ENGINE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

float _swH = ta.highest(high, liqSweepLookback)
float _swL = ta.lowest (low,  liqSweepLookback)

bool liqSweepBull = not na(flipTop) and _swH > flipTop
bool liqSweepBear = not na(flipBot) and _swL < flipBot

var array<float> liqLevels  = array.new_float()
var array<float> liqWeights = array.new_float()
var array<int>   liqAges    = array.new_int()
var array<int>   liqTypes   = array.new_int()

float volAvg  = ta.sma(volume, 20)
float normVol = volAvg > 0 ? volume[pivotLen] / volAvg : 1.0

if not na(pivH) or not na(pivL)
    float lvl   = not na(pivH) ? pivH : pivL
    int   lType = not na(pivH) ? 1 : -1
    float swRng = (high[pivotLen] - low[pivotLen]) / math.max(atr, 1e-10)
    float wt    = normVol * swRng
    array.push(liqLevels,  lvl)
    array.push(liqWeights, wt)
    array.push(liqAges,    bar_index - pivotLen)
    array.push(liqTypes,   lType)

if array.size(liqLevels) > 150
    array.shift(liqLevels)
    array.shift(liqWeights)
    array.shift(liqAges)
    array.shift(liqTypes)

float wDensity      = 0.0
float wDensityAbove = 0.0
float wDensityBelow = 0.0
float liqRadiusP    = atr * liqRadius
float liqRadiusWide = atr * liqRadius * 3.0

if array.size(liqLevels) > 0
    for i = 0 to array.size(liqLevels) - 1
        float lvl  = array.get(liqLevels,  i)
        float wt   = array.get(liqWeights, i)
        int   age  = bar_index - array.get(liqAges, i)
        float dcy  = math.pow(liqAgDecay, age)
        float dist = math.abs(close - lvl)
        if dist < liqRadiusP
            wDensity += wt * dcy
        if dist < liqRadiusWide
            if lvl > close
                wDensityAbove += wt * dcy * (1.0 - dist / liqRadiusWide)
            else
                wDensityBelow += wt * dcy * (1.0 - dist / liqRadiusWide)

float liqHeatRaw = math.min((wDensityAbove + wDensityBelow) / 2.0, 5.0) / 5.0 * 100.0
liqHeat         := math.min(math.max(liqHeatRaw, 0.0), 100.0)
string liqZone   = liqHeat < 30 ? "Open space" : liqHeat < 70 ? "Active" : "Congested"
bool liqVacuum   = wDensity < 0.5

bool liqSweepOK = not requireLiqSweep or
     (direction ==  1 and (liqSweepBull or liqVacuum)) or
     (direction == -1 and (liqSweepBear or liqVacuum))

plotshape(showLiq and not na(pivH), "Pivot High", shape.circle,
     location.abovebar, color.new(color.orange, 50), size=size.tiny)
plotshape(showLiq and not na(pivL), "Pivot Low",  shape.circle,
     location.belowbar, color.new(color.blue,   50), size=size.tiny)

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 11 — GEOMETRY ENGINE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

int   obAge       = not na(obBirthBar) ? bar_index - obBirthBar : 0
bool  obFresh     = obAge <= obMaxBars
float obFreshness = not na(obBirthBar) ? math.max(0.0, 1.0 - obAge / float(obMaxBars)) : 0.0

float originToExtreme = na
if not na(point4OriginHigh) and not na(point4OriginLow)
    float orig = direction == 1 ? point4OriginLow : point4OriginHigh
    float extr = direction == 1 ? nz(cycleHigh, orig) : nz(cycleLow, orig)
    originToExtreme := math.abs(extr - orig)

float extremeToFlipzone = na
if not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot) and not na(cycleHigh) and not na(cycleLow)
    float fzMid = (flipTop + flipBot) / 2.0
    float extr  = direction == 1 ? cycleHigh : cycleLow
    extremeToFlipzone := math.abs(extr - fzMid)

float flipzoneWidth = not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot) ? flipTop - flipBot : na

float remainingRoom = na
if not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot)
    float fzMid = (flipTop + flipBot) / 2.0
    remainingRoom := math.min(math.abs(close - fzMid) / math.max(atr * 4.0, 1e-10) * 100.0, 100.0)
float availableSpace = remainingRoom

string cycleCapacity = na(availableSpace)     ? "–"              :
                       availableSpace >= 60   ? "ROOM: HIGH"     :
                       availableSpace >= 30   ? "ROOM: MID"      : "ROOM: LOW"

bool geoFullConvexityPossible    = not na(originToExtreme) and not na(flipzoneWidth) and
     originToExtreme > atr * 6.0 and flipzoneWidth < atr * 3.0
bool geoPartialConvexityPossible = not na(originToExtreme) and
     originToExtreme > atr * 3.0 and originToExtreme <= atr * 6.0
bool geoAbsorptionOnly           = not na(originToExtreme) and originToExtreme <= atr * 3.0

float zonePrecision = not na(flipzoneWidth) ?
     math.max(100.0 - math.min((flipzoneWidth / math.max(atr * 0.5, 1e-10)) * 50.0, 100.0), 0.0) : 0.0

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 12 — WAVE INTELLIGENCE SYSTEM
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

float ref_effNorm     = math.min(efficiency,                                         1.0)
float ref_dispNorm    = math.min(displacement / math.max(dispThresh * 2.0, 1e-10),   1.0)
float ref_velNorm     = math.min(math.abs(velocity) / math.max(atr * 0.15, 1e-10),   1.0)
float ref_curvNorm    = math.min(math.abs(convSmooth) / math.max(atr * convMult * 2.0, 1e-10), 1.0)
float ref_absNorm     = math.min(obs_AbsorptionScore / 100.0,                        1.0)
float ref_decayNorm   = math.min(obs_DecayScore / 100.0,                             1.0)
float ref_liqNorm     = math.min(obs_LiquidityScore / 100.0,                         1.0)

f_idealSim(float _eObs, float _dObs, float _vObs, float _cObs,
           float _eIdeal, float _dIdeal, float _vIdeal, float _cIdeal) =>
    float _diff = math.pow(_eObs - _eIdeal, 2) +
                  math.pow(_dObs - _dIdeal, 2) +
                  math.pow(_vObs - _vIdeal, 2) +
                  math.pow(_cObs - _cIdeal, 2)
    math.max(0.0, 100.0 * (1.0 - _diff / 4.0))

float sim_Expansion    = f_idealSim(ref_effNorm, ref_dispNorm, ref_velNorm, ref_curvNorm, 0.85, 0.80, 0.80, 0.10)
float sim_PreConv      = f_idealSim(ref_effNorm, ref_dispNorm, ref_velNorm, ref_curvNorm, 0.60, 0.55, 0.40, 0.50)
float sim_Induction    = f_idealSim(ref_effNorm, ref_dispNorm, ref_velNorm, ref_curvNorm, 0.65, 0.60, 0.30, 0.60)
float sim_Liquidity    = f_idealSim(ref_effNorm, ref_dispNorm, ref_velNorm, ref_curvNorm, 0.45, 0.85, 0.15, 0.80)
float sim_Creation     = f_idealSim(ref_effNorm, ref_dispNorm, ref_velNorm, ref_curvNorm, 0.30, 0.70, 0.05, 0.90)
float sim_Absorption   = f_idealSim(ref_effNorm, ref_dispNorm, ref_velNorm, ref_curvNorm, 0.20, 0.25, 0.10, 0.40)
float sim_Retracement  = f_idealSim(ref_effNorm, ref_dispNorm, ref_velNorm, ref_curvNorm, 0.70, 0.65, 0.65, 0.25)
float sim_DemandReturn = f_idealSim(ref_effNorm, ref_dispNorm, ref_velNorm, ref_curvNorm, 0.50, 0.40, 0.35, 0.20)

// ── 12-POS: GEOMETRIC WAVE POSITION ENGINE ────────────────────────────────────

float waveTotalRange   = not na(originToExtreme) ? originToExtreme : atr * 5.0
float currentToFlipMid = not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot) ?
     math.abs(close - (flipTop + flipBot) / 2.0) : atr * 4.0
float currentToExtreme = direction == 1 ?
     math.abs(nz(cycleHigh, close + atr) - close) :
     math.abs(close - nz(cycleLow, close - atr))

float distToCreation_atr    = currentToExtreme / math.max(atr, 1e-10)
float distToAbsorption_atr  = (currentToExtreme + atr * 0.5) / math.max(atr, 1e-10)
float distToRetracement_atr = (currentToExtreme + atr * 1.5) / math.max(atr, 1e-10)
float distToDemand_atr      = currentToFlipMid  / math.max(atr, 1e-10)
float distToOrigin_atr      = not na(point4OriginHigh) and not na(point4OriginLow) ?
     math.abs(close - (direction == 1 ? point4OriginLow : point4OriginHigh)) / math.max(atr, 1e-10) :
     waveTotalRange / math.max(atr, 1e-10)

float _posNormDen = math.max(waveTotalRange, atr * 0.5)
float posDistToCreation    = math.min(currentToExtreme / _posNormDen * 100.0, 100.0)
float posDistToAbsorption  = math.min((currentToExtreme + atr * 0.5) / _posNormDen * 100.0, 100.0)
float posDistToRetracement = math.min((currentToExtreme + atr * 1.5) / _posNormDen * 100.0, 100.0)
float posDistToDemand      = math.min(currentToFlipMid / _posNormDen * 100.0, 100.0)
float posDistToOrigin      = math.min(distToOrigin_atr * atr / _posNormDen * 100.0, 100.0)

// ── 12-CM: CONVEXITY MATURITY ENGINE ─────────────────────────────────────────

float expWeaknessScore = math.min(
     ((efficiency < effThresh ? (1.0 - efficiency / math.max(effThresh, 1e-10)) * 40.0 : 0.0) +
     (obs_DecayScore * 0.30) +
     (math.abs(velocity) < math.abs(velocity[2]) * 0.6 ? 20.0 : 0.0)) * (100.0 / 90.0),
     100.0)

float inductionMatScore = math.min(
     (inductionEvidence ? 35.0 : 0.0) +
     (obs_CurvatureScore * 0.35) +
     (preConvEvidence ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (displacement > dispThresh * 1.2 and (bullMomDecay or bearMomDecay) ? 10.0 : 0.0),
     100.0)

float liqMatScore = math.min(
     (obs_LiquidityScore * 0.50) +
     (liqSweepBull or liqSweepBear ? 30.0 : 0.0) +
     (liqHeat > 60 ? 20.0 : liqHeat > 30 ? 10.0 : 0.0),
     100.0)

float rawConvexityMaturity = math.min(
     expWeaknessScore   * 0.35 +
     inductionMatScore  * 0.35 +
     liqMatScore        * 0.30,
     100.0)

// convexityMaturity is declared as var before Engine 1A; update it here with the computed raw value.
convexityMaturity := convexityMaturity + (2.0 / (beliefSmooth + 1)) * (rawConvexityMaturity - convexityMaturity)

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ENGINE 1A — UNIFIED DISPLAY-PHASE AUTHORITY (global; single source for ALL labels)
// Every chart label, panel, narrative and the M5 decision row consume the single
// string `currentDisplayPhase` and the `liqg_*` overlay produced here. This is the
// sole owner of the visible phase string — no downstream object re-derives it.
// Includes Engine 1A.7 (Pre-Objective Liquidation Wave) as a live, physics-driven
// overlay on the two Induction phases. "Physics" here is the EARLY-available
// consensus that exists at this point in the file: EDE dissipation, RE resolution,
// geometric/convexity capacity and momentum efficiency, plus the M5 structural
// objective (se5_tgt) for distance. The late FRZ/DOM/rotation engines refine the
// panels downstream but never reclassify this authority. Additive — the canonical
// ie1a_currentPhase is unchanged and is the structural backbone consumed below.
// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
var bool   liqg_active   = false
var bool   liqg_isRetr   = false
var int    liqg_dir      = 0
var float  liqg_target   = na
var float  liqg_initDist = na
bool   _liqgRetr = ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Induction"
bool   _liqgArm  = ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Induction" or _liqgRetr
float  _liqgObj  = se5_tgt
if _liqgArm and not liqg_active and not na(_liqgObj)
    liqg_active   := true
    liqg_isRetr   := _liqgRetr
    liqg_target   := _liqgObj
    liqg_dir      := _liqgObj > close ? 1 : -1
    liqg_initDist := math.max(math.abs(_liqgObj - close), atr * 0.5)
if liqg_active and not na(_liqgObj)
    liqg_target := _liqgObj
// Distance compression: 100% = at origin, 0% = arrived (physics distance, never time)
float  _liqgRemain  = (liqg_active and not na(liqg_target)) ? math.abs(liqg_target - close) : na
float  liqg_distPct = (liqg_active and not na(_liqgRemain)) ? math.min(100.0, _liqgRemain / math.max(liqg_initDist, 1e-10) * 100.0) : na
bool   _liqgCapExh   = ede_dissipationProgress > 60 or convexityMaturity > 60
bool   _liqgResolved = re_resolutionState == "RESOLVED"
bool   _liqgEnergyLo = efficiency < effThresh * 0.7
bool   _liqgMagnet   = liqg_active and not na(liqg_distPct) and liqg_distPct < 20
// OBJECTIVE ARRIVAL — Structure ∧ Momentum ∧ Physics simultaneously
bool   _liqgArrStruct = liqg_active and not na(liqg_target) and (liqg_dir == 1 ? close >= liqg_target : close <= liqg_target)
bool   _liqgArrPhys   = _liqgCapExh and (_liqgResolved or _liqgMagnet)
bool   liqg_objArrival = _liqgArrStruct and _liqgEnergyLo and _liqgArrPhys
// TRUE CHANGE OF CHARACTER — never from BOS alone
bool   _liqgCounterBOS = liqg_dir == 1 ? bearBOS : bullBOS
bool   liqg_trueCHoCH  = liqg_objArrival and _liqgCounterBOS and _liqgEnergyLo and _liqgResolved
// Sub-state from distance compression + physics (Initialization → Objective Arrival)
string liqg_subPhase =
     not liqg_active                                          ? "" :
     liqg_objArrival                                          ? "Objective Arrival" :
     (_liqgMagnet and _liqgEnergyLo)                          ? "Terminal Liquidation" :
     (convexityMaturity > 40 or ede_dissipationProgress > 40) ? "Induction" :
     (not na(liqg_distPct) and liqg_distPct < 70)             ? "Displacement" :
     (not na(liqg_distPct) and liqg_distPct < 95)             ? "Push" : "Initialization"
string liqg_title =
     not liqg_active ? "" :
     liqg_isRetr and displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 ? "Pre-Supply Return Liquidation Wave" :
     liqg_isRetr                              ? "Pre-Demand Return Liquidation Wave" :
     displayWaveDir_M5 == -1                  ? "Pre-New Low Liquidation Wave" : "Pre-New High Liquidation Wave"
// Retire when the canonical phase LEAVES the induction/liquidity window (so the
// liquidation overlay can never latch indefinitely), or on genuine completion.
// This keeps currentDisplayPhase == the engine's real phase outside that window.
bool _liqgInWindow = ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Induction" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Liquidity" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Induction" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Liquidity"
if liqg_active and (not _liqgInWindow or (liqg_objArrival and liqg_trueCHoCH))
    liqg_active := false
// ABSORPTION GATE (9.8): the visible phase may only read "Absorption" after a genuine
// objective arrival + true CHoCH for THIS wave. Latch unlocks on arrival+CHoCH and
// resets when a new wave is born — preventing premature absorption regardless of BOS.
var bool liqg_absorbUnlocked = false
if liqg_objArrival and liqg_trueCHoCH
    liqg_absorbUnlocked := true
if ie1a_currentPhase == "Point 4 Origin"
    liqg_absorbUnlocked := false
// SINGLE phase-string authority — consumed by every label / panel / narrative below
string currentDisplayPhase = liqg_active ? (liqg_title + (liqg_subPhase != "" ? " • " + liqg_subPhase : "")) : ie1a_currentPhase
string _cdpDir   = displayWaveDir_M5 == 1 ? "Bullish" : displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 ? "Bearish" : "Neutral"
string liqg_arrTx = liqg_objArrival ? "Yes" : (not na(liqg_distPct) and liqg_distPct < 12) ? "Imminent" : "No"
// 3-D AGREEMENT → dynamic confidence / integrity (agreement quality, not score thresholds).
//   Structure: wave still holds its M5 origin · Momentum: travelling with the wave ·
//   Physics: energy not yet fully resolved/dissipated. Each dimension contributes equally.
bool  _cdpSAgree = displayWaveDir_M5 != 0 and (displayWaveDir_M5 == 1 ? close > se5_inv : close < se5_inv)
bool  _cdpMAgree = displayWaveDir_M5 != 0 and (displayWaveDir_M5 == 1 ? velocity > 0 : velocity < 0)
bool  _cdpPAgree = re_resolutionState != "RESOLVED" and ede_dissipationProgress < 80
float phaseConfidence = (_cdpSAgree ? 34.0 : 0.0) + (_cdpMAgree ? 33.0 : 0.0) + (_cdpPAgree ? 33.0 : 0.0)
float phaseIntegrity  = math.max(0.0, math.min(100.0, phaseConfidence * 0.6 + (100.0 - math.min(ede_dissipationProgress, 100.0)) * 0.4))
// REAL PHASE PROGRESS (dynamic, continuous, never time/bar based): distance consumed
// toward the M5 objective + energy dissipated + convexity maturity. During a
// liquidation wave it tracks the objective-completion distance directly.
float _ppDistConsumed = (not na(se5_tgt) and not na(se5_inv)) ? math.min(100.0, math.abs(close - se5_inv) / math.max(math.abs(se5_tgt - se5_inv), 1e-10) * 100.0) : na
float phaseProgress = liqg_active and not na(liqg_distPct) ? (100.0 - liqg_distPct) : na(_ppDistConsumed) ? math.min(100.0, ede_dissipationProgress * 0.5 + convexityMaturity * 0.5) : math.min(100.0, _ppDistConsumed * 0.5 + convexityMaturity * 0.3 + ede_dissipationProgress * 0.2)
// Full chart-label projection (Direction · Phase [· Substate] · Target · Distance · Arrival · Confidence · Integrity)
string liqg_readout = _cdpDir + " · " + currentDisplayPhase + (liqg_active ? ("\nTarget " + (na(liqg_target) ? "forming" : str.tostring(math.round_to_mintick(liqg_target))) + "   Dist " + (na(liqg_distPct) ? "–" : str.tostring(math.round(liqg_distPct)) + "%") + "   Arrival " + liqg_arrTx) : "") + "   ·   Conf " + str.tostring(math.round(phaseConfidence)) + "%  Integ " + str.tostring(math.round(phaseIntegrity)) + "%"

string convMatStage =
     convexityMaturity >= 80 ? "Terminal Convexity" :
     convexityMaturity >= 50 ? "Mature Convexity"   :
     convexityMaturity >= 20 ? "Developing Conv"    : "Early Convexity"

// ── 12-WP: WAVE PROGRESS ESTIMATION ──────────────────────────────────────────

float _progressFromGeom = na
if not na(point4OriginHigh) and not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot)
    float _origin  = direction == 1 ? point4OriginLow  : point4OriginHigh
    float _extreme = direction == 1 ? nz(cycleHigh, close + atr) : nz(cycleLow, close - atr)
    float _fzMid   = (flipTop + flipBot) / 2.0
    float _totalMove = math.abs(_extreme - _origin)
    float _toFzMid   = math.abs(_extreme - _fzMid)
    float _traveled  = math.abs(close - _origin)
    float _expProg   = _totalMove > 1e-10 ? math.min(_traveled / _totalMove * 60.0, 60.0) : 30.0
    float _retrMove  = math.abs(close - _extreme)
    float _retrProg  = _toFzMid > 1e-10 ? math.min(_retrMove / math.max(_toFzMid, 1e-10) * 40.0, 40.0) : 0.0
    float _retrWeight = math.min(obs_AbsorptionScore / 40.0, 1.0)
    _progressFromGeom := _expProg + _retrProg * _retrWeight

float _geomProgress = nz(_progressFromGeom, 30.0)

float _simAnchor =
     sim_DemandReturn >= sim_Retracement and sim_DemandReturn >= sim_Absorption and
     sim_DemandReturn >= sim_Creation    and sim_DemandReturn >= sim_Expansion   ? 95.0 :
