     sim_Retracement  >= sim_Absorption and sim_Retracement  >= sim_Creation    and
     sim_Retracement  >= sim_Expansion                                           ? 87.0 :
     sim_Absorption   >= sim_Creation   and sim_Absorption   >= sim_Expansion   ? 75.0 :
     sim_Creation     >= sim_Liquidity  and sim_Creation     >= sim_Expansion   ? 62.0 :
     sim_Liquidity    >= sim_Induction  and sim_Liquidity    >= sim_Expansion   ? 52.0 :
     sim_Induction    >= sim_PreConv    and sim_Induction    >= sim_Expansion   ? 43.0 :
     sim_PreConv      >= sim_Expansion                                           ? 33.0 : 22.0

float _convBandCenter   = 47.5
float _convBandHalfW    = 14.5
float _convWeight = math.max(0.0, 1.0 - math.abs(_simAnchor - _convBandCenter) / _convBandHalfW)
float _convAdjust = (convexityMaturity / 100.0) * (_simAnchor - 33.0) * 0.50 * _convWeight

float _physProgress = _simAnchor + _convAdjust

float rawWaveProgress = _geomProgress * 0.60 + _physProgress * 0.40

var float waveProgress = 30.0
waveProgress := waveProgress + (2.0 / (beliefSmooth + 1)) * (rawWaveProgress - waveProgress)
waveProgress := math.max(0.0, math.min(100.0, waveProgress))

// NOTE: waveProgressLabel is now a display-only relay of ENGINE 1A's canonical phase.
// The numeric waveProgress score remains available as a confidence/proximity signal
// for downstream engines but DOES NOT determine canonical lifecycle phase.
// All phase assignment authority belongs exclusively to ie1a_currentPhase.
string waveProgressLabel = ie1a_currentPhase

// ── 12-FIT: WAVE MODEL FIT ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

float _bestSim = math.max(sim_Expansion, sim_PreConv, sim_Induction, sim_Liquidity,
                           sim_Creation, sim_Absorption, sim_Retracement, sim_DemandReturn)

float _geomConsistency = math.min(
     (not na(originToExtreme) and originToExtreme > atr * 2.0 ? 30.0 : 0.0) +
     (not na(flipzoneWidth)   and flipzoneWidth < atr * 4.0    ? 25.0 : 0.0) +
     (not na(cycleHigh) or not na(cycleLow)                    ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (direction != 0                                           ? 25.0 : 0.0),
     100.0)

float rawWaveModelFit = _bestSim * 0.55 + _geomConsistency * 0.45
var float waveModelFit = 50.0
waveModelFit := waveModelFit + (2.0 / (beliefSmooth + 1)) * (rawWaveModelFit - waveModelFit)
waveModelFit := math.max(0.0, math.min(100.0, waveModelFit))

// ── 12A: BELIEF ENGINE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

preConvEvidence    := bullMomDecay or bearMomDecay
inductionEvidence  := (direction == 1  and bearImpulse and structBias ==  1) or
                          (direction == -1 and bullImpulse and structBias == -1)
bool liquidityEvidence  = obs_LiquidityScore > 50.0 and obs_DecayScore > 40.0

float _expPosMult = waveProgress < 40.0 ? 1.20 : waveProgress < 60.0 ? 0.80 : 0.50
float rawExpansionBelief = math.min(
     (obs_ExpansionScore * 0.45 +
     (bullImpulse or bearImpulse ? 30.0 : 0.0) +
     (efficiency > effThresh * 1.1 ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     sim_Expansion * 0.10) * _expPosMult,
     100.0)

float _convPosMult = (waveProgress >= 30.0 and waveProgress <= 65.0) ? 1.30 : 0.70
float rawConvexityBelief = math.min(
     (obs_DecayScore * 0.30 +
     obs_CurvatureScore * 0.25 +
     (preConvEvidence   ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     (inductionEvidence ? 10.0 : 0.0) +
     (liquidityEvidence ?  5.0 : 0.0) +
     convexityMaturity  * 0.08) * _convPosMult,
     100.0)

float _creatPosMult = (waveProgress >= 45.0 and waveProgress <= 68.0) ? 1.40 : 0.60
float rawCreationBelief = math.min(
     ((convexityMaturity > 50 ? convexityMaturity * 0.12 : 0.0) +
     (obs_DecayScore > 60 ? obs_DecayScore * 0.20 : 0.0) +
     (obs_LiquidityScore > 50 ? obs_LiquidityScore * 0.20 : 0.0) +
     (obs_AbsorptionScore > 20 ? obs_AbsorptionScore * 0.15 : 0.0) +
     (not na(cycleHigh) and not na(cycleLow) and
      ((direction == 1 and high >= nz(cycleHigh, high) * 0.998) or
       (direction == -1 and low <= nz(cycleLow, low) * 1.002)) ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     sim_Creation * 0.10 +
     (posDistToCreation < 15.0 ? (15.0 - posDistToCreation) * 1.0 : 0.0)) * _creatPosMult,
     100.0)

float rawAbsorptionBelief = math.min(
     obs_AbsorptionScore * 0.50 +
     (efficiency < effThresh * 0.6 ? 25.0 : 0.0) +
     (displacement < dispThresh * 0.5 ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     sim_Absorption * 0.10,
     100.0)

float rawRetracementBelief = math.min(
     ((direction == 1  and bearImpulse) or (direction == -1 and bullImpulse) ? 45.0 : 0.0) +
     (rawAbsorptionBelief > 50 ? rawAbsorptionBelief * 0.30 : 0.0) +
     (obs_CurvatureScore > 40 ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     sim_Retracement * 0.10,
     100.0)

float rawDemandReturnBelief = math.min(
     (not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot) and
      close <= flipTop and close >= flipBot ? 35.0 : 0.0) +
     (rawRetracementBelief > 60 ? rawRetracementBelief * 0.30 : 0.0) +
     (liqHeat > 50 ? liqHeat * 0.15 : 0.0) +
     (liqSweepBull or liqSweepBear ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     sim_DemandReturn * 0.10,
     100.0)

// ── FIX: guard against NaN before EMA smoothing ───────────────────────────────
float safeRawExpBelief   = nz(rawExpansionBelief,    0.0)
float safeRawConvBelief  = nz(rawConvexityBelief,    0.0)
float safeRawCreatBelief = nz(rawCreationBelief,     0.0)
float safeRawAbsBelief   = nz(rawAbsorptionBelief,   0.0)
float safeRawRetrBelief  = nz(rawRetracementBelief,  0.0)
float safeRawDRBelief    = nz(rawDemandReturnBelief, 0.0)

var float expansionBelief    = 0.0
var float convexityBelief    = 0.0
var float creationBelief     = 0.0
var float absorptionBelief   = 0.0
var float retracementBelief  = 0.0
var float demandReturnBelief = 0.0

float bSmAlpha = 2.0 / (beliefSmooth + 1)
expansionBelief    := expansionBelief    + bSmAlpha * (safeRawExpBelief   - expansionBelief)
convexityBelief    := convexityBelief    + bSmAlpha * (safeRawConvBelief  - convexityBelief)
creationBelief     := creationBelief     + bSmAlpha * (safeRawCreatBelief - creationBelief)
absorptionBelief   := absorptionBelief   + bSmAlpha * (safeRawAbsBelief   - absorptionBelief)
retracementBelief  := retracementBelief  + bSmAlpha * (safeRawRetrBelief  - retracementBelief)
demandReturnBelief := demandReturnBelief + bSmAlpha * (safeRawDRBelief    - demandReturnBelief)

// Final display-safe values (clamp 0–100 and strip any residual NaN)
float d_expansionBelief    = math.max(0.0, math.min(100.0, nz(expansionBelief,    0.0)))
float d_convexityBelief    = math.max(0.0, math.min(100.0, nz(convexityBelief,    0.0)))
float d_creationBelief     = math.max(0.0, math.min(100.0, nz(creationBelief,     0.0)))
float d_absorptionBelief   = math.max(0.0, math.min(100.0, nz(absorptionBelief,   0.0)))
float d_retracementBelief  = math.max(0.0, math.min(100.0, nz(retracementBelief,  0.0)))
float d_demandReturnBelief = math.max(0.0, math.min(100.0, nz(demandReturnBelief, 0.0)))

// ── 12B: PHASE PROXIMITY ENGINE ──────────────────────────────────────────────

float expansionProximity = math.min(
     sim_Expansion * 0.50 +
     (bullImpulse or bearImpulse ? 25.0 : 0.0) +
     (waveProgress < 35.0 ? (35.0 - waveProgress) * 0.50 : 0.0) +
     (obs_ExpansionScore * 0.25), 100.0)

float convexityProximity = math.min(
     sim_PreConv * 0.25 + sim_Induction * 0.25 + sim_Liquidity * 0.20 +
     (preConvEvidence ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     (waveProgress >= 30.0 and waveProgress <= 65.0 ? 15.0 : 0.0), 100.0)

float creationProximity = math.min(
     sim_Creation * 0.50 +
     (not na(cycleHigh) and direction == 1  and high >= nz(cycleHigh, high)  * 0.995 ? 25.0 : 0.0) +
     (not na(cycleLow)  and direction == -1 and low  <= nz(cycleLow,  low)   * 1.005 ? 25.0 : 0.0) +
     (convexityMaturity > 60 ? convexityMaturity * 0.25 : 0.0), 100.0)

float absorptionProximity = math.min(
     sim_Absorption * 0.50 +
     (obs_AbsorptionScore * 0.35) +
     (waveProgress >= 68.0 and waveProgress <= 80.0 ? 15.0 : 0.0), 100.0)

float retracementProximity = math.min(
     sim_Retracement * 0.50 +
     ((direction == 1  and bearImpulse) or (direction == -1 and bullImpulse) ? 30.0 : 0.0) +
     (waveProgress >= 78.0 and waveProgress <= 93.0 ? 20.0 : 0.0), 100.0)

float demandReturnProximity = math.min(
     sim_DemandReturn * 0.50 +
     (not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot) and close <= flipTop and close >= flipBot ? 30.0 : 0.0) +
     (waveProgress >= 90.0 ? 20.0 : 0.0), 100.0)

// ── 12D: HYPOTHESIS ENGINE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

float _fitMult = math.max(0.60, waveModelFit / 100.0)

float hyp_LateExpansion = (
     expansionBelief * 0.35 +
     (waveProgress < 38.0 ? (38.0 - waveProgress) * 0.80 : 0.0) +
     (convexityMaturity < 30 ? (30.0 - convexityMaturity) * 0.30 : 0.0) +
     sim_Expansion * 0.20 +
     (expansionBelief > 55 and convexityBelief > 30 ? 10.0 : 0.0)
     ) * _fitMult

float hyp_TerminalConvexity = (
     convexityBelief * 0.30 +
     (convexityMaturity > 50 ? convexityMaturity * 0.25 : 0.0) +
     (waveProgress >= 38.0 and waveProgress <= 62.0 ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (sim_Induction + sim_Liquidity) * 0.10 +
     (posDistToCreation < 25.0 ? (25.0 - posDistToCreation) * 0.50 : 0.0)
     ) * _fitMult

float hyp_CreationForming = (
     creationBelief * 0.40 +
     (convexityMaturity > 65 ? (convexityMaturity - 65.0) * 0.40 : 0.0) +
     (posDistToCreation < 15.0 ? (15.0 - posDistToCreation) * 1.50 : 0.0) +
     sim_Creation * 0.20
     ) * _fitMult

float hyp_AbsorptionActive = (
     absorptionBelief * 0.45 +
     (waveProgress >= 68.0 and waveProgress <= 80.0 ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     sim_Absorption * 0.25 +
     (m1AbsorptionEmer ? 10.0 : 0.0)
     ) * _fitMult

float hyp_RetracementActive = (
     retracementBelief * 0.45 +
     (waveProgress >= 78.0 and waveProgress <= 92.0 ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     sim_Retracement * 0.25 +
     ((direction == 1 and bearImpulse) or (direction == -1 and bullImpulse) ? 10.0 : 0.0)
     ) * _fitMult

float hyp_DemandReturn = (
     demandReturnBelief * 0.45 +
     (waveProgress >= 88.0 ? (waveProgress - 88.0) * 1.20 : 0.0) +
     sim_DemandReturn * 0.25 +
     (closeInside ? 15.0 : 0.0)
     ) * _fitMult

// Fixed theoretical maxima (with _fitMult <= 1.0) replace the old "rescale-to-100"
// normalization, which always forced the leading hypothesis to ~100% regardless
// of how weak its raw score was.
float HYP_MAX_LATEEXP   = 105.0
float HYP_MAX_TERMCONV  = 108.0
float HYP_MAX_CREATFORM = 97.0
float HYP_MAX_ABS       = 100.0
float HYP_MAX_RETR      = 100.0
float HYP_MAX_DR        = 100.0

float hyp_LateExpansion_N     = math.max(0.0, math.min(hyp_LateExpansion     / HYP_MAX_LATEEXP   * 100.0, 100.0))
float hyp_EarlyConvexity_N    = math.max(0.0, math.min(hyp_TerminalConvexity / HYP_MAX_TERMCONV  * 100.0, 100.0))
float hyp_CreationForming_N   = math.max(0.0, math.min(hyp_CreationForming   / HYP_MAX_CREATFORM * 100.0, 100.0))
float hyp_AbsorptionActive_N  = math.max(0.0, math.min(hyp_AbsorptionActive  / HYP_MAX_ABS        * 100.0, 100.0))
float hyp_RetracementActive_N = math.max(0.0, math.min(hyp_RetracementActive / HYP_MAX_RETR       * 100.0, 100.0))
float hyp_DemandReturn_N      = math.max(0.0, math.min(hyp_DemandReturn      / HYP_MAX_DR         * 100.0, 100.0))

float hypMax = math.max(hyp_LateExpansion_N, hyp_EarlyConvexity_N, hyp_CreationForming_N,
                         hyp_AbsorptionActive_N, hyp_RetracementActive_N, hyp_DemandReturn_N)

// primaryHypothesis — DISPLAY ONLY, sourced exclusively from ENGINE 1A.
// Maps ie1a_hypFamily to the hypothesis vocabulary for dashboard display and
// belief-score confidence rendering. Does NOT independently assign lifecycle phase.
// Belief scores (hyp_LateExpansion_N etc.) remain as confidence metrics only.
string primaryHypothesis = ie1a_hypFamily

// primaryHypothesisConf — confidence level for the current IE1A phase family,
// sourced from the belief score corresponding to ie1a_hypFamily.
float primaryHypothesisConf =
     primaryHypothesis == "EXPANSION"           ? hyp_LateExpansion_N     :
     primaryHypothesis == "CONVEXITY FORMING"   ? hyp_EarlyConvexity_N    :
     primaryHypothesis == "CREATION FORMING"    ? hyp_CreationForming_N   :
     primaryHypothesis == "ABSORPTION"          ? hyp_AbsorptionActive_N  :
     primaryHypothesis == "RETRACEMENT"         ? hyp_RetracementActive_N : hyp_DemandReturn_N

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// CANONICAL PHASE CLASSIFIER
// ENGINE 1A is the sole lifecycle authority.  l0_targetWave / l0_currentPhase
// are assigned directly from ie1a_waveDirection / ie1a_currentPhase.
//
// f_toCanonicalPhase and f_classifyWave are retained as utility functions for
// L1 / L2 / L3 HTF layers which translate HTF belief-score vocabulary into
// canonical lifecycle phases.  They do NOT assign current-TF lifecycle state.
// Only ENGINE 1A may do that.
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

f_toCanonicalPhase(string rawPhase, bool isExpansionSide, bool isBull) =>
    string _out = "Point 4 Origin"
    if rawPhase == "EXPANSION"
        _out := "Expansion"
    else if rawPhase == "CONVEXITY FORMING"
        _out := isExpansionSide ? "Expansion Pre-Convexity" : "Retracement Pre-Convexity"
    else if rawPhase == "CREATION FORMING"
        _out := isBull ? "New High" : "New Low"
    else if rawPhase == "ABSORPTION"
        _out := "Absorption"
    else if rawPhase == "RETRACEMENT"
        _out := "Retracement"
    else if rawPhase == "DEMAND/SUPPLY RETURN"
        _out := isBull ? "Demand Return" : "Supply Return"
    else if rawPhase == "Expansion"
        _out := "Expansion"
    else if rawPhase == "Pre-Convexity"
        _out := isExpansionSide ? "Expansion Pre-Convexity" : "Retracement Pre-Convexity"
    else if rawPhase == "Liquidity"
        _out := isExpansionSide ? "Expansion Liquidity" : "Retracement Liquidity"
    else if rawPhase == "Absorption"
        _out := "Absorption"
    else if rawPhase == "M1 Expansion"
        _out := "Expansion"
    else if rawPhase == "M1 Exp Weak"
        _out := "Expansion Pre-Convexity"
    else if rawPhase == "M1 Convexity"
        _out := isExpansionSide ? "Expansion Induction" : "Retracement Induction"
    else if rawPhase == "M1 Liquidity"
        _out := isExpansionSide ? "Expansion Liquidity" : "Retracement Liquidity"
    else if rawPhase == "M1 Absorption"
        _out := "Absorption"
    _out

f_classifyWave(string _rawPhase, int _dir, bool _expSide) =>
    string _targetWave   = _dir == 1 ? "Bullish Wave" : _dir == -1 ? "Bearish Wave" : "Neutral"
    bool   _isBull       = _dir == 1
    string _currentPhase = f_toCanonicalPhase(_rawPhase, _expSide, _isBull)
    [_targetWave, _currentPhase]

// ── L0 PRIMARY: assigned exclusively from ENGINE 1A ──────────────────────────
// ENGINE 1A is the sole lifecycle authority — l0_targetWave and l0_currentPhase
// must not be derived from primaryHypothesis, waveProgress, or any score.
string l0_targetWave   = l0_dirLabel     // L0 = M5 fixed-tf structure (v90)
string l0_currentPhase = l0_phaseCanon   // L0 = M5 fixed-tf lifecycle (v90)

// ── 12E: PREDICTION ENGINE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

float predScore_Expansion =
     (waveProgress < 35.0 ? (35.0 - waveProgress) * 1.00 : 0.0) +
     (expansionBelief > 55 ? expansionBelief * 0.30 : 0.0) +
     (convexityMaturity < 25 ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (posDistToCreation > 30 ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     (htfAlign == direction and direction != 0 ? 15.0 : 0.0)

float predScore_Convexity =
     (waveProgress >= 25.0 and waveProgress <= 60.0 ? 30.0 : 0.0) +
     (convexityMaturity > 20 ? convexityMaturity * 0.30 : 0.0) +
     (obs_DecayScore > 40 ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (m1ConvexityEmer ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     (preConvEvidence ? 15.0 : 0.0)

float predScore_Creation =
     (convexityMaturity > 55 ? (convexityMaturity - 55.0) * 1.20 : 0.0) +
     (posDistToCreation < 20.0 ? (20.0 - posDistToCreation) * 2.00 : 0.0) +
     (obs_LiquidityScore > 55 ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (liqSweepBull or liqSweepBear ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     (m1LiquidityEmer ? 10.0 : 0.0)

float predScore_Absorption =
     (predScore_Creation > 50 ? predScore_Creation * 0.40 : 0.0) +
     (obs_AbsorptionScore > 35 ? obs_AbsorptionScore * 0.30 : 0.0) +
     (m1AbsorptionEmer ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (waveProgress >= 60.0 and waveProgress <= 78.0 ? 15.0 : 0.0)

float predScore_Retracement =
     (absorptionBelief > 45 ? absorptionBelief * 0.35 : 0.0) +
     ((direction == 1 and bearMicroImpulse) or (direction == -1 and bullMicroImpulse) ? 25.0 : 0.0) +
     (waveProgress >= 72.0 and waveProgress <= 90.0 ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (physicsConsensus < 40 ? 10.0 : 0.0)

float predScore_DemandReturn =
     (retracementBelief > 45 ? retracementBelief * 0.35 : 0.0) +
     (posDistToDemand < 20.0 ? (20.0 - posDistToDemand) * 1.50 : 0.0) +
     (liqSweepBull or liqSweepBear ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (waveProgress >= 88.0 ? (waveProgress - 88.0) * 1.20 : 0.0)

float _maxPredScore = math.max(predScore_Expansion, predScore_Convexity, predScore_Creation,
                                predScore_Absorption, predScore_Retracement, predScore_DemandReturn)

string expectedNextPhase =
     predScore_DemandReturn >= predScore_Retracement and predScore_DemandReturn >= predScore_Absorption and
     predScore_DemandReturn >= predScore_Creation    and predScore_DemandReturn >= predScore_Convexity   and
     predScore_DemandReturn >= predScore_Expansion   ? (direction == -1 ? "Supply Return" : "Demand Return") :
     predScore_Retracement  >= predScore_Absorption  and predScore_Retracement >= predScore_Creation    and
     predScore_Retracement  >= predScore_Convexity   and predScore_Retracement >= predScore_Expansion   ? "Retracement"             :
     predScore_Absorption   >= predScore_Creation    and predScore_Absorption  >= predScore_Convexity   and
     predScore_Absorption   >= predScore_Expansion                                                       ? "Absorption"              :
     predScore_Creation     >= predScore_Convexity   and predScore_Creation    >= predScore_Expansion   ? (direction == -1 ? "New Low" : "New High") :
     predScore_Convexity    >= predScore_Expansion                                                       ? "Expansion Pre-Convexity" : "Expansion"

float expectedNextProb = _maxPredScore > 0 ? math.min(_maxPredScore / math.max(_maxPredScore + 30.0, 1.0) * 100.0, 95.0) : 50.0

// ── 12F: VALIDATION ENGINE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Tracks ENGINE 1A canonical phase transition accuracy.
// predTransition fires when IE1A transitions to a new canonical phase.
// predSucceeded when the new IE1A phase matches the previously predicted next phase.

var array<int> predOutcomes = array.new_int(100, 0)
var int        predTotalIdx = 0

var string lastExpectedPhase    = "Point 4 Origin"
var string lastIE1APhase        = "Point 4 Origin"

// Track IE1A phase transitions (not primaryHypothesis)
bool predTransition = ie1a_currentPhase != lastIE1APhase
bool predSucceeded  = predTransition and ie1a_currentPhase == lastExpectedPhase

if predTransition
    array.set(predOutcomes, predTotalIdx % 100, predSucceeded ? 1 : 0)
    predTotalIdx := predTotalIdx + 1

lastExpectedPhase := expectedNextPhase
lastIE1APhase     := ie1a_currentPhase

f_predAcc(int _n) =>
    int   _cnt = math.min(_n, predTotalIdx)
    int   _sum = 0
    int   _start = math.max(0, predTotalIdx - _cnt)
    if _cnt > 0
        for i = _start to predTotalIdx - 1
            _sum := _sum + array.get(predOutcomes, i % 100)
    _cnt > 0 ? _sum / float(_cnt) * 100.0 : 50.0

float predAcc10  = f_predAcc(10)
float predAcc25  = f_predAcc(25)
float predAcc50  = f_predAcc(50)
float predAcc100 = f_predAcc(100)
float predReliability = (predAcc10 * 0.4 + predAcc25 * 0.3 + predAcc50 * 0.2 + predAcc100 * 0.1)

// ── 12G: ADAPTIVE CONFIDENCE ENGINE ──────────────────────────────────────────

var float modelConfidence = 50.0

float confIncrease =
     (predSucceeded                                    ? 3.0  : 0.0) +
     (physicsConsensus > 70                            ? 2.0  : 0.0) +
     (htfAlign == direction and direction != 0         ? 1.5  : 0.0) +
     (dir_tf1 == dir_tf2 and dir_tf1 != 0             ? 1.0  : 0.0)

float confDecrease =
     (predTransition and not predSucceeded             ? 2.0  : 0.0) +
     (physicsDiff > 60                                 ? 2.0  : 0.0) +
     (htfAlign != direction and direction != 0         ? 1.5  : 0.0) +
     (dir_tf1 != dir_tf2 and dir_tf1 != 0 and dir_tf2 != 0 ? 1.0 : 0.0)

modelConfidence := math.max(10.0, math.min(100.0,
     modelConfidence + confIncrease - confDecrease - confDecayRate * (modelConfidence - 50.0)))

// ── 12H: WAVE DEVIATION ENGINE ────────────────────────────────────────────────

float idealExpansionSig  = efficiency
float idealConvSig       = obs_DecayScore / 100.0
float idealAbsSig        = obs_AbsorptionScore / 100.0

float waveDeviationRaw =
     math.abs(idealExpansionSig - (ie1a_hypFamily == "EXPANSION" ? 0.85 : 0.30)) * 40.0 +
     math.abs(idealConvSig      - (ie1a_hypFamily == "CONVEXITY FORMING" ? 0.70 : 0.20)) * 30.0 +
     math.abs(idealAbsSig       - (ie1a_hypFamily == "ABSORPTION" ? 0.70 : 0.15)) * 30.0

float waveDeviation = math.min(waveDeviationRaw * 100.0, 100.0)
bool deviationAlert = waveDeviation > devReinterpThresh

// ── 12I: M1 EARLY WARNING ENGINE ─────────────────────────────────────────────

f_m1Physics(float _c, float _h, float _l) =>
    float _v  = ta.ema(_c - _c[1], 3)
    float _a  = _v - _v[1]
    float _cv = _a - _a[1]
    float _m  = math.abs(_c - _c[effLen])
    float _ps = math.sum(math.abs(_c - _c[1]), effLen)
    float _e  = _ps > 0 ? _m / _ps : 0.0
    float _d  = (_h - _l) / math.max(ta.atr(atrLen), 1e-10)
    bool _mD  = math.abs(_a) < math.abs(_a[1]) * 0.8
    bool _expWeak  = _e < effThresh * 0.7 and _mD
    bool _convEmer = math.abs(_cv) > ta.atr(atrLen) * convMult * 1.5 and _mD
    bool _indEmer  = _e > effThresh and _a < 0 and _v > 0
    bool _liqEmer  = _d > dispThresh * 1.2 and _mD
    bool _absEmer  = _e < effThresh * 0.5 and _d < dispThresh * 0.6
    [_expWeak, _convEmer, _indEmer, _liqEmer, _absEmer]

[m1_expWeak, m1_convEmer, m1_indEmer, m1_liqEmer, m1_absEmer] = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("1"),
    f_m1Physics(close, high, low), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)

bool m1ExpansionWeak   = int(nz(int(m1_expWeak  ? 1 : 0), 0)) != 0
m1ConvexityEmer       := int(nz(int(m1_convEmer ? 1 : 0), 0)) != 0
bool m1InductionEmer   = int(nz(int(m1_indEmer  ? 1 : 0), 0)) != 0
m1LiquidityEmer       := int(nz(int(m1_liqEmer  ? 1 : 0), 0)) != 0
m1AbsorptionEmer      := int(nz(int(m1_absEmer  ? 1 : 0), 0)) != 0

int m1WarningScore =
     (m1ExpansionWeak  ? 1 : 0) +
     (m1ConvexityEmer  ? 1 : 0) +
     (m1InductionEmer  ? 1 : 0) +
     (m1LiquidityEmer  ? 1 : 0) +
     (m1AbsorptionEmer ? 1 : 0)

string m1Warning =
     m1WarningScore >= 4 ? "CRITICAL" :
     m1WarningScore >= 3 ? "HIGH"     :
     m1WarningScore >= 2 ? "MODERATE" :
     m1WarningScore >= 1 ? "LOW"      : "CLEAR"

// ── 12J: MULTI-TIMEFRAME BELIEF STACK ────────────────────────────────────────

float htf_ExpBelief  = math.min((expScr_tf2 * 0.5 + expScr_tf1 * 0.5), 100.0)
float htf_ConvBelief = math.min((decScr_tf2 * 0.4 + curvScr_tf2 * 0.3 + decScr_tf1 * 0.3), 100.0)
float htf_AbsBelief  = math.min((abScr_tf2  * 0.5 + abScr_tf1  * 0.5), 100.0)
float htf_LiqBelief  = math.min((liqScr_tf2 * 0.5 + liqScr_tf1 * 0.5), 100.0)

// htf_PrimaryInterp — DISPLAY ONLY: relays IE1A canonical phase for HTF context row.
// HTF belief scores (htf_ExpBelief etc.) remain available as confidence context metrics
// but do NOT independently assign a lifecycle phase.
string htf_PrimaryInterp = l0_phaseCanon   // L0 = M5 fixed-tf lifecycle (v90)

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 13 — WAVE SPAWN ENGINE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

f_spawnWave(int _newDir) =>
    float _obTop    = _newDir == 1 ? lastPivotPrice  : prevPivotPrice
    float _obBot    = _newDir == 1 ? prevPivotPrice  : lastPivotPrice
    int   _anchBar  = prevPivotBar
    float _fzIP     = f_findInducPrice(_anchBar, _obTop, _obBot, inducLookback)
    float _fzL      = not na(_fzIP) ? _fzIP - atr * inducZoneWidth : na
    float _fzH      = not na(_fzIP) ? _fzIP + atr * inducZoneWidth : na
    [_obTop, _obBot, _anchBar, _fzIP, _fzL, _fzH]

// v90: wave spawn is governed by the FIXED M5 (L0) structure engine — NOT chart
// impulses/CHoCH — so `direction` (and every execution / FRZ output derived from
// it) is timeframe-independent. The spawn fires when the M5 structure flips.
bool _allowSpawn = l0_dir != 0 and l0_dir != direction

if _allowSpawn
    int _newDir = l0_dir
    [_obTop, _obBot, _anchBar, _fzIP, _fzL, _fzH] = f_spawnWave(_newDir)
    _obTop := nz(l0_p4High, _obTop)
    _obBot := nz(l0_p4Low, _obBot)

    lastSpawnDir       := _newDir
    direction          := _newDir
    flipTop            := _obTop
    flipBot            := _obBot
    barsInZone         := 0
    obBirthBar         := bar_index
    contBar            := na

    point4OriginHigh   := _obTop
    point4OriginLow    := _obBot
    point4OriginBar    := bar_index

    flipzoneInducPrice := _fzIP
    flipzoneInducLow   := _fzL
    flipzoneInducHigh  := _fzH

    inducExpOriginHigh       := na
    inducExpExtremeLow       := na
    inducExpOriginLow        := na
    inducExpExtremeHigh      := na
    inducRetrOriginHigh      := na
    inducRetrExtremeLow      := na
    inducRetrOriginLow       := na
    inducRetrExtremeHigh     := na
    inducZoneLow             := na
    inducZoneHigh            := na
    cycleHigh                := high
    cycleLow                 := low
    isRecursiveWave          := false
    entryCycle               := 0
    waveDepth                := 0

    // Entry-cycle label for the PRIMARY wave (DIE-8 only labels recursive cycles).
    // Gated by the "Show Wave Intelligence Labels" setting so it always appears
    // for a new wave regardless of Display Mode.
    if showLabels
        label.new(bar_index, _newDir == 1 ? low - atr * 0.4 : high + atr * 0.4,
             _newDir == 1 ? "EC▲" : "EC▼",
             style=_newDir == 1 ? label.style_label_up : label.style_label_down,
             textcolor=_newDir == 1 ? color.lime : color.red, color=color.new(color.black, 100), size=size.tiny)

    if not na(p4Box)
        box.delete(p4Box)
    if showP4Box
        p4Box := box.new(left=_anchBar, top=_obTop, right=bar_index + 300, bottom=_obBot,
             bgcolor=f_zoneFill(color.new(color.orange, 92)),
             border_color=color.new(color.orange, 40),
             border_style=line.style_dotted, border_width=2)
    if not na(p4LineTop)
        line.delete(p4LineTop)
    if not na(p4LineBot)
        line.delete(p4LineBot)
    if showP4Box
        p4LineTop := line.new(x1=_anchBar, y1=_obTop, x2=bar_index + 300, y2=_obTop,
             color=color.new(color.orange, 20), style=line.style_dotted, width=1)
        p4LineBot := line.new(x1=_anchBar, y1=_obBot, x2=bar_index + 300, y2=_obBot,
             color=color.new(color.orange, 20), style=line.style_dotted, width=1)

    // Supply/Demand zone boxes removed — replaced by the clean, persistent
    // Primary-Attractor entry zone (see "High-Probability Entry Zone" below).
    // Delete any legacy S/D boxes so toggling no longer leaves them on chart.
    if not na(demandBox)
        box.delete(demandBox)
        demandBox := na
    if not na(supplyBox)
        box.delete(supplyBox)
        supplyBox := na

    // DIE: POINT 4 ORIGIN label — only render at Priority 90 (not in High density execution mode)
    // In High density Execution mode this is suppressed; medium/low density shows it.
    bool _die_p4_show = displayMode == "Research" or displayMode == "Context"
    if showLabels and entryCycle == 0 and _die_p4_show and ecvShow_Origin
        label.new(bar_index, _newDir == 1 ? low - atr * 0.5 : high + atr * 0.5,
             "POINT 4 ORIGIN",
             style=_newDir == 1 ? label.style_label_up : label.style_label_down,
             textcolor=color.black, color=color.new(color.orange, 30), size=size.tiny)

    bool _originLabelOK = displayMode == "Research" or displayMode == "Context"
    if showOriginShort and _newDir == -1 and _originLabelOK and ecvShow_Origin
        label.new(_anchBar, _obTop + atr * 0.1, "Origin S",
             style=label.style_label_down, textcolor=color.new(color.red, 0),
             color=color.new(color.red, 85), size=size.tiny)
    if showOriginLong and _newDir == 1 and _originLabelOK and ecvShow_Origin
        label.new(_anchBar, _obBot - atr * 0.1, "Origin L",
             style=label.style_label_up, textcolor=color.new(color.teal, 0),
             color=color.new(color.teal, 85), size=size.tiny)

    if not na(flipBox)
        box.delete(flipBox)
    // Flip-zone box kept as an invisible object for downstream structure logic
    // (its green fill was removed for a cleaner chart).
    flipBox := box.new(left=_anchBar, top=flipTop, right=bar_index + 300, bottom=flipBot,
         bgcolor=color.new(color.black, 100), border_color=color.new(color.black, 100), border_width=1)

if direction == 1 and high > nz(cycleHigh, high)
    cycleHigh := high
if direction == -1 and low < nz(cycleLow, low)
    cycleLow := low

bool expInducBuyEv  = direction == 1  and bearImpulse and structBias ==  1
bool expInducSellEv = direction == -1 and bullImpulse and structBias == -1

if expInducBuyEv and na(inducExpOriginHigh)
    inducExpOriginHigh := nz(point4OriginHigh, nz(cycleHigh, high))
    inducExpExtremeLow := low
    inducZoneLow       := nz(point4OriginHigh, low) - atr * inducZoneWidth
    inducZoneHigh      := nz(point4OriginHigh, low) + atr * inducZoneWidth

if expInducSellEv and na(inducExpOriginLow)
    inducExpOriginLow    := nz(point4OriginLow, nz(cycleLow, low))
    inducExpExtremeHigh  := high
    inducZoneLow         := nz(point4OriginLow, high) - atr * inducZoneWidth
    inducZoneHigh        := nz(point4OriginLow, high) + atr * inducZoneWidth

if not na(inducExpExtremeLow) and direction == 1 and low < inducExpExtremeLow
    inducExpExtremeLow := low
    inducZoneLow       := low - atr * inducZoneWidth
    inducZoneHigh      := low + atr * inducZoneWidth

if not na(inducExpExtremeHigh) and direction == -1 and high > inducExpExtremeHigh
    inducExpExtremeHigh := high
    inducZoneLow        := high - atr * inducZoneWidth
    inducZoneHigh       := high + atr * inducZoneWidth

nearFlipzone := not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot) and
     close <= flipTop * 1.02 and close >= flipBot * 0.98

bool retrInducBuyEv  = direction == 1  and bullImpulse and structBias == -1 and nearFlipzone
bool retrInducSellEv = direction == -1 and bearImpulse and structBias ==  1 and nearFlipzone

if retrInducBuyEv and na(inducRetrOriginLow)
    inducRetrOriginLow   := nz(cycleLow, low)
    inducRetrExtremeHigh := high
    inducZoneLow         := high - atr * inducZoneWidth
    inducZoneHigh        := high + atr * inducZoneWidth

if retrInducSellEv and na(inducRetrOriginHigh)
    inducRetrOriginHigh := nz(cycleHigh, high)
    inducRetrExtremeLow := low
    inducZoneLow        := low - atr * inducZoneWidth
    inducZoneHigh       := low + atr * inducZoneWidth

if not na(inducRetrExtremeHigh) and direction == 1 and high > inducRetrExtremeHigh
    inducRetrExtremeHigh := high
    inducZoneLow         := high - atr * inducZoneWidth
    inducZoneHigh        := high + atr * inducZoneWidth

if not na(inducRetrExtremeLow) and direction == -1 and low < inducRetrExtremeLow
    inducRetrExtremeLow  := low
    inducZoneLow         := low - atr * inducZoneWidth
    inducZoneHigh        := low + atr * inducZoneWidth

closeInside          := not na(flipTop) and close <= flipTop and close >= flipBot
bool priceInDemand   = not na(flipBot) and low < flipBot and
     (not na(point4OriginHigh) and low <= point4OriginHigh)
bool priceInSupply   = not na(flipTop) and high > flipTop and
     (not na(point4OriginLow)  and high >= point4OriginLow)

bool trueCHoCH_bull  = direction ==  1 and priceInDemand and bullImpulse and liqSweepOK
bool trueCHoCH_bear  = direction == -1 and priceInSupply and bearImpulse and liqSweepOK
bool structFlipBull  = direction ==  1 and bullConvShift and structBias == -1
bool structFlipBear  = direction == -1 and bearConvShift and structBias ==  1

bool recursiveTrigger = (trueCHoCH_bull or trueCHoCH_bear or structFlipBull or structFlipBear) and
     (ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return") and
     demandReturnBelief > 40 and direction != 0 and not na(flipTop)

var bool recursiveJustFired = false
var int  recursiveFiredBar  = na

if recursiveTrigger and (na(recursiveFiredBar) or (bar_index - recursiveFiredBar) > resetBars)
    recursiveJustFired := true
    recursiveFiredBar  := bar_index
    recursiveComplete  := true
else
    recursiveJustFired := false

if recursiveJustFired
    f_storeCycleState(math.max(entryCycle, 1), flipTop, flipBot, flipTop, flipBot,
         point4OriginHigh, point4OriginLow, point4OriginBar, direction)

    waveGeneration  := waveGeneration + 1
    entryCycle      := math.min(entryCycle + 1, 4)
    isRecursiveWave := true
    waveDepth       := entryCycle

    int _nextDir = l0_dir != 0 ? l0_dir : ((bullImpulse or bullConvShift) ? 1 : -1)
    [_obTop2, _obBot2, _anchBar2, _fzIP2, _fzL2, _fzH2] = f_spawnWave(_nextDir)

    lastSpawnDir       := _nextDir
    direction          := l0_dir != 0 ? l0_dir : _nextDir
    flipTop            := _obTop2
    flipBot            := _obBot2
    barsInZone         := 0
    obBirthBar         := bar_index

    point4OriginHigh   := _obTop2
    point4OriginLow    := _obBot2
    point4OriginBar    := bar_index

    flipzoneInducPrice := _fzIP2
    flipzoneInducLow   := _fzL2
    flipzoneInducHigh  := _fzH2

    inducExpOriginHigh     := na
    inducExpExtremeLow     := na
    inducExpOriginLow      := na
    inducExpExtremeHigh    := na
    inducRetrOriginHigh    := na
    inducRetrExtremeLow    := na
    inducRetrOriginLow     := na
    inducRetrExtremeHigh   := na
    inducZoneLow           := na
    inducZoneHigh          := na
    cycleHigh              := high
    cycleLow               := low
    contBar                := bar_index

    if not na(p4Box)
        box.delete(p4Box)
    if showP4Box
        p4Box := box.new(left=_anchBar2, top=_obTop2, right=bar_index + 300, bottom=_obBot2,
             bgcolor=f_zoneFill(color.new(color.orange, 92)),
             border_color=color.new(color.orange, 40),
             border_style=line.style_dotted, border_width=2)
    if not na(p4LineTop)
        line.delete(p4LineTop)
    if not na(p4LineBot)
        line.delete(p4LineBot)
    if showP4Box
        p4LineTop := line.new(x1=_anchBar2, y1=_obTop2, x2=bar_index + 300, y2=_obTop2,
             color=color.new(color.orange, 20), style=line.style_dotted, width=1)
        p4LineBot := line.new(x1=_anchBar2, y1=_obBot2, x2=bar_index + 300, y2=_obBot2,
             color=color.new(color.orange, 20), style=line.style_dotted, width=1)

    // Supply/Demand zone boxes removed (replaced by the clean Primary-Attractor
    // entry zone). Delete any legacy boxes so toggling no longer leaves them.
    if not na(demandBox)
        box.delete(demandBox)
        demandBox := na
    if not na(supplyBox)
        box.delete(supplyBox)
        supplyBox := na

    // DIE: Entry Cycle label now rendered by Display Intelligence Engine (DIE-8)
    // Original label suppressed here — size-scaled, quality-scored label fires in DIE-8
    // if showLabels
    //     label.new(bar_index, _nextDir == 1 ? low - atr * 0.5 : high + atr * 0.5,
    //          "ENTRY CYCLE " + str.tostring(entryCycle),
    //          style=_nextDir == 1 ? label.style_label_up : label.style_label_down,
    //          textcolor=color.black, color=color.new(#00ff88, 30), size=size.tiny)

    if not na(flipBox)
        box.delete(flipBox)
    flipBox := box.new(left=_anchBar2, top=flipTop, right=bar_index + 300, bottom=flipBot,
         bgcolor=color.new(color.black, 100), border_color=color.new(color.black, 100), border_width=1)

var float retestHigh = na
var float retestLow  = na

// IE1A authority: gate on canonical Demand Return / Supply Return phases
if ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return"
    barsInZone := closeInside ? barsInZone + 1 : 0
    if barsInZone >= acceptBars
        retestHigh := _g_highestAB
        retestLow  := _g_lowestAB

int  barsSinceCont = not na(contBar) ? bar_index - contBar : (not na(obBirthBar) ? bar_index - obBirthBar : 0)
bool bullInvalid   = direction ==  1 and close < flipBot - atr * 0.5
bool bearInvalid   = direction == -1 and close > flipTop + atr * 0.5
bool opposingMove  = (direction ==  1 and bearImpulse) or (direction == -1 and bullImpulse)
// Hard structural invalidation (wave origin broken) ALWAYS resets — a structurally
// dead wave must not persist as the active direction, regardless of ERF dissipation
// suppression. The softer rotation-based reset keeps its existing gates.
bool hardInvalid   = bullInvalid or bearInvalid
bool softReset     = barsSinceCont > resetBars and opposingMove and
     (ie1a_currentPhase != "Demand Return" and ie1a_currentPhase != "Supply Return") and
     demandReturnBelief < 30 and expansionBelief < 30 and
     not erf_suppressRotation
bool safeToReset   = hardInvalid or softReset

// v90: direction is governed by the M5 engine, so the chart-based reset to
// "Point 4 Origin" (direction 0) no longer fires (direction always tracks l0_dir).
if direction != l0_dir and safeToReset
    direction              := 0
    lastSpawnDir           := 0
    flipTop                := na
    flipBot                := na
    contBar                := na
    obBirthBar             := na
    barsInZone             := 0
    isRecursiveWave        := false
    entryCycle             := 0
    waveDepth              := 0
    recursiveComplete      := false
    if not na(flipBox)
        box.delete(flipBox)
        flipBox := na
    if not na(p4Box)
        box.delete(p4Box)
        p4Box := na
    if not na(p4LineTop)
        line.delete(p4LineTop)
        p4LineTop := na
    if not na(p4LineBot)
        line.delete(p4LineBot)
        p4LineBot := na
    if not na(demandBox)
        box.delete(demandBox)
        demandBox := na
    if not na(supplyBox)
        box.delete(supplyBox)
        supplyBox := na

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 14 — INDUCTION ZONE CLASSIFICATION
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

bool inRetracementInducZone = not na(pivL) and not na(inducZoneLow) and not na(inducZoneHigh) and
     direction ==  1 and pivL >= inducZoneLow and pivL <= inducZoneHigh and retrInducBuyEv

bool inShortRetrInducZone = not na(pivH) and not na(inducZoneLow) and not na(inducZoneHigh) and
     direction == -1 and pivH >= inducZoneLow and pivH <= inducZoneHigh and retrInducSellEv

bool inExpansionInducZone = not na(pivH) and not na(inducZoneLow) and not na(inducZoneHigh) and
     direction ==  1 and pivH >= inducZoneLow and pivH <= inducZoneHigh and expInducBuyEv

bool inShortExpInducZone = not na(pivL) and not na(inducZoneLow) and not na(inducZoneHigh) and
     direction == -1 and pivL >= inducZoneLow and pivL <= inducZoneHigh and expInducSellEv

float inducConfidence = 0.0
if direction ==  1 and inRetracementInducZone
    inducConfidence := 1.0
else if direction ==  1 and not na(pivL) and not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot) and
     pivL < flipTop and pivL > flipBot and not inRetracementInducZone
    inducConfidence := -0.5
else if direction == -1 and inShortRetrInducZone
    inducConfidence := 1.0
else if direction == -1 and not na(pivH) and not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot) and
     pivH > flipBot and pivH < flipTop and not inShortRetrInducZone
    inducConfidence := -0.5

if showInducLabels and ecvShow_Induction and not na(pivH) and not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot) and
     pivH > flipBot and pivH < flipTop and direction == -1 and
     (retrInducSellEv or nearFlipzone)
    label.new(bar_index, high + atr * 0.25,
         inShortRetrInducZone ? "Retracement Induction ✓" : "False CHoCH",
         style=label.style_label_down,
         textcolor=inShortRetrInducZone ? color.lime : color.red,
         color=color.new(color.white, 92), size=size.tiny)

if showInducLabels and ecvShow_Induction and not na(pivL) and not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot) and
     pivL < flipTop and pivL > flipBot and direction == 1 and
     (retrInducBuyEv or nearFlipzone)
    label.new(bar_index, low - atr * 0.25,
         inRetracementInducZone ? "Retracement Induction ✓" : "False CHoCH",
         style=label.style_label_up,
         textcolor=inRetracementInducZone ? color.lime : color.red,
         color=color.new(color.white, 92), size=size.tiny)

bool expansionPreConvSeen     = preConvEvidence and obs_DecayScore > 30
bool expansionInductionConf   = inductionEvidence
bool retracementPreConvSeen   = nearFlipzone and (bullMomDecay or bearMomDecay)
bool retracementInductionConf = inRetracementInducZone or inShortRetrInducZone
bool expConvFormationActive   = convexityBelief > 40 and expansionBelief > 30
bool retrConvFormationActive  = convexityBelief > 40 and retracementBelief > 40
bool convexityComplete        = creationBelief > 50 or absorptionBelief > 40

int flipzoneStagesComplete =
     demandReturnBelief > 75 and recursiveComplete ? 5 :
     demandReturnBelief > 60 ? 4 :
     retracementBelief  > 55 ? 3 :
     retracementInductionConf ? 2 :
     retracementPreConvSeen   ? 1 : 0

float flipzoneScore = flipzoneStagesComplete / 5.0 * 100.0

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 15 — SCORING ENGINE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

float poiMid   = not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot) ? (flipTop + flipBot) / 2.0 : na
float energy   = not na(poiMid) ? math.abs(close - poiMid) / math.max(atr, 1e-10) : 0.0

float sStruct  = flipzoneScore * 0.30
float sConv    = math.min(math.abs(convSmooth) / math.max(atr * convMult, 1e-10) * 25.0, 25.0)
float sEnergy  = math.min(energy * 10.0, 20.0)
float sEff     = efficiency * 15.0
float sVol     = math.min((atr / math.max(close, 1e-10)) * 1000.0, 10.0)
float contProb = math.min(sStruct + sConv + sEnergy + sEff + sVol, 100.0)

string grade    = contProb > 90 ? "A+" : contProb > 80 ? "A" : contProb > 70 ? "B" : contProb > 60 ? "C" : "D"
color  gradeCol = grade == "A+" ? #00ff88 : grade == "A" ? color.lime : grade == "B" ? color.yellow : grade == "C" ? color.orange : color.red

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 16 — BAYESIAN PROBABILISTIC MODEL
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

float bayesStruct   = structBias == liveWaveDir ? 0.90 : structBias == 0 ? 0.50 : 0.15
float bayesMomentum = (liveWaveDir ==  1 and velocity > 0 and acceleration > 0) ? 0.85 :
                      (liveWaveDir == -1 and velocity < 0 and acceleration < 0) ? 0.85 :
                      (liveWaveDir ==  1 and velocity > 0) or
                      (liveWaveDir == -1 and velocity < 0) ? 0.60 : 0.30
float bayesLiq      = liqHeat > 70 ? 0.80 : liqHeat > 30 ? 0.55 : 0.35
float bayesHTF      = liveHtfAlign == liveWaveDir and liveHtfAlign != 0 ? 0.90 : liveHtfAlign == 0 ? 0.55 : 0.20
float bayesDisp     = displacement > dispThresh * 1.5 ? 0.85 : displacement > dispThresh ? 0.65 : 0.35
float bayesOB       = obFreshness > 0.7 ? 0.80 : obFreshness > 0.4 ? 0.60 : 0.35
float bayesInduc    = inducConfidence > 0 ? 0.90 : inducConfidence < 0 ? 0.20 : 0.50
float bayesFlipzone = flipzoneStagesComplete >= 4 ? 0.92 :
                      flipzoneStagesComplete >= 3 ? 0.75 :
                      flipzoneStagesComplete >= 2 ? 0.58 :
                      flipzoneStagesComplete >= 1 ? 0.42 : 0.25

float w1 = 0.15
float w2 = 0.14
float w3 = 0.10
float w4 = 0.14
float w5 = 0.11
float w6 = 0.07
float w7 = 0.12
float w8 = 0.17

float logOdds =
     w1 * math.log(math.max(bayesStruct,   1e-10) / math.max(1.0 - bayesStruct,   1e-10)) +
     w2 * math.log(math.max(bayesMomentum, 1e-10) / math.max(1.0 - bayesMomentum, 1e-10)) +
     w3 * math.log(math.max(bayesLiq,      1e-10) / math.max(1.0 - bayesLiq,      1e-10)) +
     w4 * math.log(math.max(bayesHTF,      1e-10) / math.max(1.0 - bayesHTF,      1e-10)) +
     w5 * math.log(math.max(bayesDisp,     1e-10) / math.max(1.0 - bayesDisp,     1e-10)) +
     w6 * math.log(math.max(bayesOB,       1e-10) / math.max(1.0 - bayesOB,       1e-10)) +
     w7 * math.log(math.max(bayesInduc,    1e-10) / math.max(1.0 - bayesInduc,    1e-10)) +
     w8 * math.log(math.max(bayesFlipzone, 1e-10) / math.max(1.0 - bayesFlipzone, 1e-10))

float finalProb = 1.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-logOdds)) * 100.0

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 17 — PROBABILITY PANELS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

float velDecay = phys_vd70 ? 1.0 : 0.0

float expansionProbability = math.min(
     (not bullInvalid and not bearInvalid ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (convexityComplete                  ? 20.0 : convexityScore * 0.4) +
     (recursiveComplete                  ? 15.0 : flipzoneStagesComplete * 3.0) +
     (liveHtfAlign == liveWaveDir and liveHtfAlign != 0 ? 25.0 : liveHtfAlign == 0 ? 12.5 : 0.0) +
     (liqHeat > 50                       ? 20.0 : liqHeat * 0.4),
     100.0)

float reversalProbability = math.min(
     (convexityScore > 70             ? 25.0 : convexityScore * 0.35) +
     (retracementInductionConf        ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (liqHeat > 70                    ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (velDecay * 20.0) +
     (liveHtfAlign != liveWaveDir and liveHtfAlign != 0 ? 15.0 : 0.0),
     100.0)

float tradeReadiness = math.min(
     (liveWaveDir != 0                    ? 10.0 : 0.0) +
     (flipzoneStagesComplete >= 3        ? 15.0 : flipzoneStagesComplete * 5.0) +
     (velocityScore * 0.10) +
     (expansionScore * 0.10) +
     (liqHeat < 50                       ? 10.0 : liqHeat > 70 ? -5.0 : 0.0) +
     (liveHtfAlign == liveWaveDir and liveHtfAlign != 0 ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     (expansionProbability * 0.20) +
     (bayesFlipzone * 3.0),
     100.0)

f_scoreColor(float v) =>
    v >= 85 ? #00ff88 : v >= 70 ? color.lime : v >= 40 ? color.yellow : color.red

f_scoreLabel(float v) =>
    v >= 85 ? "Exceptional" : v >= 70 ? "Strong" : v >= 40 ? "Neutral" : "Weak"

// ─── SECTION 6 / 15 — DIRECTION OWNERSHIP HELPERS ─────────────────────────────
// Every wave-state display must explicitly identify Buyers (Bull) or Sellers
// (Bear). Uses ONLY the existing `direction`, `dir_tf1`, `dir_tf2` bias
// variables — no new directional calculations are introduced.
//
// Mapping (per spec Section 6):
//   Expansion       -> Bull/Bear Expansion
//   Absorption      -> Bull/Bear Absorption
//   Pre-Convexity   -> Bull/Bear Pre-Convexity
//   Convexity       -> Bull/Bear Convexity
//   Demand Return   -> Bull Demand Return
//   Supply Return   -> Bear Supply Return
//   (all other state names pass through unchanged)
f_dirOwner(int dir) =>
    dir == 1 ? "Bull" : dir == -1 ? "Bear" : "Neutral"

f_applyDirection(string phase, int dir) =>
    string _own = f_dirOwner(dir)
    string _out = phase
    if phase == "Expansion" or phase == "EXPANSION"
        _out := _own + " Expansion"
    else if phase == "Absorption" or phase == "ABSORPTION"
        _out := _own + " Absorption"
    else if phase == "Pre-Convexity"
        _out := _own + " Pre-Convexity"
    else if phase == "Demand Return" or phase == "DEMAND/SUPPLY RETURN"
        _out := dir == -1 ? "Bear Supply Return" : "Bull Demand Return"
    else if phase == "Supply Return"
        _out := "Bear Supply Return"
    else if phase == "Convexity" or phase == "CONVEXITY FORMING"
        _out := _own + " Convexity"
    _out

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 18 — SLIPPAGE & TRADE OPPORTUNITY ENGINE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

float spreadEstimate   = atr * 0.05
float volatilityFactor = volRatio * 0.10
float slippageCost     = atr * volatilityFactor + spreadEstimate
float liqDepthPenalty  = liqHeat > 70 ? atr * 0.05 : 0.0
float totalSlippage    = slippageCost + liqDepthPenalty

float baseTrend     = efficiency * 30
float impulseScore  = displacement > dispThresh ? 20 : 0
float momentum      = phys_mom
float momentumScore = momentum > 0 ? 10 : -10
float accelScore    = acceleration > 0 ? 10 : -10
float structScore   = structBias == 1 ? 20 : structBias == -1 ? -20 : 0
float htfScore      = htfAlign == 1 ? 20 : htfAlign == -1 ? -20 : 0
float liqScore      = wDensity < 0.5 ? 10 : -5
float zoneScore     = closeInside ? 15 : 0
float inducScore    = inducConfidence > 0 ? 10 : inducConfidence < 0 ? -10 : 0
float fzStageScore  = flipzoneStagesComplete * 6.0
float beliefBonus   = (direction == 1  and demandReturnBelief > 60) ? demandReturnBelief * 0.10 :
                      (direction == -1 and demandReturnBelief > 60) ? demandReturnBelief * 0.10 : 0.0
float confMult      = math.max(0.7, math.min(modelConfidence / 100.0 * 1.3, 1.3))

float buyScore =
     (baseTrend + impulseScore +
     math.max(momentumScore, 0) + math.max(accelScore, 0) +
     math.max(structScore, 0)   + math.max(htfScore, 0) +
     liqScore + zoneScore + math.max(inducScore, 0) + fzStageScore + beliefBonus +
     (fractalStackDir == 1 ? fractalCtxScore * 0.30 : 0.0)) * confMult

float sellScore =
     (baseTrend + impulseScore +
     math.max(-momentumScore, 0) + math.max(-accelScore, 0) +
     math.max(-structScore, 0)   + math.max(-htfScore, 0) +
     liqScore + zoneScore + math.max(-inducScore, 0) + fzStageScore + beliefBonus +
     (fractalStackDir == -1 ? fractalCtxScore * 0.30 : 0.0)) * confMult

float netEdge         = buyScore - sellScore
float netEdgeAdjusted = netEdge - (totalSlippage / math.max(atr, 1e-10) * 10.0)
bool  edgePassesFilter = math.abs(netEdgeAdjusted) > execThreshold

float BUY_SELL_SCORE_MAX = 279.5  // theoretical max incl. confMult<=1.3 and fractal-stack bonus (v90)
float buyProb  = math.min(math.max(buyScore  / BUY_SELL_SCORE_MAX * 100.0, 0.0), 100.0)
float sellProb = math.min(math.max(sellScore / BUY_SELL_SCORE_MAX * 100.0, 0.0), 100.0)

string liveDirective =
     netEdgeAdjusted > 25  ? "BUY PRESSURE"   :
     netEdgeAdjusted > 10  ? "BULLISH BIAS"   :
     netEdgeAdjusted < -25 ? "SELL PRESSURE"  :
     netEdgeAdjusted < -10 ? "BEARISH BIAS"   : "NEUTRAL / WAIT"

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 19 — HTF ALIGNMENT GATE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

bool htfAligned = direction != 0 and (htfAlign == direction or htfAlign == 0)
int resonance = htfAligned ? 2 : 1

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 20 — ADAPTIVE EXECUTION LOCK
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

var int  lastSignalBar = na
var int  lastLongBar   = na
var int  lastShortBar  = na
var bool engineArmed   = true

int dynamicLockBars = math.round(baseLockBars * volMult)

bool inducRearmLong  = direction ==  1 and inRetracementInducZone
bool inducRearmShort = direction == -1 and inShortRetrInducZone

if recursiveJustFired
    engineArmed := true
if inducRearmLong or inducRearmShort
    engineArmed := true

bool withinGlobalLock = not na(lastSignalBar) and (bar_index - lastSignalBar) < dynamicLockBars
bool withinLongLock   = not na(lastLongBar)   and (bar_index - lastLongBar)   < dynamicLockBars
bool withinShortLock  = not na(lastShortBar)  and (bar_index - lastShortBar)  < dynamicLockBars
bool signalLocked     = withinGlobalLock and not engineArmed

bool htfLongOK  = not requireHTFAlign or (htfBias1 >= 0 and htfBias2 >= 0)
bool htfShortOK = not requireHTFAlign or (htfBias1 <= 0 and htfBias2 <= 0)

bool preConvOK_long  = not requirePreConv   or retracementPreConvSeen
bool preConvOK_short = not requirePreConv   or retracementPreConvSeen
bool inducOK_long    = not requireInduction or retracementInductionConf
bool inducOK_short   = not requireInduction or retracementInductionConf

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 21 — ENTRY SIGNALS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

bool gradeOK = useStrictStructure ?
     (grade == "A+" or grade == "A" or grade == "B") :
     (grade == "A+" or grade == "A" or grade == "B" or grade == "C")

// Entry signals gate on IE1A canonical phase (Engine 1A is sole lifecycle authority).
// beliefEntryLong/Short additionally require the IE1A Demand Return / Supply Return phase
// to be confirmed, ensuring belief scores serve as confidence context only.
bool beliefEntryLong  = direction == 1  and
     (ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return") and
     demandReturnBelief > 50 and
     expansionBelief < 60 and absorptionBelief > 25
bool beliefEntryShort = direction == -1 and
     (ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return") and
     demandReturnBelief > 50 and
     expansionBelief < 60 and absorptionBelief > 25

bool longSignal = showSignals and beliefEntryLong and
     htfAligned and gradeOK and
     not signalLocked and not withinLongLock and
     edgePassesFilter and
     preConvOK_long and inducOK_long and
     structLongOK and liqSweepOK and obFresh and htfLongOK and
     erf_entryGate

bool shortSignal = showSignals and beliefEntryShort and
     htfAligned and gradeOK and
     not signalLocked and not withinShortLock and
     edgePassesFilter and
     preConvOK_short and inducOK_short and
     structShortOK and liqSweepOK and obFresh and htfShortOK and
     erf_entryGate

if longSignal
    lastSignalBar := bar_index
    lastLongBar   := bar_index
    engineArmed   := false

if shortSignal
    lastSignalBar := bar_index
    lastShortBar  := bar_index
    engineArmed   := false

plotshape(longSignal,  "Long Entry",  shape.triangleup,   location.belowbar, color.teal, size=size.normal)
plotshape(shortSignal, "Short Entry", shape.triangledown, location.abovebar, color.red,  size=size.normal)

if longSignal or shortSignal
    label.new(
         bar_index,
         longSignal ? low - atr * 0.7 : high + atr * 0.7,
         grade + " | " + str.tostring(math.round(finalProb)) + "%",
         style     = longSignal ? label.style_label_up : label.style_label_down,
         color     = gradeCol,
         textcolor = color.black,
         size      = size.small)

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 22 — WAVE INTELLIGENCE LABELS ON CHART
// Priority 80 — Market Context. Gated by DIE density. Narrative Engine (DIE-6)
// renders the single active narrative instead of stacking these.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// NOTE (v21): the legacy "hypothesis label" block was REMOVED. It was a SECOND
// on-chart phase-label authority that (a) only rendered in Context/Research mode,
// (b) spawned a fresh event label on every canonical-phase change (flood), and
// (c) coloured Expansion Pre-Convexity, Expansion Induction AND Expansion
// Liquidity the SAME purple (#c084fc) while labelling them with l0_currentPhase
// — so two different phases showed as near-identical purple "...Liquidity"
// labels. The single live region label (die_regionLbl, Engine-1A authority) is
// now the sole on-chart phase display and renders in every display mode.

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 23 — INDUCEMENT ZONE BANDS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

float shortBandLow  = direction == -1 ? inducZoneLow  : na
float shortBandHigh = direction == -1 ? inducZoneHigh : na
float longBandLow   = direction ==  1 ? inducZoneLow  : na
float longBandHigh  = direction ==  1 ? inducZoneHigh : na

sIndL = plot(showInducZone ? shortBandLow  : na, "Short Induc Low",  color=color.new(color.red,  75), linewidth=1)
sIndH = plot(showInducZone ? shortBandHigh : na, "Short Induc High", color=color.new(color.red,  75), linewidth=1)
lIndL = plot(showInducZone ? longBandLow   : na, "Long Induc Low",   color=color.new(color.teal, 75), linewidth=1)
lIndH = plot(showInducZone ? longBandHigh  : na, "Long Induc High",  color=color.new(color.teal, 75), linewidth=1)

fill(sIndL, sIndH, color=color.new(color.red,  88))
fill(lIndL, lIndH, color=color.new(color.teal, 88))

float fzInducPlotLow  = not na(flipzoneInducLow)  ? flipzoneInducLow  : na
float fzInducPlotHigh = not na(flipzoneInducHigh) ? flipzoneInducHigh : na

fzL = plot(showInducZone ? fzInducPlotLow  : na, "FZ Trap Low",  color=color.new(color.purple, 65), linewidth=1, style=plot.style_circles)
fzH = plot(showInducZone ? fzInducPlotHigh : na, "FZ Trap High", color=color.new(color.purple, 65), linewidth=1, style=plot.style_circles)
fill(fzL, fzH, color=color.new(color.purple, 92))

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 24 — TRADE STATE ENGINE
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

var int tradeDir = 0
var int exitFiredBar = na

bool exitCondition =
     (tradeDir ==  1 and bearBOS) or
     (tradeDir == -1 and bullBOS) or
     (tradeDir ==  1 and bearConvShift and energy < energy[1]) or
     (tradeDir == -1 and bullConvShift and energy < energy[1]) or
     (tradeDir ==  1 and htfAlign == -1) or
     (tradeDir == -1 and htfAlign ==  1) or
     (tradeDir != 0  and not obFresh) or
     (tradeDir != 0  and safeToReset) or
     (tradeDir ==  1 and bullInvalid) or
     (tradeDir == -1 and bearInvalid) or
     // IE1A phase gate: exit when IE1A transitions to Absorption or Retracement
     (tradeDir ==  1 and (ie1a_currentPhase == "Absorption" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement")) or
     (tradeDir == -1 and (ie1a_currentPhase == "Absorption" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement"))

if longSignal
    tradeDir     := 1
    exitFiredBar := na
else if shortSignal
    tradeDir     := -1
    exitFiredBar := na
else if exitCondition and tradeDir != 0
    exitFiredBar := bar_index
    tradeDir     := 0

bool exitLatchActive = not na(exitFiredBar) and (bar_index - exitFiredBar) < 3

string directiveStr =
     longSignal                        ? "BUY  (ENTER LONG)"    :
     shortSignal                       ? "SELL  (ENTER SHORT)"  :
     exitLatchActive                   ? "EXIT NOW"             :
     tradeDir ==  1                    ? "HOLD LONG"            :
     tradeDir == -1                    ? "HOLD SHORT"           : "NO TRADE / STAND DOWN"

color directiveCol =
     longSignal                        ? #00ff88      :
     shortSignal                       ? #ff1744      :
     exitLatchActive                   ? color.orange :
     tradeDir ==  1                    ? color.lime   :
     tradeDir == -1                    ? color.red    : color.gray

color directiveBg =
     longSignal                        ? color.new(#00ff88,     75) :
     shortSignal                       ? color.new(#ff1744,     75) :
     exitLatchActive                   ? color.new(color.orange,75) :
     tradeDir ==  1                    ? color.new(color.lime,  85) :
     tradeDir == -1                    ? color.new(color.red,   85) : color.new(color.gray, 88)

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 26 — DISPLAY INTELLIGENCE ENGINE (DIE)
// Visual-layer only. Zero changes to any detection, logic, or calculation above.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ── DIE-1: DISPLAY DENSITY ENGINE ────────────────────────────────────────────
// Count labels placed in the last 100 bars as a proxy for density.
// We use a running var counter that increments when we place a label this bar
// and we sample a look-back sum periodically.

var int  die_labelCount   = 0        // labels placed this bar (reset each bar)
var int  die_totalLabels  = 0        // rolling total
var array<int> die_barCounts = array.new_int(100, 0)

// Rotate the ring-buffer
array.set(die_barCounts, bar_index % 100, die_labelCount)
int die_density100 = array.sum(die_barCounts)    // labels per 100 bars

string die_densityLevel =
     die_density100 < 30  ? "Low"    :
     die_density100 < 80  ? "Medium" : "High"

// Helper: should we show objects at a given priority given current density?
f_die_show(int _priority) =>
    bool _ok = false
    if displayMode == "Research"
        _ok := true
    else if displayMode == "Context"
        _ok := _priority >= 60
    else
        // Execution mode — only highest-priority objects render
        if die_densityLevel == "Low"
            _ok := _priority >= 80
        else
            _ok := _priority >= 100
    _ok


// Reset label counter each bar (approximate — we track at render time)
die_labelCount := 0

// ── DIE-2: FU ORDER BLOCK ENGINE ─────────────────────────────────────────────
// Detects Bull and Bear FU candles, tracks lifecycle, renders zones + labels.
// NO changes to any detection variables used elsewhere (fuBoostBelief etc).

var array<float>  fu_top        = array.new_float ()
var array<float>  fu_bot        = array.new_float ()
var array<int>    fu_birthBar   = array.new_int   ()
var array<int>    fu_dir        = array.new_int   ()   // 1=bull, -1=bear
var array<string> fu_state      = array.new_string()   // Fresh/Active/Interacting/Exhausted/Invalidated
var array<box>    fu_boxes      = array.new<box>  ()
var array<label>  fu_labels     = array.new<label>()

// FU candle detection (display-only — detection mirrors existing fuDetect logic pattern)
// BEAR FU supply zone characteristics (from screenshot analysis):
//   1. Large bearish body (fuMinBodyRatio of range)
//   2. Upper wick present (liquidity grab above)
//   3. Gap leaving the candle at the top — close[0] has a gap below it relative to open[1]
//      i.e. the NEXT bar's open is below this bar's body close = price doesn't return
//   4. Liquidity left to the left — a prior high that was swept
// BULL FU demand zone characteristics (mirror):
//   1. Large bullish body
//   2. Lower wick (liquidity grab below)
//   3. Gap leaving upward — next bar opens above close or body
//   4. Liquidity left below (prior low swept)
//
// fuRequireInZone is used as a BOOST filter, not a hard gate, so zones form
// at genuine structural supply/demand regardless of whether price is in the flipzone.

float fuRange     = high - low
float fuBody      = math.abs(close - open)
float fuUpperWick = high - math.max(open, close)
float fuLowerWick = math.min(open, close) - low

// Gap-leave detection: the bar AFTER the FU candle opens with a gap
// (checked on the PREVIOUS bar since current bar is the one after the FU)
float prevBody      = math.abs(close[1] - open[1])
float prevRange     = high[1] - low[1]
float prevUpperWick = high[1] - math.max(open[1], close[1])
float prevLowerWick = math.min(open[1], close[1]) - low[1]
float prevBodyRatio = prevRange > 1e-10 ? prevBody / prevRange : 0.0
float prevUpperWickRatio = prevRange > 1e-10 ? prevUpperWick / prevRange : 0.0
float prevLowerWickRatio = prevRange > 1e-10 ? prevLowerWick / prevRange : 0.0

// Gap: current open is BELOW previous candle's close (bearish gap leave after bear FU)
// or current open is ABOVE previous candle's close (bullish gap leave after bull FU)
bool bearGapLeave = open < close[1] - atr * 0.05   // gap down from prior close = supply zone left behind
bool bullGapLeave = open > close[1] + atr * 0.05   // gap up from prior close = demand zone left behind

// Liquidity left: a swing high (for bear FU) to the left was swept by the wick
// Uses existing pivH/pivL variables — no new detection
bool liqLeftBear = not na(pivH) or (high[1] > nz(currSwingHigh[1], high[1]) * 0.998)
bool liqLeftBull = not na(pivL) or (low[1]  < nz(currSwingLow[1],  low[1])  * 1.002)

// BEAR FU: detected on current bar if PREVIOUS bar was the FU candle
// (so we can check whether THIS bar gapped away from it)
bool isBearFU_prev = prevRange > atr * 0.5 and
     prevBodyRatio      >= fuMinBodyRatio and
     close[1]           < open[1] and
     prevUpperWickRatio >= fuMinWickRatio and
     liqLeftBear and
     bearGapLeave

// BULL FU: detected on current bar if PREVIOUS bar was the FU candle
bool isBullFU_prev = prevRange > atr * 0.5 and
     prevBodyRatio      >= fuMinBodyRatio and
     close[1]           > open[1] and
     prevLowerWickRatio >= fuMinWickRatio and
     liqLeftBull and
     bullGapLeave

// Legacy same-bar detection (kept for compatibility — zone requirement relaxed)
bool isBullFU = fuRange > atr * 0.5 and
     fuBody / math.max(fuRange, 1e-10) >= fuMinBodyRatio and
     close > open and
     fuLowerWick / math.max(fuRange, 1e-10) >= fuMinWickRatio and
     (not fuRequireInZone or (not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot) and
     close >= flipBot * 0.98 and close <= flipTop * 1.02))

bool isBearFU = fuRange > atr * 0.5 and
     fuBody / math.max(fuRange, 1e-10) >= fuMinBodyRatio and
     close < open and
     fuUpperWick / math.max(fuRange, 1e-10) >= fuMinWickRatio and
     (not fuRequireInZone or (not na(flipTop) and not na(flipBot) and
     close >= flipBot * 0.98 and close <= flipTop * 1.02))

// Spawn new FU block — gap-confirmed (prev-bar FU + current gap leave)
// These are high-conviction zones: liquidity was left + price gapped away
if isBearFU_prev and showFUBlocks
    // Zone = body of the FU candle (previous bar)
    float _fuPrevTop = math.max(open[1], close[1])
    float _fuPrevBot = low[1]
    array.push(fu_top,      _fuPrevTop)
    array.push(fu_bot,      _fuPrevBot)
    array.push(fu_birthBar, bar_index - 1)
    array.push(fu_dir,      -1)
    array.push(fu_state,    "Fresh")
    box _fuBoxGC = box.new(left=bar_index - 1, top=_fuPrevTop,
         bottom=_fuPrevBot, right=bar_index - 1 + fuMaxBarsActive,
         bgcolor=f_zoneFill(color.new(color.red, 92)),
         border_color=color.new(#ff6600, 50), border_width=2)
    array.push(fu_boxes, _fuBoxGC)
    if showFULabels and ecvShow_FUImbalance
        label _fuLblGC = label.new(bar_index - 1, high[1] + atr * 0.5,
             "BEAR FU ⚡",
             style=label.style_label_down,
             color=color.new(#ff6600, 15),
             textcolor=color.white, size=size.small)
        array.push(fu_labels, _fuLblGC)
        die_labelCount := die_labelCount + 1
    else
        array.push(fu_labels, na)

if isBullFU_prev and showFUBlocks
    float _fuPrevTop2 = high[1]
    float _fuPrevBot2 = math.min(open[1], close[1])
    array.push(fu_top,      _fuPrevTop2)
    array.push(fu_bot,      _fuPrevBot2)
    array.push(fu_birthBar, bar_index - 1)
    array.push(fu_dir,      1)
    array.push(fu_state,    "Fresh")
    box _fuBoxGC2 = box.new(left=bar_index - 1, top=_fuPrevTop2,
         bottom=_fuPrevBot2, right=bar_index - 1 + fuMaxBarsActive,
         bgcolor=f_zoneFill(color.new(color.lime, 92)),
         border_color=color.new(#00ffaa, 50), border_width=2)
    array.push(fu_boxes, _fuBoxGC2)
    if showFULabels and ecvShow_FUImbalance
        label _fuLblGC2 = label.new(bar_index - 1, low[1] - atr * 0.5,
             "BULL FU ⚡",
             style=label.style_label_up,
             color=color.new(#00ffaa, 15),
             textcolor=color.black, size=size.small)
        array.push(fu_labels, _fuLblGC2)
        die_labelCount := die_labelCount + 1
    else
        array.push(fu_labels, na)

// Spawn new FU block — legacy same-bar detection
if isBullFU and showFUBlocks
    array.push(fu_top,      high)
    array.push(fu_bot,      math.min(open, close))
    array.push(fu_birthBar, bar_index)
    array.push(fu_dir,      1)
    array.push(fu_state,    "Fresh")
    box _fuBox = box.new(left=bar_index, top=high,
         bottom=math.min(open, close), right=bar_index + fuMaxBarsActive,
         bgcolor=f_zoneFill(color.new(color.lime, 92)),
         border_color=color.new(color.lime, 40), border_width=1)
    array.push(fu_boxes, _fuBox)
    if showFULabels and ecvShow_FUCandle
        label _fuLbl = label.new(bar_index, low - atr * 0.4, "BULL FU",
             style=label.style_label_up, color=color.new(color.lime, 25),
             textcolor=color.black, size=size.small)
        array.push(fu_labels, _fuLbl)
        die_labelCount := die_labelCount + 1
    else
        array.push(fu_labels, na)

if isBearFU and showFUBlocks
    array.push(fu_top,      math.max(open, close))
    array.push(fu_bot,      low)
    array.push(fu_birthBar, bar_index)
    array.push(fu_dir,      -1)
    array.push(fu_state,    "Fresh")
    box _fuBox2 = box.new(left=bar_index, top=math.max(open, close),
         bottom=low, right=bar_index + fuMaxBarsActive,
         bgcolor=f_zoneFill(color.new(color.red, 92)),
         border_color=color.new(color.red, 40), border_width=1)
    array.push(fu_boxes, _fuBox2)
    if showFULabels and ecvShow_FUCandle
        label _fuLbl2 = label.new(bar_index, high + atr * 0.4, "BEAR FU",
             style=label.style_label_down, color=color.new(color.red, 25),
             textcolor=color.white, size=size.small)
        array.push(fu_labels, _fuLbl2)
        die_labelCount := die_labelCount + 1
    else
        array.push(fu_labels, na)

// Update FU block lifecycle states + trim expired
int _fuN = array.size(fu_top)

// ── Pass 1: Update lifecycle states and box visuals ──────────────────────
if _fuN > 0
    for _fi = 0 to _fuN - 1
        if _fi < array.size(fu_top)
            float  _fTop = array.get(fu_top,      _fi)
            float  _fBot = array.get(fu_bot,      _fi)
            int    _fBB  = array.get(fu_birthBar, _fi)
            int    _fDir = array.get(fu_dir,      _fi)
            string _fSt  = array.get(fu_state,    _fi)
            int    _fAge = bar_index - _fBB

            string _newState = _fSt
            if _fAge <= 3
                _newState := "Fresh"
            else if close > _fTop and _fDir == 1
                _newState := "Exhausted"
            else if close < _fBot and _fDir == -1
                _newState := "Exhausted"
            else if (close <= _fTop and close >= _fBot)
                _newState := "Interacting"
            else if (_fDir == 1 and close < _fBot - atr * 0.5) or (_fDir == -1 and close > _fTop + atr * 0.5)
                _newState := "Invalidated"
            else if _fAge > 3
                _newState := "Active"

            box _bx = array.get(fu_boxes, _fi)
            if not na(_bx)
                if _fAge < fuMaxBarsActive and _newState != "Invalidated"
                    box.set_right(_bx, bar_index + 10)
                    color _fc =
                         _newState == "Interacting" ? color.new(_fDir == 1 ? color.lime : color.red, 70) :
                         _newState == "Exhausted"   ? color.new(color.gray, 85)                          :
                         _newState == "Invalidated" ? color.new(color.gray, 90)                          :
                         _newState == "Fresh"       ? color.new(_fDir == 1 ? color.lime : color.red, 80) :
                                                      color.new(_fDir == 1 ? color.lime : color.red, 88)
                    box.set_bgcolor(_bx, _fc)
                else
                    box.delete(_bx)
                    array.set(fu_boxes, _fi, na)

            array.set(fu_state, _fi, _newState)

// ── Pass 2: Remove expired/invalidated (iterate backwards to avoid index shift)
int _fuN2 = array.size(fu_top)
if _fuN2 > 0
    for _fi2 = _fuN2 - 1 to 0
        if _fi2 < array.size(fu_top)
            int    _fAge2 = bar_index - array.get(fu_birthBar, _fi2)
            string _fSt2  = array.get(fu_state, _fi2)
            if _fAge2 >= fuMaxBarsActive or _fSt2 == "Invalidated"
                box   _bx2 = array.get(fu_boxes,  _fi2)
                label _lb2 = array.get(fu_labels, _fi2)
                if not na(_bx2)
                    box.delete(_bx2)
                if not na(_lb2)
                    label.delete(_lb2)
                array.remove(fu_top,      _fi2)
                array.remove(fu_bot,      _fi2)
                array.remove(fu_birthBar, _fi2)
                array.remove(fu_dir,      _fi2)
                array.remove(fu_state,    _fi2)
                array.remove(fu_boxes,    _fi2)
                array.remove(fu_labels,   _fi2)

// Track active FU state for confluence
bool die_anyBullFUActive = false
bool die_anyBearFUActive = false
int  die_activeFUCount   = 0
int  _fuN3 = array.size(fu_state)
if _fuN3 > 0
    for _fj = 0 to _fuN3 - 1
        string _st = array.get(fu_state, _fj)
        int    _fd = array.get(fu_dir,   _fj)
        if _st == "Active" or _st == "Fresh" or _st == "Interacting"
            die_activeFUCount := die_activeFUCount + 1
            if _fd == 1
                die_anyBullFUActive := true
            else
                die_anyBearFUActive := true

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ENGINE 1A.8 / 1A.9 — FU WICK CAPTURE AUTHORITY  (Relevant Structure Authority)
// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Sits ABOVE destination / target / induction / liquidation: the market is drawn
// toward liquidity TRAPPED by a validated FU wick. A FU candle = a spike that
// pierces a prior swing (steals liquidity), closes back inside ("the middle
// finger"), and is later VALIDATED when price destroys the candle's OPPOSITE
// extreme. The captured wick becomes a future MAGNET; its 38–62% midpoint is the
// INDUCTION BAND (the default execution / early-trader trap region). Self-
// contained, chart-timeframe, single live objects (no per-bar trail). Renders
// FU / FU MID / MAGNET / INDUCTION BAND and exposes fuw_* for downstream engines.
showFUWick     = input.bool (true, "Show FU Wick Authority (1A.8/1A.9)", group=GRP_FUOB)
fuwMinWickFrac = input.float(0.4,  "FU Spike: min wick / range",         group=GRP_FUOB, minval=0.2, maxval=0.9, step=0.05)
fuwLookback    = input.int  (3,    "FU Spike: structure lookback (bars)", group=GRP_FUOB, minval=2, maxval=30)
showFUConv     = input.bool (true, "Show FU Conversation Route (1A.11/1A.12 arrows)", group=GRP_FUOB)
showAFE        = input.bool (true, "Show AFE Flip-Echo Path (1A.9B arrow)", group=GRP_FUOB)
fuRouteMinConf = input.int  (35,   "FU Route: min path confidence %",    group=GRP_FUOB, minval=0, maxval=100)
fuAuthMin      = input.int  (40,   "FU Route: min node authority score", group=GRP_FUOB, minval=0, maxval=100)

var float fuw_tip      = na      // wick extreme (manipulation point)
var float fuw_bodyHigh = na
var float fuw_bodyLow  = na
var float fuw_mid      = na      // 50% of captured wick
var float fuw_mid38    = na
var float fuw_mid62    = na
var int   fuw_dir      = 0       // 1 = bull FU (lower spike), -1 = bear FU (upper spike)
var float fuw_leftPool = na      // swept swing = trapped (captured) liquidity = future magnet
var int   fuw_bar      = na
var bool  fuw_valid    = false   // becomes true once the opposite extreme is destroyed
var float fuw_strength = na

// NEW CANDIDATE — a spike through LOCAL structure (the highest high / lowest low
// of the prior `fuwLookback` bars) that closes back inside it: the "middle finger"
// that sweeps recent liquidity. Using LOCAL structure (not just the major swing)
// is what catches the obvious FU spikes through nearby equal highs / lows. The
// swept level becomes the captured left-liquidity pool (the future magnet).
float _fuwRange    = math.max(high - low, 1e-10)
float _fuwPriorHi  = ta.highest(high, fuwLookback)[1]
float _fuwPriorLo  = ta.lowest(low,  fuwLookback)[1]
bool  _fuwBearCand = not na(_fuwPriorHi) and high > _fuwPriorHi and close < _fuwPriorHi and (high - math.max(open, close)) / _fuwRange >= fuwMinWickFrac
bool  _fuwBullCand = not na(_fuwPriorLo) and low  < _fuwPriorLo and close > _fuwPriorLo and (math.min(open, close) - low) / _fuwRange >= fuwMinWickFrac

if _fuwBearCand
    fuw_dir      := -1
    fuw_tip      := high
    fuw_bodyHigh := math.max(open, close)
    fuw_bodyLow  := math.min(open, close)
    fuw_mid      := fuw_bodyHigh + (fuw_tip - fuw_bodyHigh) * 0.50
    fuw_mid38    := fuw_bodyHigh + (fuw_tip - fuw_bodyHigh) * 0.38
    fuw_mid62    := fuw_bodyHigh + (fuw_tip - fuw_bodyHigh) * 0.62
    fuw_leftPool := _fuwPriorHi
    fuw_bar      := bar_index
    fuw_valid    := false
    fuw_strength := math.min(100.0, (fuw_tip - fuw_bodyHigh) / math.max(atr, 1e-10) * 40.0 + 40.0)
else if _fuwBullCand
    fuw_dir      := 1
    fuw_tip      := low
    fuw_bodyHigh := math.max(open, close)
    fuw_bodyLow  := math.min(open, close)
    fuw_mid      := fuw_tip + (fuw_bodyLow - fuw_tip) * 0.50
    fuw_mid38    := fuw_tip + (fuw_bodyLow - fuw_tip) * 0.38
    fuw_mid62    := fuw_tip + (fuw_bodyLow - fuw_tip) * 0.62
    fuw_leftPool := _fuwPriorLo
    fuw_bar      := bar_index
    fuw_valid    := false
    fuw_strength := math.min(100.0, (fuw_bodyLow - fuw_tip) / math.max(atr, 1e-10) * 40.0 + 40.0)

// VALIDATION — later price DESTROYS the candle's opposite extreme (break-confirm).
if not fuw_valid and fuw_dir == -1 and not na(fuw_bodyLow) and bar_index > nz(fuw_bar) and close < fuw_bodyLow
    fuw_valid := true
if not fuw_valid and fuw_dir ==  1 and not na(fuw_bodyHigh) and bar_index > nz(fuw_bar) and close > fuw_bodyHigh
    fuw_valid := true

// INDUCTION BAND = 38–62% of the captured wick. "Induction expected" when price
// trades back into that band of a VALIDATED FU. futureMagnet = captured liquidity.
float fuw_bandHi = (na(fuw_mid38) or na(fuw_mid62)) ? na : math.max(fuw_mid38, fuw_mid62)
float fuw_bandLo = (na(fuw_mid38) or na(fuw_mid62)) ? na : math.min(fuw_mid38, fuw_mid62)
bool  fuw_inductionExpected = fuw_valid and not na(fuw_bandHi) and close <= fuw_bandHi and close >= fuw_bandLo
float fuw_futureMagnet      = fuw_valid ? fuw_leftPool : na

// RENDER — single live objects (created once, then moved/updated). Not gated by
// displayMode, so the FU authority is visible in Execution mode too.
var box   fuw_bandBox = na
var label fuw_lblFU   = na
var label fuw_lblMid  = na
var label fuw_lblMag  = na
var label fuw_lblBand = na

if showFUWick and fuw_valid and not na(fuw_tip) and not na(fuw_bandHi)
    int   _fuwR    = bar_index + 12
    float _fuwBand = (fuw_bandHi + fuw_bandLo) / 2.0
    color _fuwCol  = fuw_dir == 1 ? #00ffaa : #ff6600
    // Induction band box (mid38..mid62), extended to the right edge.
    if na(fuw_bandBox)
        fuw_bandBox := box.new(nz(fuw_bar, bar_index), fuw_bandHi, _fuwR, fuw_bandLo, bgcolor=color.new(color.yellow, 82), border_color=color.new(color.yellow, 35), border_width=1)
    else
        box.set_lefttop(fuw_bandBox, nz(fuw_bar, bar_index), fuw_bandHi)
        box.set_rightbottom(fuw_bandBox, _fuwR, fuw_bandLo)
    // FU label at the wick extreme (manipulation point).
    if na(fuw_lblFU)
        fuw_lblFU := label.new(nz(fuw_bar, bar_index), fuw_tip, "FU", style=fuw_dir == -1 ? label.style_label_down : label.style_label_up, color=color.new(_fuwCol, 20), textcolor=color.white, size=size.small)
    else
        label.set_xy(fuw_lblFU, nz(fuw_bar, bar_index), fuw_tip)
        label.set_style(fuw_lblFU, fuw_dir == -1 ? label.style_label_down : label.style_label_up)
        label.set_color(fuw_lblFU, color.new(_fuwCol, 20))
    // FU MID label at midpoint.
    if na(fuw_lblMid)
