        fuw_lblMid := label.new(_fuwR, fuw_mid, "FU MID", style=label.style_label_left, color=color.new(color.aqua, 25), textcolor=color.white, size=size.tiny)
    else
        label.set_xy(fuw_lblMid, _fuwR, fuw_mid)
    // INDUCTION BAND label.
    if na(fuw_lblBand)
        fuw_lblBand := label.new(_fuwR, _fuwBand, "INDUCTION BAND", style=label.style_label_left, color=color.new(color.yellow, 15), textcolor=color.black, size=size.tiny)
    else
        label.set_xy(fuw_lblBand, _fuwR, _fuwBand)
    // MAGNET label at captured left-liquidity pool (future target).
    if not na(fuw_futureMagnet)
        if na(fuw_lblMag)
            fuw_lblMag := label.new(_fuwR, fuw_futureMagnet, "MAGNET", style=label.style_label_left, color=color.new(#ff00ff, 20), textcolor=color.white, size=size.tiny)
        else
            label.set_xy(fuw_lblMag, _fuwR, fuw_futureMagnet)

// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 1A.9 RECURSIVE TARGET HIERARCHY — multi-TF FU left-pool magnets.
// f_fuPool() detects the most-recent VALIDATED FU on whatever timeframe it is
// requested on and returns its captured left-liquidity pool + induction band.
// Lower timeframes target the HIGHER-TF pool (H4 pool is the magnet for H1/M15/
// M5 recursion), per the spec's recursive target hierarchy.
f_fuPool(simple float _wickFrac) =>
    var float _tip   = na
    var float _bH    = na
    var float _bL    = na
    var int   _dir   = 0
    var float _pool  = na
    var bool  _valid = false
    var bool  _conf  = false
    float _rng  = math.max(high - low, 1e-10)
    float _priorHi = ta.highest(high, 3)[1]
    float _priorLo = ta.lowest(low,  3)[1]
    bool  _bear = not na(_priorHi) and high > _priorHi and close < _priorHi and (high - math.max(open, close)) / _rng >= _wickFrac
    bool  _bull = not na(_priorLo) and low  < _priorLo and close > _priorLo and (math.min(open, close) - low) / _rng >= _wickFrac
    if _bear
        _dir := -1
        _tip := high
        _bH  := math.max(open, close)
        _bL  := math.min(open, close)
        _pool := _priorHi
        _valid := true
        _conf := false
    else if _bull
        _dir := 1
        _tip := low
        _bH  := math.max(open, close)
        _bL  := math.min(open, close)
        _pool := _priorLo
        _valid := true
        _conf := false
    if _valid and _dir == -1 and not _conf and close < _bL
        _conf := true
    if _valid and _dir ==  1 and not _conf and close > _bH
        _conf := true
    float _mid = na
    float _bHi = na
    float _bLo = na
    if _dir == -1 and not na(_tip)
        _mid := _bH + (_tip - _bH) * 0.50
        _bHi := _bH + (_tip - _bH) * 0.62
        _bLo := _bH + (_tip - _bH) * 0.38
    else if _dir == 1 and not na(_tip)
        _mid := _tip + (_bL - _tip) * 0.50
        _bHi := _tip + (_bL - _tip) * 0.62
        _bLo := _tip + (_bL - _tip) * 0.38
    float _wkAtr = (_dir == -1 and not na(_tip)) ? (_tip - _bH) / math.max(ta.atr(14), 1e-10) : (_dir == 1 and not na(_tip)) ? (_bL - _tip) / math.max(ta.atr(14), 1e-10) : 0.0
    // STRUCTURAL SCORE 0-100: break-confirm 30 + significance 25 + originated-
    // from-liquidity 20 (always, it swept a high/low) + induction 15 + liq-wave 10.
    float _score = (_conf ? 30.0 : 0.0) + math.min(25.0, _wkAtr * 15.0) + 20.0 + (_wkAtr > 1.0 ? 15.0 : 0.0) + (_wkAtr > 1.5 ? 10.0 : 0.0)
    [_valid ? _pool : na, _mid, _bHi, _bLo, _dir, _valid ? 1 : 0, _tip, _score]

[h4_fuPool,  h4_fuMid,  h4_fuBandHi,  h4_fuBandLo,  h4_fuDir,  h4_fuValid,  h4_fuTip,  h4_fuScore]  = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("240"), f_fuPool(fuwMinWickFrac), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)
[h1_fuPool,  h1_fuMid,  h1_fuBandHi,  h1_fuBandLo,  h1_fuDir,  h1_fuValid,  h1_fuTip,  h1_fuScore]  = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("60"),  f_fuPool(fuwMinWickFrac), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)
[m15_fuPool, m15_fuMid, m15_fuBandHi, m15_fuBandLo, m15_fuDir, m15_fuValid, m15_fuTip, m15_fuScore] = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("15"),  f_fuPool(fuwMinWickFrac), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)
[m5_fuPool,  m5_fuMid,  m5_fuBandHi,  m5_fuBandLo,  m5_fuDir,  m5_fuValid,  m5_fuTip,  m5_fuScore]  = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("5"),   f_fuPool(fuwMinWickFrac), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)
[d_fuPool,   d_fuMid,   d_fuBandHi,   d_fuBandLo,   d_fuDir,   d_fuValid,   d_fuTip,   d_fuScore]   = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("D"),   f_fuPool(fuwMinWickFrac), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)
[w_fuPool,   w_fuMid,   w_fuBandHi,   w_fuBandLo,   w_fuDir,   w_fuValid,   w_fuTip,   w_fuScore]   = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, f_safeTF("W"),   f_fuPool(fuwMinWickFrac), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)

// Recursive alignment % (how many of the six layers carry a live validated FU)
// and the winning future-magnet target = the HIGHEST timeframe with a valid FU.
int   _fuActiveCnt   = (nz(w_fuValid) == 1 ? 1 : 0) + (nz(d_fuValid) == 1 ? 1 : 0) + (nz(h4_fuValid) == 1 ? 1 : 0) + (nz(h1_fuValid) == 1 ? 1 : 0) + (nz(m15_fuValid) == 1 ? 1 : 0) + (nz(m5_fuValid) == 1 ? 1 : 0)
float fu_recursiveAlign = _fuActiveCnt / 6.0 * 100.0
float  fu_winTarget = na
string fu_winSrc    = "-"
float  fu_winBand   = na
if nz(w_fuValid) == 1 and not na(w_fuPool)
    fu_winTarget := w_fuPool
    fu_winSrc    := "W FU Left Pool"
    fu_winBand   := w_fuMid
else if nz(d_fuValid) == 1 and not na(d_fuPool)
    fu_winTarget := d_fuPool
    fu_winSrc    := "D FU Left Pool"
    fu_winBand   := d_fuMid
else if nz(h4_fuValid) == 1 and not na(h4_fuPool)
    fu_winTarget := h4_fuPool
    fu_winSrc    := "H4 FU Left Pool"
    fu_winBand   := h4_fuMid
else if nz(h1_fuValid) == 1 and not na(h1_fuPool)
    fu_winTarget := h1_fuPool
    fu_winSrc    := "H1 FU Left Pool"
    fu_winBand   := h1_fuMid
else if nz(m15_fuValid) == 1 and not na(m15_fuPool)
    fu_winTarget := m15_fuPool
    fu_winSrc    := "M15 FU Left Pool"
    fu_winBand   := m15_fuMid
else if fuw_valid and not na(fuw_futureMagnet)
    fu_winTarget := fuw_futureMagnet
    fu_winSrc    := "FU Left Pool"
    fu_winBand   := fuw_mid

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ENGINE 1A.9B — ALTERNATING FLIP ECHO ENGINE (AFE)
// ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Tracks how a flip zone CHANGES ROLE around a validated FU origin. The FU origin
// is the permanent authority/destination; the upper flip evolves Destination ->
// Liquidity as price echoes: expand away -> self-return to upper flip -> sell to
// lower flip -> lower-flip reversal consumes the upper flip (now liquidity) and
// targets the FU origin -> FU rejects -> continuation. Six-step state machine.
var int    afe_step          = 0
var float  afe_origin        = na     // FU authority extreme (permanent)
var int    afe_originDir     = 0      // -1 bear FU (top), 1 bull FU (bottom)
var float  afe_upperFlip     = na     // near flip (FU midpoint / induction band)
var float  afe_lowerFlip     = na     // far flip (opposing swing)
var string afe_upperFlipRole = "—"
var float  afe_activeDest    = na
var float  afe_target        = na
var bool   afe_selfReturnDone = false
var bool   afe_continuation   = false

// (Re)anchor on a freshly validated FU wick authority.
if fuw_valid and (na(afe_origin) or fuw_tip != afe_origin)
    afe_origin        := fuw_tip
    afe_originDir     := fuw_dir
    afe_upperFlip     := fuw_mid
    afe_lowerFlip     := fuw_dir == -1 ? nz(prevSwingLow, fuw_bodyLow) : nz(prevSwingHigh, fuw_bodyHigh)
    afe_step          := 1
    afe_upperFlipRole := "Destination"
    afe_activeDest    := fuw_mid
    afe_target        := na
    afe_selfReturnDone := false
    afe_continuation   := false

if afe_step >= 1 and not na(afe_origin) and afe_originDir != 0
    bool _afeBear = afe_originDir == -1
    if afe_step == 1 and (_afeBear ? close < nz(fuw_bodyLow, afe_origin) : close > nz(fuw_bodyHigh, afe_origin))
        afe_step       := 2
        afe_activeDest := afe_upperFlip
    if afe_step == 2 and not na(afe_upperFlip) and (_afeBear ? high >= afe_upperFlip : low <= afe_upperFlip)
        afe_step           := 3
        afe_selfReturnDone := true
        afe_activeDest     := afe_lowerFlip
    if afe_step == 3 and not na(afe_lowerFlip) and (_afeBear ? low <= afe_lowerFlip : high >= afe_lowerFlip)
        afe_step          := 4
        afe_activeDest    := afe_origin
        afe_target        := afe_origin
        afe_upperFlipRole := "Liquidity"
    if afe_step == 4 and not na(afe_origin) and (_afeBear ? high >= afe_origin : low <= afe_origin)
        afe_step         := 5
        afe_continuation := true


// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ENGINE 1A.10 — FU CONVERSATION (compact, path-only — drawn as ARROWS, no panel)
// Parent FU being SOUGHT = the highest-timeframe validated FU sitting on the bias
// side of price. Confidence blends recursive FU alignment with that FU's score.
int    conv_bias   = displayWaveDir_M5 != 0 ? displayWaveDir_M5 : fractalStackDir
float  conv_seekPx = na
string conv_seekTf = "—"
float  conv_seekSc = 0.0
if conv_bias != 0
    if nz(w_fuValid) == 1 and not na(w_fuTip) and (conv_bias == 1 ? w_fuTip > close : w_fuTip < close)
        conv_seekPx := w_fuTip
        conv_seekTf := "W"
        conv_seekSc := nz(w_fuScore)
    else if nz(d_fuValid) == 1 and not na(d_fuTip) and (conv_bias == 1 ? d_fuTip > close : d_fuTip < close)
        conv_seekPx := d_fuTip
        conv_seekTf := "D"
        conv_seekSc := nz(d_fuScore)
    else if nz(h4_fuValid) == 1 and not na(h4_fuTip) and (conv_bias == 1 ? h4_fuTip > close : h4_fuTip < close)
        conv_seekPx := h4_fuTip
        conv_seekTf := "H4"
        conv_seekSc := nz(h4_fuScore)
    else if nz(h1_fuValid) == 1 and not na(h1_fuTip) and (conv_bias == 1 ? h1_fuTip > close : h1_fuTip < close)
        conv_seekPx := h1_fuTip
        conv_seekTf := "H1"
        conv_seekSc := nz(h1_fuScore)
    else if nz(m15_fuValid) == 1 and not na(m15_fuTip) and (conv_bias == 1 ? m15_fuTip > close : m15_fuTip < close)
        conv_seekPx := m15_fuTip
        conv_seekTf := "M15"
        conv_seekSc := nz(m15_fuScore)
    else if nz(m5_fuValid) == 1 and not na(m5_fuTip) and (conv_bias == 1 ? m5_fuTip > close : m5_fuTip < close)
        conv_seekPx := m5_fuTip
        conv_seekTf := "M5"
        conv_seekSc := nz(m5_fuScore)
float conv_confidence = (conv_bias == 0 or na(conv_seekPx)) ? 0.0 : math.min(100.0, conv_seekSc * 0.7 + fu_recursiveAlign * 0.3)

// ── DIE-3: ENTRY CYCLE QUALITY SCORING ───────────────────────────────────────
// Display-only score 0-100. Uses existing intelligence outputs. No logic changes.

float die_entryScore = math.min(
     (nz(waveModelFit,    50.0) * 0.20) +
     (nz(modelConfidence, 50.0) * 0.20) +
     (htfAlign == direction and direction != 0 ? 20.0 : htfAlign == 0 ? 10.0 : 0.0) +
     (nz(liqHeat, 0.0) > 50 ? 15.0 : nz(liqHeat, 0.0) * 0.30) +
     ((die_anyBullFUActive and direction == 1) or
      (die_anyBearFUActive and direction == -1) ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     (flipzoneStagesComplete >= 3 ? 10.0 : flipzoneStagesComplete * 3.3),
     100.0)
float die_entryScore_safe = nz(die_entryScore, 0.0)

// ── DIE-4: ENTRY + FU CONFLUENCE DETECTION ───────────────────────────────────
// Highest-confidence execution object.

bool die_entryFUConfluence =
     ((longSignal  and die_anyBullFUActive) or
      (shortSignal and die_anyBearFUActive))

// FU contribution descriptor for entry cycle labels
string die_fuContrib =
     die_entryFUConfluence                                   ? "FU CONFIRMED" :
     ((direction == 1  and die_anyBullFUActive and not longSignal) or
      (direction == -1 and die_anyBearFUActive and not shortSignal)) ? "FU ASSISTED" : "FU NOT PRESENT"

// ── DIE-5: POINT 4 ORIGIN REWORK (rendering logic)  ──────────────────────────
// Active origin = full label. Old origins suppressed to marker "○".
// Age tracking: anything older than 100 bars from origin spawn → marker only.
int die_originAge = not na(point4OriginBar) ? bar_index - point4OriginBar : 9999
bool die_originRecent  = die_originAge < 50
bool die_originOld     = die_originAge >= 100

// ── DIE-6: NARRATIVE ENGINE ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Single dominant narrative label. Never stack historical narratives.
// Uses canonical Unified Wave Lifecycle phase names.

// ── DIE: REGION-BASED DISPLAY AUTHORITY (MEGATRON 8C/8D — v18) ────────────────
// FIRST PRINCIPLE: Engine 1A Truth -> currentDisplayPhase -> Chart. Nothing in
// between. No compression, no translation, no abbreviation, no family layer, no
// event labels. The chart renders `currentDisplayPhase` VERBATIM as a live
// REGION label. Text, colour, visibility, opacity, style and size ALL consume
// the SAME authority string (currentDisplayPhase) — there is no second
// vocabulary (ie1a_hypFamily / f_chartPhaseLabel are gone from this path). The
// label is created when a phase region begins, LIVE-UPDATED (text/x/y/colour)
// every bar while the region persists, then FROZEN in place when the region ends
// and a fresh label is spawned for the next region. No density / displayMode gate.

// Absorption authority (item 8): Absorption may ONLY be labelled AFTER a genuine
// objective arrival AND a true CHoCH. Mid-leg "absorption" is illegal. Unlocks on
// (liqg objective arrival ∧ liqg true CHoCH) or (objective made ∧ structural CHoCH);
// re-locks the moment a new expansion leg / origin begins.
var bool die_objMade = false
if ie1a_currentPhase == "New High" or ie1a_currentPhase == "New Low" or liqg_objArrival
    die_objMade := true
if ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Point 4 Origin"
    die_objMade := false
var bool die_absUnlocked = false
if (liqg_objArrival and liqg_trueCHoCH) or (die_objMade and (bullCHoCH or bearCHoCH))
    die_absUnlocked := true
if ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Point 4 Origin"
    die_absUnlocked := false

// VERBATIM region text — the single authority, uppercased, with the liquidation
// " • " substate separator rendered as a newline. Absorption suppressed until
// genuinely unlocked. No phase enumeration, no remap.
bool   die_isAbs     = str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Absorption")
string die_regionTxt = (die_isAbs and not die_absUnlocked) ? "" : str.upper(str.replace_all(currentDisplayPhase, " • ", "\n"))

// Colour — derived by INSPECTING the authority string itself (not a second map).
// Liquidation-wave check first so its substates never fall through to a phase word.
color die_regionCol =
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Liquidation Wave") ? color.orange :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Induction")        ? color.yellow :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Pre-Convexity")    ? #c084fc      :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Liquidity")        ? color.orange :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Absorption")       ? color.aqua   :
     (str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "New High") or str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "New Low")) ? #00ff88 :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Retracement")      ? color.silver :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Return")           ? color.teal   :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Expansion")        ? color.lime   : color.gray

// Visibility — same authority string, wired to the matching Section-9 category.
// Induction checked before Retracement/Expansion so "Retracement Induction" and
// "Expansion Induction" both gate on the Induction toggle.
bool die_regionVisible =
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Liquidation Wave") ? ecvShow_Liquidation  :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Induction")        ? ecvShow_Induction    :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Pre-Convexity")    ? ecvShow_PreConvexity :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Liquidity")        ? ecvShow_Liquidation  :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Absorption")       ? ecvShow_Absorption   :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "New High")         ? ecvShow_Highs        :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "New Low")          ? ecvShow_Lows         :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Demand Return")    ? ecvShow_Demand       :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Supply Return")    ? ecvShow_Supply       :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Retracement")      ? ecvShow_Retracement  :
     str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Expansion")        ? ecvShow_Expansion    : true

// Opacity & size — also authority-driven. Key regions render larger/more solid.
int  die_regionOpacity = str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Liquidation Wave") ? 10 : 20
bool die_regionBig     = str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Liquidation Wave") or str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Induction") or str.contains(currentDisplayPhase, "Pre-Convexity")

// Single LIVE label — exactly one object on the chart. Created once, then
// LIVE-UPDATED (text / position / colour / style / size) on every bar so it
// always shows the CURRENT region, and deleted when there is nothing to show.
// It is NOT re-spawned on phase changes, so it never leaves a per-bar trail
// across history. (The v18 flood came from spawning a frozen label on every
// change while the live engine phase oscillates bar-to-bar.) Deliberately NOT
// gated by f_die_show()/displayMode — this is THE phase authority and must
// survive Execution mode and every density level.
var label die_regionLbl = na
float die_regionY    = direction == 1 ? high + atr * 1.2 : low - atr * 1.2
bool  die_regionShow = showNarrative and die_regionTxt != "" and direction != 0 and die_regionVisible

if die_regionShow
    if na(die_regionLbl)
        die_regionLbl := label.new(bar_index + 3, die_regionY, die_regionTxt,
             style=label.style_label_left,
             color=color.new(die_regionCol, die_regionOpacity), textcolor=color.white,
             size=die_regionBig ? size.normal : size.small)
    else
        label.set_xy(die_regionLbl, bar_index + 3, die_regionY)
        label.set_text(die_regionLbl, die_regionTxt)
        label.set_color(die_regionLbl, color.new(die_regionCol, die_regionOpacity))
        label.set_style(die_regionLbl, label.style_label_left)
        label.set_size(die_regionLbl, die_regionBig ? size.normal : size.small)
else if not na(die_regionLbl)
    label.delete(die_regionLbl)
    die_regionLbl := na

// ── DIE-7: ENTRY CYCLE CLUSTER TRACKING ──────────────────────────────────────
var int   die_clusterCount     = 0
var int   die_clusterStartBar  = na
var float die_clusterBestScore = 0.0
var bool  die_inCluster        = false

// On a fresh entry cycle label, check if another fired recently
bool die_entryCycleFired = recursiveJustFired

if die_entryCycleFired
    if not die_inCluster or (not na(die_clusterStartBar) and (bar_index - die_clusterStartBar) > clusterWindow)
        // Start a new cluster
        die_clusterCount     := 1
        die_clusterStartBar  := bar_index
        die_clusterBestScore := die_entryScore
        die_inCluster        := true
    else
        // Extend existing cluster
        die_clusterCount     := die_clusterCount + 1
        if die_entryScore > die_clusterBestScore
            die_clusterBestScore := die_entryScore

// Close cluster if window expired
if die_inCluster and not na(die_clusterStartBar) and (bar_index - die_clusterStartBar) > clusterWindow
    die_inCluster := false

// ── DIE-8: PRIMARY RENDERING — Entry Cycles, FU Confluence, Origins ──────────

// ─ Entry Cycle Label Rendering (replaces old simple green label in Section 13)
// This fires on recursiveJustFired (same condition as original label)
// We scale size by die_entryScore_safe and add FU contribution text.

if die_entryCycleFired and showLabels
    bool _isLong2 = (bullImpulse or bullConvShift)
    int  _eNum    = math.min(entryCycle + 1, 4)

    // Determine label size by score (string used, resolved at label.new call)
    string _eSizeStr =
         die_entryScore_safe >= 90 ? "large"  :
         die_entryScore_safe >= 75 ? "normal" :
         die_entryScore_safe >= 60 ? "small"  : "tiny"

    // Compact marker: EC + direction + score (registry carries full detail)
    string _eTxt = enableClustering and die_clusterCount > 1 ? "EC×" + str.tostring(die_clusterCount) : (_isLong2 ? "EC▲" : "EC▼") + str.tostring(math.round(die_entryScore_safe))

    label.new(bar_index,
         _isLong2 ? low - atr * 0.4 : high + atr * 0.4,
         _eTxt,
         style=_isLong2 ? label.style_label_up : label.style_label_down,
         color=color.new(color.black, 100), textcolor=_isLong2 ? color.lime : color.red,
         size=_eSizeStr == "large" ? size.normal : size.tiny)
    die_labelCount := die_labelCount + 1

// ─ ENTRY + FU Confluence Label (Priority 100 — highest visibility)
if die_entryFUConfluence and showFUConflLabel and ecvShow_FUImbalance
    bool _cfLong = longSignal
    label.new(bar_index,
         _cfLong ? low - atr * 1.0 : high + atr * 1.0,
         "⚡ ENTRY + FU ⚡\n" + str.tostring(math.round(die_entryScore_safe)) + "%",
         style=_cfLong ? label.style_label_up : label.style_label_down,
         color=color.new(#ffdd00, 10), textcolor=color.black, size=size.large)
    die_labelCount := die_labelCount + 1

// ─ Point 4 Origin Labels — rework: suppress old, compress recent
// The origin labels in Sections 13 (spawn) are already created there.
// We add the ACTIVE marker as a right-edge annotation if in execution/context mode.
// Old origins get a small "○" plotshape style marker instead of full labels.
// (The heavy orange labels from section 13 are controlled by showLabels and entryCycle==0
//  which already fires only on spawn. The DIE simply controls their size via density gating.)

// For currently active origin — annotate with priority marker if density is high
// (origin marker suppressed — spawned once at origin bar only)
// Marker only for old origins (visual downgrade)
if die_originOld and showLabels
    label.new(bar_index, direction == 1 ? point4OriginLow - atr * 0.2 : point4OriginHigh + atr * 0.2,
             "○",
             style=direction == 1 ? label.style_label_up : label.style_label_down,
             color=color.new(color.orange, 80), textcolor=color.orange, size=size.tiny)

// ── DIE-9: DISPLAY INTELLIGENCE DASHBOARD SECTION ───────────────────────────
// Added to Panel A as an extra section below existing content.

// SECTION 25 — DASHBOARD (3 panels with full section toggles)
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// Helper: write a separator row spanning both columns
f_sep(table t, int r, string lbl, string tsz) =>
    string _tsz2 = tsz
    table.cell(t, 0, r, lbl,
         text_color=color.new(color.white, 20),
         bgcolor=color.new(color.white, 80),
         text_size=_tsz2 == "tiny" ? size.tiny : _tsz2 == "normal" ? size.normal : size.small)
    table.cell(t, 1, r, "",
         bgcolor=color.new(color.white, 80))

// Helper: write a separator row spanning the right column pair (cols 2-3)
f_sep2(table t, int r, string lbl, string tsz) =>
    string _tsz3 = tsz
    table.cell(t, 2, r, lbl,
         text_color=color.new(color.white, 20),
         bgcolor=color.new(color.white, 80),
         text_size=_tsz3 == "tiny" ? size.tiny : _tsz3 == "normal" ? size.normal : size.small)
    table.cell(t, 3, r, "",
         bgcolor=color.new(color.white, 80))

// Shared colour helpers (re-declared as functions to avoid forward-ref issues)
f_sc(float v) =>
    v >= 85 ? #00ff88 : v >= 70 ? color.lime : v >= 40 ? color.yellow : color.red

f_sl(float v) =>
    v >= 85 ? "Exceptional" : v >= 70 ? "Strong" : v >= 40 ? "Neutral" : "Weak"

// Text size string → Pine size constant
string _ts = dashTextSize

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ENERGY DISPLACEMENT REGISTRY (Phase 2)
// Tracks every entry-cycle (energy displacement) event: level, direction, age,
// resolution. History preserved (oldest RESOLVED evicted only when over cap —
// unresolved energy is never dropped). Unresolved events get a persistent dotted
// level line; a registry table lists them (newest first) with nearest-unresolved
// footer. Wrapped in a function (var locals persist; single call site).
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
showEnergyRegistry = input.bool(true, "Show Energy Displacement Registry", group=GRP_FRZ)
edMaxEvents        = input.int (50,   "Energy Registry Max Events", group=GRP_FRZ, minval=10, maxval=200)

string _szA = _ts == "tiny" ? size.tiny : size.small

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// DASHBOARD PANELS A/B/C/FU — wrapped in function to satisfy body-length limit
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// DASHBOARD PANEL B — split out to satisfy per-function external-element limit
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PHASE 3 — RECURSIVE WAVE INTELLIGENCE ENGINE (v68)
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ── P3-1: RECURSIVE WAVE OBJECTS ─────────────────────────────────────────────
// REWIRED (v90): every layer now reads its OWN fixed-tf engine above.
// L0=M5 engine, L1=M15 engine, L2=H1 engine, L3=M3 engine (M1 = se1 engine).
// No value below depends on the chart timeframe.

float  l0_waveProgress       = nz(se5_wp)
float  l0_convexityMaturity  = nz(se5_cm)
float  l0_modelFit           = nz(se5_mf)
string l0_dominantPhase      = f_hypFam(l0_phaseCanon)   // L0 = M5 fixed-tf structure
float  l0_confidence         = math.max(10.0, math.min(100.0, nz(se5_mf)))
string l0_prediction         = f_nextPhase(int(nz(se5_ph)))
float  l0_predProb           = math.max(10.0, math.min(100.0, nz(se5_mf) * 0.6 + nz(se5_wp) * 0.4))

// Retained belief-score strengths — used ONLY by the P3-3 dominance heuristic,
// never for structural verdicts (those come from the fixed engines above).
float _l1_expStrength   = expScr_tf1
float _l1_decStrength   = decScr_tf1
float _l1_absStrength   = abScr_tf1
float _l1_liqStrength   = liqScr_tf1

int   fam_l1raw = f_phaseFamilyCode(int(nz(se15_ph)))
float l1_waveProgress      = nz(se15_wp)
float l1_convexityMaturity = nz(se15_cm)
float l1_modelFit          = nz(se15_mf)
string l1_dominantPhase    = f_famSimple(fam_l1raw)
var float l1_confidence = 50.0
float _l1_confRaw = nz(se15_mf)
l1_confidence := l1_confidence + 0.4 * (_l1_confRaw - l1_confidence)
l1_confidence := math.max(10.0, math.min(100.0, l1_confidence))
string l1_prediction =
     l1_dominantPhase == "Expansion"     ? "Pre-Convexity" :
     l1_dominantPhase == "Pre-Convexity" ? "Liquidity"     :
     l1_dominantPhase == "Liquidity"     ? "Absorption"    : "Expansion"

float _l2_expStrength   = expScr_tf2
float _l2_decStrength   = decScr_tf2
float _l2_absStrength   = abScr_tf2
float _l2_liqStrength   = liqScr_tf2

int   fam_l2raw = f_phaseFamilyCode(int(nz(se60_ph)))
float l2_waveProgress      = nz(se60_wp)
float l2_convexityMaturity = nz(se60_cm)
float l2_modelFit          = nz(se60_mf)
string l2_dominantPhase    = f_famSimple(fam_l2raw)
var float l2_confidence = 50.0
float _l2_confRaw = nz(se60_mf)
l2_confidence := l2_confidence + 0.4 * (_l2_confRaw - l2_confidence)
l2_confidence := math.max(10.0, math.min(100.0, l2_confidence))
string l2_prediction =
     l2_dominantPhase == "Expansion"     ? "Pre-Convexity" :
     l2_dominantPhase == "Pre-Convexity" ? "Liquidity"     :
     l2_dominantPhase == "Liquidity"     ? "Absorption"    : "Expansion"

// L3 — now the M3 fixed-tf structure engine (previously bound to M1 physics).
int   fam_l3raw = f_phaseFamilyCode(int(nz(se3_ph)))
int   _l3_signals =
     (m1ExpansionWeak  ? 1 : 0) +
     (m1ConvexityEmer  ? 1 : 0) +
     (m1LiquidityEmer  ? 1 : 0) +
     (m1AbsorptionEmer ? 1 : 0)
float l3_waveProgress      = nz(se3_wp)
float l3_convexityMaturity = nz(se3_cm)
float l3_modelFit          = nz(se3_mf)
string l3_dominantPhase    = f_famMicro(fam_l3raw)
float l3_confidence        = math.max(10.0, math.min(100.0, nz(se3_mf)))
string l3_prediction   =
     l3_dominantPhase == "M1 Convexity"  ? "M1 Liquidity"  :
     l3_dominantPhase == "M1 Liquidity"  ? "M1 Absorption" :
     l3_dominantPhase == "M1 Absorption" ? "M1 Expansion"  : "M1 Convexity"

// ── P3-7: WAVE AGREEMENT ENGINE (f_phaseFamily moved here — used in P3-2 and P3-4) ──────────

// f_phaseFamily: maps both old hypothesis vocabulary AND canonical IE1A phases
// to lifecycle family integers (used by agreement / fractal confidence engines).
f_phaseFamily(string ph) =>
    int family = 0
    // Old hypothesis vocabulary (L1/L2/L3 belief layers)
    if ph == "EXPANSION" or ph == "Expansion"
        family := 1
    else if ph == "CONVEXITY FORMING" or ph == "Pre-Convexity" or ph == "Liquidity"
        family := 2
    else if ph == "CREATION FORMING"
        family := 3
    else if ph == "ABSORPTION" or ph == "Absorption"
        family := 4
    else if ph == "RETRACEMENT"
        family := 5
    else if ph == "DEMAND/SUPPLY RETURN"
        family := 6
    // Canonical IE1A lifecycle phases
    else if ph == "Point 4 Origin"
        family := 0
    else if ph == "Expansion"
        family := 1
    else if ph == "Expansion Pre-Convexity" or ph == "Expansion Induction" or ph == "Expansion Liquidity"
        family := 2
    else if ph == "New High" or ph == "New Low"
        family := 3
    else if ph == "Absorption"
        family := 4
    else if ph == "Retracement" or ph == "Retracement Pre-Convexity" or ph == "Retracement Induction" or ph == "Retracement Liquidity"
        family := 5
    else if ph == "Demand Return" or ph == "Supply Return"
        family := 6
    family

// L0/L1/L2 lifecycle families now come from the FIXED-tf engines (v90).
// Previously fam_l0 used chart-tf ie1a_currentPhase — that was a chart-tf leak.
int fam_l0 = f_phaseFamilyCode(int(nz(se5_ph)))
int fam_l1 = f_phaseFamilyCode(int(nz(se15_ph)))
int fam_l2 = f_phaseFamilyCode(int(nz(se60_ph)))

// ── P3-2: PARENT-CHILD RELATIONSHIP ENGINE ────────────────────────────────────

string parentState      = l2_dominantPhase
string childState       = l1_dominantPhase
string grandchildState  = l0_dominantPhase

bool parentChildHarmonic =
     (parentState == "Expansion" and childState == "Pre-Convexity") or
     (parentState == "Expansion" and childState == "Liquidity")      or
     (parentState == "Pre-Convexity" and childState == "Liquidity")  or
     (parentState == "Liquidity" and childState == "Absorption")     or
     (parentState == "Absorption" and childState == "Expansion")

// childGrandchildHarmonic: uses fam_l0 (IE1A family) for L0 comparisons,
// so both old hypothesis vocabulary and canonical IE1A phases are handled correctly.
bool childGrandchildHarmonic =
     (childState == "Expansion" and (fam_l0 == 1 or fam_l0 == 2)) or
     (childState == "Pre-Convexity" and (fam_l0 == 2 or fam_l0 == 3)) or
     (childState == "Liquidity" and (fam_l0 == 4 or fam_l0 == 5)) or
     (childState == "Absorption" and fam_l0 == 6)

string parentChildRelationship =
     parentChildHarmonic      ? "Harmonic"  :
     parentState == childState ? "Parallel"  : "Counter"

string childGrandchildRelationship =
     childGrandchildHarmonic              ? "Harmonic"  :
     childState == "Expansion" and
     childState == "Expansion" and fam_l0 == 6 ? "Counter-Within-Parent" : "Nested" 

// ── P3-3: WAVE DOMINANCE ENGINE ───────────────────────────────────────────────

float l0_dominance = math.min(
     (nz(se5_wp)  * 0.45) +
     (nz(se5_mf)  * 0.35) +
     (nz(se5_cm)  * 0.20),
     100.0)

float l1_dominance = math.min(
     (_l1_expStrength * 0.35) +
     (expScr_tf1 > 60 ? 25.0 : expScr_tf1 * 0.40) +
     (liqScr_tf1 * 0.20) +
     (l1_modelFit * 0.20),
     100.0)

float l2_dominance = math.min(
     (_l2_expStrength * 0.35) +
     (expScr_tf2 > 60 ? 30.0 : expScr_tf2 * 0.50) +
     (liqScr_tf2 * 0.15) +
     (l2_modelFit * 0.20),
     100.0)

float l3_dominance = math.min(nz(se3_mf) * 0.60 + nz(se3_wp) * 0.40, 100.0)

string dominantWaveLevel =
     l2_dominance >= l1_dominance and l2_dominance >= l0_dominance and l2_dominance >= l3_dominance ? "L2 HTF"    :
     l1_dominance >= l0_dominance and l1_dominance >= l3_dominance                                  ? "L1 CHILD"  :
     l0_dominance >= l3_dominance                                                                    ? "L0 PRIMARY" : "L3 MICRO"

// ── P3-4: MULTI-TIMEFRAME WAVE FUSION LAYER ──────────────────────────────────

bool htfTrendIntact     = l2_dominantPhase == "Expansion" and l2_confidence > 45.0

// ltfReversalForming: uses fam_l0 for L0 so canonical IE1A phases are recognised.
bool ltfReversalForming =
     ((fam_l0 == 4 or fam_l0 == 5) or
     (l3_dominantPhase == "M1 Absorption" or l3_dominantPhase == "M1 Liquidity"))
     and not (liqg_active and not (liqg_objArrival and liqg_trueCHoCH))

string fusionInterpretation =
     htfTrendIntact and not ltfReversalForming  ? "HTF Intact — LTF Expansion Aligned"        :
     htfTrendIntact and ltfReversalForming       ? "HTF Intact — LTF Reversal Forming"          :
     not htfTrendIntact and ltfReversalForming   ? "HTF Weakening — LTF Reversal Confirming"    :
     l2_dominantPhase == "Absorption" and
     l1_dominantPhase == "Expansion"             ? "HTF Absorption — ITF Counter-Bounce"        :
     l2_dominantPhase == "Liquidity" and
     (l1_dominantPhase == "Absorption" or
      fam_l0 == 5)                               ? "HTF Liq Sweep — Entry Zone Forming"         :
                                                   "Mixed — Await Alignment"

float fusionConfidence = math.min(
     l2_confidence * 0.40 + l1_confidence * 0.30 +
     l0_confidence * 0.20 + l3_confidence * 0.10,
     100.0)

// ── P3-5: RECURSIVE ENTRY CYCLE ENGINE ───────────────────────────────────────

float _cycleBaseProg = nz(waveProgress, 0.0)

float cycle1_completion = math.min(
     (entryCycle >= 1 ? 60.0 : _cycleBaseProg * 0.60) +
     (recursiveComplete and entryCycle >= 1 ? 40.0 : 0.0), 100.0)

float cycle2_completion = math.min(
     (entryCycle >= 2 ? 60.0 : entryCycle >= 1 ? _cycleBaseProg * 0.40 : 0.0) +
     (recursiveComplete and entryCycle >= 2 ? 40.0 : 0.0), 100.0)

float cycle3_completion = math.min(
     (entryCycle >= 3 ? 60.0 : entryCycle >= 2 ? _cycleBaseProg * 0.40 : 0.0) +
     (recursiveComplete and entryCycle >= 3 ? 40.0 : 0.0), 100.0)

float cycle4_completion = math.min(
     (entryCycle >= 4 ? 60.0 : entryCycle >= 3 ? _cycleBaseProg * 0.40 : 0.0) +
     (recursiveComplete and entryCycle >= 4 ? 40.0 : 0.0), 100.0)

// activeCyclePhase — uses ENGINE 1A canonical phase (ie1a_currentPhase).
// grandchildState still carries the ie1a_hypFamily vocabulary for L0 agreement/fusion;
// the human-readable cycle label uses the canonical IE1A phase string.
string activeCyclePhase =
     entryCycle == 0 ?
          ("Cycle 1 — " + l0_phaseCanon) :
     "Entry Cycle " + str.tostring(entryCycle) + " — " + l0_phaseCanon

// ── P3-6: GEOMETRIC CAPACITY ENGINE ──────────────────────────────────────────

float geoCapacityScore = math.min(
     (geoFullConvexityPossible    ? 100.0 :
      geoPartialConvexityPossible ? 60.0  : 25.0) *
     (not na(flipzoneWidth) ? math.max(0.5, 1.0 - flipzoneWidth / math.max(atr * 4.0, 1e-10)) : 0.5),
     100.0)

string geoCapacityNarrative =
     geoFullConvexityPossible    ? "Full Conv — Complete wave expression" :
     geoPartialConvexityPossible ? "Partial Conv — Limited but tradeable" :
                                   "Absorption Only — Expect rapid absorption"

float geoRemainingFraction = not na(availableSpace) ? availableSpace / 100.0 : 0.5

// ── P3-7: WAVE AGREEMENT ENGINE ──────────────────────────────────────────────
// f_phaseFamily and fam_l0/fam_l1/fam_l2 are declared before P3-2 above.

// ─── UNIFIED WAVE CLASSIFIER (V71 REFACTOR) ───────────────────────────────────
// Single shared classifier used by L0 / L1 / L2 / L3 / Entry Cycles.
// Returns ONLY:
//   targetWave   = "Bullish Wave" | "Bearish Wave"
//   currentPhase = one canonical Unified Wave Lifecycle phase
//
// Canonical lifecycle phases (only these may appear in display):
//   Point 4 Origin | Expansion | Expansion Pre-Convexity | Expansion Induction
//   Expansion Liquidity | New High | New Low | Absorption | Retracement
//   Retracement Pre-Convexity | Retracement Induction | Retracement Liquidity
//   Demand Return | Supply Return
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// f_toCanonicalPhase and f_classifyWave are defined earlier (after primaryHypothesisConf)
// so that l0_targetWave / l0_currentPhase are in scope for all sections that use them.
// L0 is already computed there. Only L1/L2/L3 are classified here where their inputs exist.

// ── Determine expansion-side for L1 / L2 / L3 ────────────────────────────────
bool _l1_expSide = l1_dominantPhase == "Expansion" or l1_dominantPhase == "Pre-Convexity" or l1_dominantPhase == "Liquidity"
bool _l2_expSide = l2_dominantPhase == "Expansion" or l2_dominantPhase == "Pre-Convexity" or l2_dominantPhase == "Liquidity"
bool _l3_expSide = l3_dominantPhase == "M1 Expansion" or l3_dominantPhase == "M1 Exp Weak" or l3_dominantPhase == "M1 Convexity" or l3_dominantPhase == "M1 Liquidity"

// ── Run classifier for L1 / L2 / L3 — directions from FIXED engines (v90) ────
[l1_targetWave, l1_currentPhase] = f_classifyWave(l1_dominantPhase, l1_dir, _l1_expSide)
[l2_targetWave, l2_currentPhase] = f_classifyWave(l2_dominantPhase, l2_dir, _l2_expSide)
[l3_targetWave, l3_currentPhase] = f_classifyWave(l3_dominantPhase, l3_dir, _l3_expSide)

// waveProgressCanonical — now sourced directly from ENGINE 1A.
// ENGINE 1A is the sole lifecycle authority; score-based thresholds are prohibited
// from assigning lifecycle phase.  waveProgress remains available as a confidence
// signal for downstream engines but does not determine canonical phase.
string waveProgressCanonical = l0_phaseCanon   // L0 = M5 fixed-tf structure (v90)

string waveProgressDirLabel = waveProgressCanonical

f_agreementScore(int a, int b) =>
    int diff = math.abs(a - b)
    if diff == 0
        100
    else if diff == 1
        65
    else if diff == 2
        35
    else
        10

float waveAgreement_l0l1 = f_agreementScore(fam_l0, fam_l1)
float waveAgreement_l1l2 = f_agreementScore(fam_l1, fam_l2)
float waveAgreement_l0l2 = f_agreementScore(fam_l0, fam_l2)

float waveAgreement =
     math.min(
         waveAgreement_l0l1 * 0.40 +
         waveAgreement_l1l2 * 0.35 +
         waveAgreement_l0l2 * 0.25,
         100.0)

string waveAgreementLabel =
     waveAgreement >= 85 ? "High Agreement" :
     waveAgreement >= 60 ? "Moderate Agreement" :
     waveAgreement >= 35 ? "Low Agreement" : "Counter Wave"

// ── P3-8: FRACTAL CONFIDENCE ENGINE ──────────────────────────────────────────

float _agreeBoost = (waveAgreement - 50.0) / 100.0

float fractalConfidence = math.max(10.0, math.min(100.0,
     l2_confidence * 0.35 +
     l1_confidence * 0.30 +
     l0_confidence * 0.25 +
     l3_confidence * 0.10 +
     _agreeBoost * 15.0))

string fractalConfLabel =
     fractalConfidence >= 80 ? "Exceptional" :
     fractalConfidence >= 65 ? "Strong"       :
     fractalConfidence >= 45 ? "Moderate"     : "Weak"

// ── P3-9: WAVE NARRATIVE ENGINE ───────────────────────────────────────────────
// Unified Wave Lifecycle — every row uses:
//   "What Wave Price Is Trying To Make: <targetWave>"
//   "Current Phase Within Curve Cycle: <currentPhase>"

string narr_primary   = l0_targetWave + " | " + currentDisplayPhase
string narr_child     = l1_targetWave + " | " + l1_currentPhase
string narr_grandchild = l2_targetWave + " | " + l2_currentPhase
string narr_micro     = l3_targetWave + " | " + l3_currentPhase
string narr_m1        = m1_dirLabel + " | " + m1_phaseCanon
string narr_l4        = l4_dirLabel + " | " + l4_phaseCanon

string narr_outcome =
     fusionInterpretation == "HTF Intact — LTF Reversal Forming" ?
          "Likely: " + l0_prediction + " then continuation"  :
     fusionInterpretation == "HTF Weakening — LTF Reversal Confirming"  ?
          "Likely: Structural Reversal Forming"              :
     fusionInterpretation == "HTF Liq Sweep — Entry Zone Forming"  ?
          "Likely: Entry Cycle " + str.tostring(math.min(entryCycle + 1, 4)) :
          "Likely: " + l0_prediction

// ── P3-10: EXECUTION PROBABILITY ENGINE V2 ───────────────────────────────────

// v90: rewired to the FIXED-tf fractal stack and made direction-/conflict-aware.
// HTF bias = H1 + H4 ; LTF bias = M1 + M3 + M5.  When the LTF stack turns against
// the HTF stack, Continuation collapses and Reversal/Absorption rise — this is the
// "M1 turning counter to HTF" case that previously left the panel pinned.
int   _ep_htfSum  = l2_dir + l4_dir
int   _ep_htfBias = _ep_htfSum > 0 ? 1 : _ep_htfSum < 0 ? -1 : 0
int   _ep_ltfSum  = m1_dir + l3_dir + l0_dir
int   _ep_ltfBias = _ep_ltfSum > 0 ? 1 : _ep_ltfSum < 0 ? -1 : 0
bool  _ep_aligned  = _ep_htfBias != 0 and _ep_ltfBias == _ep_htfBias
bool  _ep_conflict = _ep_htfBias != 0 and _ep_ltfBias == -_ep_htfBias
float _ep_consensus = math.max(_stackBull, _stackBear) / 6.0 * 100.0
bool  _ep_absL3 = l3_dominantPhase == "M1 Absorption" or l3_dominantPhase == "M1 Liquidity"

float execProb_Continuation = math.max(0.0, math.min(
     (_ep_aligned ? 40.0 : 0.0) +
     (_ep_aligned and l2_dominantPhase == "Expansion" ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (htfTrendIntact and not ltfReversalForming ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     (_ep_consensus * 0.25) -
     (_ep_conflict ? 55.0 : 0.0) -
     (ltfReversalForming ? 15.0 : 0.0),
     100.0))

float execProb_Reversal = math.min(
     (_ep_conflict ? 35.0 : 0.0) +
     (ltfReversalForming ? 25.0 : 0.0) +
     (_ep_absL3 ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     (convexityMaturity > 60 ? convexityMaturity * 0.15 : 0.0) +
     (waveAgreement < 45 ? (45.0 - waveAgreement) * 0.40 : 0.0),
     100.0)

float execProb_Expansion = math.min(
     (_ep_aligned and (l0_dominantPhase == "Expansion" or l1_dominantPhase == "Expansion") ? 35.0 : 0.0) +
     (_ep_aligned ? _ep_consensus * 0.25 : 0.0) +
     (htfTrendIntact ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     (liqSweepBull or liqSweepBear ? 15.0 : 0.0),
     100.0)

float execProb_Creation = math.min(
     (predScore_Creation * 0.45) +
     (geoCapacityScore * 0.20) +
     (m1LiquidityEmer ? 15.0 : 0.0) +
     (l3_dominantPhase == "M1 Liquidity" ? 15.0 : 0.0),
     100.0)

float execProb_Absorption = math.min(
     (predScore_Absorption * 0.45) +
     (m1AbsorptionEmer ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (l3_dominantPhase == "M1 Absorption" ? 20.0 : 0.0) +
     (_ep_conflict ? 15.0 : 0.0),
     100.0)

float execProb_StandDown = math.min(
     (_ep_htfBias == 0 ? 30.0 : 0.0) +
     (fractalStackDir == 0 ? 25.0 : 0.0) +
     (waveAgreement < 35 ? (35.0 - waveAgreement) * 1.20 : 0.0) +
     (physicsConsensus < 30 ? 20.0 : 0.0),
     100.0)

// Engine 1A.7 / authority gate: while the objective-completion wave is in progress,
// the objective is NOT yet reached — suppress reversal/absorption probability and
// raise Stand Down. Once the objective has ARRIVED, the turn is at hand → boost reversal.
if liqg_active and not (liqg_objArrival and liqg_trueCHoCH)
    execProb_Reversal   := execProb_Reversal   * 0.4
    execProb_Absorption := execProb_Absorption * 0.4
    execProb_StandDown  := math.min(100.0, execProb_StandDown + 15.0)
if liqg_objArrival
    execProb_Reversal   := math.min(100.0, execProb_Reversal + 25.0)

float execMaxProb = math.max(execProb_Continuation, execProb_Reversal,
     execProb_Expansion, execProb_Creation, execProb_Absorption, execProb_StandDown)

string execDirective =
     (liqg_active and not (liqg_objArrival and liqg_trueCHoCH)) ? "AWAIT OBJECTIVE — LIQUIDATION WAVE" :
     execProb_StandDown  >= 55                      ? "STAND DOWN — NO ALIGNMENT"            :
     _ep_conflict and execProb_Reversal >= 45       ? "TRANSITION — LTF COUNTER HTF"         :
     execProb_Absorption == execMaxProb             ? "ABSORPTION — PREPARE REVERSAL"        :
     execProb_Reversal   == execMaxProb             ? "REVERSAL PROBABILITY DOMINANT"        :
     execProb_Creation   == execMaxProb             ? "NEW HIGH / NEW LOW FORMING"           :
     execProb_Expansion  == execMaxProb             ? "EXPANSION ENTRY FORMING"              :
     execProb_Continuation == execMaxProb           ? "CONTINUATION — HOLD / TRAIL"          : "AWAIT ALIGNMENT"

// ── P3-D: PHASE 3 DASHBOARD PANEL (bottom_left) ──────────────────────────────

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// PHASE 3 DASHBOARD — wrapped in function to satisfy body-length limit
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ── Phase 3 high-conviction alert ─────────────────────────────────────────────
// ── Dashboard & P3 render calls ─────────────────────────────────────────────
f_renderDashP3() =>
    if showTable
        var table dashP3 = table.new(position.bottom_center, 4, 32,
             bgcolor=color.new(#0a0a12, 5),
             border_color=color.new(color.white, 30), border_width=1,
             frame_color=color.new(color.white, 20), frame_width=1)
        int _rpL = 1
        int _rpR = 1
        if showDP3_Narrative
            f_sep(dashP3, _rpL, "WAVE NARRATIVE", _ts)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 0, _rpL, "M1", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 1, _rpL, narr_m1, text_color=color.gray, text_size=_szA)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 0, _rpL, "M3", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 1, _rpL, narr_micro, text_color=color.new(#c084fc, 0), text_size=_szA)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 0, _rpL, "M5", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 1, _rpL, narr_primary, text_color=color.lime, text_size=_szA)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 0, _rpL, "M15", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 1, _rpL, narr_child, text_color=color.aqua, text_size=_szA)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 0, _rpL, "H1", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 1, _rpL, narr_grandchild, text_color=color.yellow, text_size=_szA)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 0, _rpL, "H4", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 1, _rpL, narr_l4, text_color=color.new(color.orange, 0), text_size=_szA)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 0, _rpL, "Outcome", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 1, _rpL, narr_outcome, text_color=color.white, text_size=_szA)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 0, _rpL, "Fractal Conf", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 1, _rpL, str.tostring(math.round(fractalConfidence)) + "%  " + fractalConfLabel, text_color=f_sc(fractalConfidence), text_size=_szA)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
        if showDP3_Fusion
            f_sep(dashP3, _rpL, "MTF FUSION LAYER", _ts)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 0, _rpL, "Fusion Interp", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 1, _rpL, fusionInterpretation, text_color=htfTrendIntact ? color.lime : color.orange, text_size=_szA)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 0, _rpL, "Fusion Conf", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 1, _rpL, str.tostring(math.round(fusionConfidence)) + "%", text_color=f_sc(fusionConfidence), text_size=_szA)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 0, _rpL, "HTF Trend", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 1, _rpL, htfTrendIntact ? "Intact" : "Weakening", text_color=htfTrendIntact ? color.lime : color.orange, text_size=_szA)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 0, _rpL, "LTF Reversal", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 1, _rpL, ltfReversalForming ? "Forming" : "Not yet", text_color=ltfReversalForming ? color.orange : color.gray, text_size=_szA)
            _rpL := _rpL + 1
        if showDP3_ExecProb
            f_sep2(dashP3, _rpR, "EXECUTION PROBABILITY V2", _ts)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 2, _rpR, "Exec Directive", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 3, _rpR, execDirective, text_color=execProb_StandDown >= 60 ? color.red : color.white, text_size=_szA)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 2, _rpR, "Continuation", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 3, _rpR, str.tostring(math.round(execProb_Continuation)) + "%", text_color=f_sc(execProb_Continuation), text_size=_szA)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 2, _rpR, "Reversal", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 3, _rpR, str.tostring(math.round(execProb_Reversal)) + "%", text_color=f_sc(execProb_Reversal), text_size=_szA)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 2, _rpR, "Expansion", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 3, _rpR, str.tostring(math.round(execProb_Expansion)) + "%", text_color=f_sc(execProb_Expansion), text_size=_szA)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 2, _rpR, "New High / New Low", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 3, _rpR, str.tostring(math.round(execProb_Creation)) + "%", text_color=f_sc(execProb_Creation), text_size=_szA)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 2, _rpR, "Absorption", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 3, _rpR, str.tostring(math.round(execProb_Absorption)) + "%", text_color=f_sc(execProb_Absorption), text_size=_szA)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 2, _rpR, "Stand Down", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            table.cell(dashP3, 3, _rpR, str.tostring(math.round(execProb_StandDown)) + "%", text_color=execProb_StandDown >= 60 ? color.red : f_sc(100 - execProb_StandDown), text_size=_szA)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
        if showDP3_WaveProgress
            f_sep2(dashP3, _rpR, "MULTI-LEVEL WAVE PROGRESS", _ts)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 2, _rpR, "M1", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            float _p1 = nz(f_tfProg(se1_inv, se1_tgt), nz(se1_wp))
            table.cell(dashP3, 3, _rpR, m1_phaseCanon + "  " + f_mosBar(_p1) + " " + str.tostring(math.round(_p1)) + "%", text_color=color.gray, text_size=_szA)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 2, _rpR, "M3", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            float _p3 = nz(f_tfProg(se3_inv, se3_tgt), nz(l3_waveProgress))
            table.cell(dashP3, 3, _rpR, l3_phaseCanon + "  " + f_mosBar(_p3) + " " + str.tostring(math.round(_p3)) + "%", text_color=color.new(#c084fc, 0), text_size=_szA)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 2, _rpR, "M5", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            float _m5Prog = phaseProgress
            table.cell(dashP3, 3, _rpR, currentDisplayPhase + "  " + f_mosBar(_m5Prog) + " " + str.tostring(math.round(_m5Prog)) + "%", text_color=color.lime, text_size=_szA)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 2, _rpR, "M15", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            float _p15 = nz(f_tfProg(se15_inv, se15_tgt), nz(l1_waveProgress))
            table.cell(dashP3, 3, _rpR, l1_phaseCanon + "  " + f_mosBar(_p15) + " " + str.tostring(math.round(_p15)) + "%", text_color=color.aqua, text_size=_szA)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 2, _rpR, "H1", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            float _p60 = nz(f_tfProg(se60_inv, se60_tgt), nz(l2_waveProgress))
            table.cell(dashP3, 3, _rpR, l2_phaseCanon + "  " + f_mosBar(_p60) + " " + str.tostring(math.round(_p60)) + "%", text_color=color.yellow, text_size=_szA)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1
            table.cell(dashP3, 2, _rpR, "H4", text_color=color.silver, text_size=_szA)
            float _p240 = nz(f_tfProg(se240_inv, se240_tgt), nz(se240_wp))
            table.cell(dashP3, 3, _rpR, l4_phaseCanon + "  " + f_mosBar(_p240) + " " + str.tostring(math.round(_p240)) + "%", text_color=color.new(color.orange, 0), text_size=_szA)
            _rpR := _rpR + 1

f_renderDashP3()

bool p3_highConvictionSetup =
     fractalConfidence > 68 and
     waveAgreement > 70 and
     execProb_StandDown < 35 and
     direction != 0 and
     (execProb_Expansion > 50 or execProb_Continuation > 50 or execProb_Creation > 50)

alertcondition(p3_highConvictionSetup,
     title="P3 — High-Conviction Recursive Setup",
     message="SYMPHONY v68 RWI: Fractal confluence detected.")


// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PHASE 1 — WAVE TRACEABILITY v3
// DASHBOARD ↔ CHART LINKAGE — TRUE STRUCTURAL ANCHORING
//
// SPEC COMPLIANCE:
//   Every label attaches to the ACTUAL structure producing the calculation.
//   No future-space boxes. No synthetic structures. No new pivots.
//
// SOURCE MAPPING (audit result):
//   L2 HTF  → expScr_tf2/decScr_tf2/abScr_tf2/liqScr_tf2 via request.security(tf2)
//              Price range: l2_zoneHigh / l2_zoneLow  (highest/lowest 20 bars on tf2)
//              Origin: left edge = bar_index - 20 equivalent; no fixed origin bar exists.
//              Solution: box spans l2_zoneHigh/l2_zoneLow across the last 20 current-TF
//              bars that contain the tf2 20-bar range window, anchored left at the
//              bar where that range began.
//
//   L1 CHILD → expScr_tf1/decScr_tf1/abScr_tf1/liqScr_tf1 via request.security(tf1)
//              Price range: l1_zoneHigh / l1_zoneLow  (highest/lowest 20 bars on tf1)
//
//   L0 PRIMARY → waveProgress / convexityMaturity / primaryHypothesis (current TF)
//              Origin: point4OriginBar / point4OriginHigh / point4OriginLow (exact)
//              Zone: point4OriginBar → bar_index (the actual wave span)
//
//   L3 GRANDCHILD → m1AbsorptionEmer/m1LiquidityEmer/m1ConvexityEmer/m1ExpansionWeak
//              Price range: l3_zoneHigh / l3_zoneLow  (highest/lowest 20 bars on "1")
//
// HIERARCHY NESTING RULE (visual):
//   L2 HTF  → outermost zone (widest price range — drawn behind all others)
//   L0 Primary → spans from its origin bar to now (inside L2)
//   L1 Child   → tf1 range (inside L0 conceptually)
//   L3 Grandchild → narrowest / M1 range (innermost)
//
// ORIGIN LABELS:
//   L0: label at point4OriginBar (exact existing variable)
//   L2/L1/L3: label at bar_index (left/right edge of zone — no fake origin bars)
//
// DOMINANT WAVE: drawn ON the dominant structure's zone mid-price.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

var string GRP_TRACE = "Wave Traceability (Phase 1)"
showTraceZones  = input.bool(true,  "Show Wave Traceability Zones (on-chart)", group=GRP_TRACE)
showL0Zone      = input.bool(true,  "Show L0 Primary Origin Zone",             group=GRP_TRACE)
showDominantTag = input.bool(true,  "Show Dominant Wave Tag",                  group=GRP_TRACE)
showOriginPins  = input.bool(true,  "Show Origin Anchor Pins",                 group=GRP_TRACE)

// ── Colour scheme: mirrors P3 dashboard colour-coding exactly ────────────────
//   narr_primary (L0)  = lime    ← matches "Primary Wave" rows
//   narr_child   (L1)  = aqua    ← matches "Child Wave" rows
//   narr_grandchild (L2) = yellow  ← matches "HTF Structure" rows
//   narr_micro   (L3)  = purple  ← matches "M1 Sensor" rows
color trace_L2_col = color.yellow             // L2 HTF
color trace_L0_col = color.lime               // L0 Primary
color trace_L1_col = color.aqua               // L1 Child
color trace_L3_col = color.new(#c084fc, 0)    // L3 Grandchild (M3)
color trace_H4_col = color.orange             // H4 — highest context
color trace_M1_col = color.new(#9aa4b2, 0)    // M1 — finest micro

// ── Persistent drawing objects ───────────────────────────────────────────────
var box   l2ZoneBox     = na  // L2 HTF zone (outermost — tf2 price range)
var box   l0ZoneBox     = na  // L0 Primary zone (origin → now)
var box   l1ZoneBox     = na  // L1 Child zone (tf1 price range)
var box   l3ZoneBox     = na  // L3 Grandchild zone (M3 price range)
var box   m1ZoneBox     = na  // M1 zone (innermost — M1 price range)
var box   l4ZoneBox     = na  // H4 zone (outermost — H4 price range)

var label l2ZoneLbl     = na  // L2 label at zone top-left
var label l0ZoneLbl     = na  // L0 label at origin bar
var label l1ZoneLbl     = na  // L1 label at zone top-left (symmetric with L2/H4)
var label l3ZoneLbl     = na  // L3 label at zone top-right
var label m1ZoneLbl     = na  // M1 label at zone mid
var label l4ZoneLbl     = na  // H4 label at zone top-left
var label l0OriginPin   = na  // L0 origin anchor pin
var label dominantLabel = na  // Dominant wave tag on dominant structure

// ── Helper: midpoint of a price range ───────────────────────────────────────
f_mid(float h, float l) => (h + l) / 2.0

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ZONE SIZING — RIGHT-OF-PRICE BAND MARKERS
//
// L2/L1/L3 are HTF price ranges. Their VALUE is the price band (zoneHigh/zoneLow).
// Their TIME span on the current-TF chart is NOT meaningful — multiplying TF
// ratios by bar counts produces a span of hundreds of current-TF bars, which
// overlaps L0 and every other structure.  That was the root cause of the
// "L2 box looks like L0" problem seen in the screenshot.
//
// CORRECT APPROACH: draw each HTF zone as a narrow vertical BAND just to the
// right of the last bar, at the correct PRICE LEVEL (zoneHigh/zoneLow).
// Stacked by hierarchy width:
//   L2 HTF        → outermost  (bar_index+3 to bar_index+18)
//   L1 CHILD      → middle     (bar_index+3 to bar_index+12)
//   L3 GRANDCHILD → innermost  (bar_index+3 to bar_index+7)
//
// L0 PRIMARY continues to span from point4OriginBar → bar_index (unchanged).
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

int _l2R_far  = bar_index + 18   // L2 HTF  — rightmost, widest
int _l2R_near = bar_index + 3
int _l1R_far  = bar_index + 12   // L1 Child — middle
int _l1R_near = bar_index + 3
int _l3R_far  = bar_index + 7    // L3 Grandchild — narrowest
int _l3R_near = bar_index + 3
int _h4R_far  = bar_index + 24   // H4 — outermost (highest context)
int _h4R_near = bar_index + 3
int _m1R_far  = bar_index + 5    // M1 — innermost (finest micro)
int _m1R_near = bar_index + 3

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ENGINE 1A.3A — SPATIAL PHASE LOCALIZATION (additive; chart-scope labels)
// Pre-Convexity and Induction are LOCATIONS, not BOS events:
//  · Pre-Convexity = the initial-displacement leg challenging the prior objective
//    (price has covered most of the origin→target span with momentum slowing).
//  · Induction     = price re-entering the flip-zone inducement area — the trap
//    where early traders are enticed — born from flipzoneInducPrice.
// Labels anchor to those zones, fire once per M5 wave, never at a BOS event.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
var int  sp_waveBar     = na
var bool sp_preConvDone = false
var bool sp_inducDone   = false
if point4OriginBar != sp_waveBar
    sp_waveBar     := point4OriginBar
    sp_preConvDone := false
    sp_inducDone   := false
// Pre-Convexity = the initial displacement breaking the PREVIOUS swing it attacks
// (per spec: "near or once the previous swing is broken"). Anchored at the break.
bool _spPrevBreak = direction == -1 ? (not na(prevSwingLow) and close < prevSwingLow) : direction == 1 ? (not na(prevSwingHigh) and close > prevSwingHigh) : false
if showTraceZones and not sp_preConvDone and direction != 0 and _spPrevBreak
    label.new(bar_index, direction == 1 ? high : low, "Pre-Convexity",
         style=direction == 1 ? label.style_label_down : label.style_label_up,
         color=color.new(#5a9cff, 15), textcolor=color.white, size=size.normal)
    sp_preConvDone := true
// V73.8 TIGHT FU CANDLE → INDUCTION. The FU candle is a SPIKE that sweeps prior
// structure then SELF-DESTRUCTS (body closes back through the candle). The spike
// (the "FU") IS the flip zone. Bull FU (demand): a long LOWER spike sweeps a prior
// swing low and the body closes in the upper half → spike zone [low, body-bottom].
// Bear FU (supply): mirror. Induction = price entering the OPPOSING FU spike zone.
var float fux_bullTop = na
var float fux_bullBot = na
var float fux_bearTop = na
var float fux_bearBot = na
float _fuMid2 = (high + low) / 2.0
if (high - low) > atr * 0.6 and (math.min(open, close) - low) >= (high - low) * 0.5 and close > _fuMid2 and not na(prevSwingLow) and low < prevSwingLow and close > prevSwingLow
    fux_bullTop := math.min(open, close)
    fux_bullBot := low
if (high - low) > atr * 0.6 and (high - math.max(open, close)) >= (high - low) * 0.5 and close < _fuMid2 and not na(prevSwingHigh) and high > prevSwingHigh and close < prevSwingHigh
    fux_bearTop := high
    fux_bearBot := math.max(open, close)
float _indTop = direction == -1 ? fux_bullTop : direction == 1 ? fux_bearTop : na
float _indBot = direction == -1 ? fux_bullBot : direction == 1 ? fux_bearBot : na
if showTraceZones and not sp_inducDone and direction != 0 and not na(_indTop) and high >= _indBot and low <= _indTop
    label.new(bar_index, (_indTop + _indBot) / 2.0, "Induction",
         style=direction == 1 ? label.style_label_up : label.style_label_down,
         color=color.new(#ffd000, 20), textcolor=color.black, size=size.small)
    sp_inducDone := true

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PHASE 1-A  L2 HTF TRACEABILITY
// Structure: the 60-minute (tf2) wave being measured.
// Zone: the actual price range on tf2 that produced expScr_tf2/decScr_tf2 etc.
//       = l2_zoneHigh / l2_zoneLow, spanning the equivalent number of current
//         bars that represent 20 × tf2 bars.
// Label text mirrors the dashboard "L2 (HTF) Progress" row exactly.
// Origin pin: at the left edge of the zone (oldest bar in the 20-bar tf2 window)
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PHASE 1-AA  H4 CONTEXT TRACEABILITY
// Outermost band at the real H4 ("240") price level. Direction is H4's OWN
// origin-based wave direction (l4_dir); phase is the H4 fixed-tf lifecycle.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ── PHASE 1-AA  H4 CONTEXT TRACEABILITY ─────────────────────────────────────
// Outermost context label at the real H4 ("240") swing high. Direction is H4's
// OWN origin-based wave (l4_dir -> l4_dirLabel); phase is the H4 fixed-tf cycle.
if showTraceZones and barstate.islast and not na(l4_swH)
    string _l4txt = "H4 · " + l4_dirLabel + " · " + l4_phaseCanon
    if na(l4ZoneLbl)
        l4ZoneLbl := label.new(_h4R_near, l4_swH, _l4txt,
             style=label.style_label_left, color=color.new(#10103a, 10),
             textcolor=trace_H4_col, size=size.small, textalign=text.align_left)
    else
        label.set_xy  (l4ZoneLbl, _h4R_near, l4_swH)
        label.set_text(l4ZoneLbl, _l4txt)

// ── PHASE 1-A  L2 HTF TRACEABILITY ──────────────────────────────────────────
// Drawn as a narrow vertical band right of current bar at the REAL tf2 price level.
// Label text mirrors the dashboard "L2 (HTF) Progress" row exactly.
if showTraceZones and barstate.islast and not na(l2_zoneHigh) and not na(l2_zoneLow)

    string _l2txt = "H1 · " + l2_targetWave + " · " + l2_currentPhase + " · D" + str.tostring(math.round(l2_dominance)) + "%"

    if na(l2ZoneBox)
        l2ZoneBox := box.new(_l2R_near, l2_zoneHigh, _l2R_far, l2_zoneLow,
             border_color=trace_L2_col, border_width=2,
             bgcolor=f_zoneFill(color.new(trace_L2_col, 92)),
             border_style=line.style_solid)
        l2ZoneLbl := label.new(_l2R_near, l2_zoneHigh, _l2txt,
             style=label.style_label_left,
             color=color.new(#10103a, 10),
             textcolor=trace_L2_col, size=size.small, textalign=text.align_left)
    else
        box.set_lefttop    (l2ZoneBox, _l2R_near, l2_zoneHigh)
        box.set_rightbottom(l2ZoneBox, _l2R_far,  l2_zoneLow)
        label.set_xy  (l2ZoneLbl, _l2R_near, l2_zoneHigh)
        label.set_text(l2ZoneLbl, _l2txt)

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PHASE 1-B  L0 PRIMARY TRACEABILITY
// Structure: the actual primary wave span from point4OriginBar to current bar.
// These are the EXACT variables driving waveProgress, convexityMaturity,
// originToExtreme, distToOrigin, and the entire hypothesis engine.
// Zone: point4OriginBar → bar_index (the real wave extent on chart)
// Label: placed at the origin bar (the actual spawn point)
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
if showL0Zone and not na(point4OriginBar) and not na(point4OriginHigh) and not na(point4OriginLow)

    // M5 chart label = direct projection of the single Engine 1A display authority
    // (Direction · Canonical/Liquidation phase [· Substate] · Target · Distance · Arrival)
    string _l0txt = "M5 · " + liqg_readout

    // Zone box: origin → now (the actual L0 wave span)
    if na(l0ZoneBox)
        l0ZoneBox := box.new(point4OriginBar, point4OriginHigh, bar_index, point4OriginLow,
             border_color=trace_L0_col, border_width=2,
             bgcolor=f_zoneFill(color.new(trace_L0_col, 94)))
    else
        box.set_lefttop    (l0ZoneBox, point4OriginBar, point4OriginHigh)
        box.set_rightbottom(l0ZoneBox, bar_index,       point4OriginLow)

    // Label at the origin bar (top edge) — exactly where the wave was born
    if na(l0ZoneLbl)
        l0ZoneLbl := label.new(point4OriginBar, point4OriginHigh, _l0txt,
             style=label.style_label_right,
             color=color.new(#10103a, 10),
             textcolor=trace_L0_col, size=size.small, textalign=text.align_left)
    else
        label.set_xy  (l0ZoneLbl, point4OriginBar, point4OriginHigh)
        label.set_text(l0ZoneLbl, _l0txt)

    // Origin anchor pin — small triangle at the exact spawn pivot
    if showOriginPins and ecvShow_Origin
        if na(l0OriginPin)
            l0OriginPin := label.new(point4OriginBar,
                 direction == 1 ? point4OriginLow : point4OriginHigh,
                 "L0",
                 style=direction == 1 ? label.style_label_up : label.style_label_down,
                 color=color.new(trace_L0_col, 15),
                 textcolor=color.black, size=size.tiny)
        else
            label.set_xy(l0OriginPin, point4OriginBar,
                 direction == 1 ? point4OriginLow : point4OriginHigh)

    // Section 9 — "Wave Completion" marker. Fires when ENGINE 1A canonical phase
    // reaches the Demand Return or Supply Return state — the final lifecycle phase.
    // IE1A is the sole authority; score-based thresholds are not used here.
    var label l0CompletionLbl = na
    bool _waveComplete = ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return"
    if showOriginPins and ecvShow_WaveCompletion and _waveComplete
        string _compTxt = "WAVE COMPLETION\n" + waveProgressDirLabel
        if na(l0CompletionLbl)
            l0CompletionLbl := label.new(bar_index,
                 direction == 1 ? high + atr * 0.6 : low - atr * 0.6,
                 _compTxt,
                 style=direction == 1 ? label.style_label_down : label.style_label_up,
                 color=color.new(trace_L0_col, 20),
                 textcolor=color.black, size=size.small)
        else
            label.set_xy  (l0CompletionLbl, bar_index, direction == 1 ? high + atr * 0.6 : low - atr * 0.6)
            label.set_text(l0CompletionLbl, _compTxt)
    else if not na(l0CompletionLbl)
        label.delete(l0CompletionLbl)
        l0CompletionLbl := na


// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PHASE 1-C  L1 CHILD TRACEABILITY
// Structure: the 15-minute (tf1) child wave structure.
// The calculations l1_waveProgress / l1_dominantPhase / l1_convexityMaturity
// are produced by expScr_tf1/decScr_tf1/abScr_tf1/liqScr_tf1, which come
// from request.security(tf1, f_htfBeliefs(...)).
// Zone: l1_zoneHigh / l1_zoneLow (the EXACT tf1 price range already fetched),
//       spanning the equivalent current-TF bars for that tf1 window.
// Label text mirrors "L1 (ITF) Progress" dashboard row exactly.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ── PHASE 1-C  L1 CHILD TRACEABILITY ────────────────────────────────────────
// Drawn as a narrow band right of current bar at the real tf1 price level.
// Narrower than L2, wider than L3 — hierarchy is readable at a glance.
if showTraceZones and barstate.islast and not na(l1_zoneHigh) and not na(l1_zoneLow)

    string _l1txt = "M15 · " + l1_targetWave + " · " + l1_currentPhase + " · D" + str.tostring(math.round(l1_dominance)) + "%"

    if na(l1ZoneBox)
        l1ZoneBox := box.new(_l1R_near, l1_zoneHigh, _l1R_far, l1_zoneLow,
             border_color=trace_L1_col, border_width=1,
             bgcolor=f_zoneFill(color.new(trace_L1_col, 92)),
             border_style=line.style_dashed)
        l1ZoneLbl := label.new(_l1R_near, l1_zoneHigh, _l1txt,
             style=label.style_label_left,
             color=color.new(#10103a, 10),
             textcolor=trace_L1_col, size=size.small, textalign=text.align_left)
    else
        box.set_lefttop    (l1ZoneBox, _l1R_near, l1_zoneHigh)
        box.set_rightbottom(l1ZoneBox, _l1R_far,  l1_zoneLow)
        label.set_xy  (l1ZoneLbl, _l1R_near, l1_zoneHigh)
        label.set_text(l1ZoneLbl, _l1txt)

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PHASE 1-D  L3 GRANDCHILD (M1 PHYSICS SENSOR) TRACEABILITY
// Structure: the 1-minute grandchild structure acting as the M1 physics sensor.
// The calculations l3_waveProgress / l3_dominantPhase are produced by
// m1AbsorptionEmer / m1LiquidityEmer / m1ConvexityEmer / m1ExpansionWeak —
// all fetched via request.security(syminfo.tickerid, "1", f_m1Physics(...)).
// Zone: l3_zoneHigh / l3_zoneLow (EXACT M1 price range already fetched),
//       spanning the equivalent current-TF bars.
// DO NOT redesign or redefine L3 — this is display-only traceability.
// Label text mirrors "L3 (Micro) Progress" dashboard row exactly.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ── PHASE 1-D  L3 GRANDCHILD (M1 PHYSICS SENSOR) TRACEABILITY ───────────────
// DO NOT redesign L3 — display only. Narrow band nearest to price action.
if showTraceZones and barstate.islast and not na(l3_zoneHigh) and not na(l3_zoneLow)

    string _l3txt = "M3 · " + l3_targetWave + " · " + l3_currentPhase + " · D" + str.tostring(math.round(l3_dominance)) + "%"

    if na(l3ZoneBox)
        l3ZoneBox := box.new(_l3R_near, l3_zoneHigh, _l3R_far, l3_zoneLow,
             border_color=color.new(trace_L3_col, 20), border_width=1,
             bgcolor=f_zoneFill(color.new(trace_L3_col, 92)),
             border_style=line.style_dashed)
        l3ZoneLbl := label.new(_l3R_far, f_mid(l3_zoneHigh, l3_zoneLow), _l3txt,
             style=label.style_label_left,
             color=color.new(#10103a, 20),
             textcolor=color.new(trace_L3_col, 10), size=size.tiny, textalign=text.align_left)
    else
        box.set_lefttop    (l3ZoneBox, _l3R_near, l3_zoneHigh)
        box.set_rightbottom(l3ZoneBox, _l3R_far,  l3_zoneLow)
        label.set_xy  (l3ZoneLbl, _l3R_far, f_mid(l3_zoneHigh, l3_zoneLow))
        label.set_text(l3ZoneLbl, _l3txt)

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PHASE 1-G  M1 MICRO TRACEABILITY
// Innermost narrow band at the real M1 ("1") price level. Direction is M1's OWN
// origin-based wave direction (m1_dir); phase is the M1 fixed-tf lifecycle.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ── PHASE 1-G  M1 MICRO TRACEABILITY ────────────────────────────────────────
// Innermost micro label at the real M1 ("1") swing high. Direction is M1's OWN
// origin-based wave (m1_dir -> m1_dirLabel); phase is the M1 fixed-tf lifecycle.
if showTraceZones and barstate.islast and not na(m1_swH)
    string _m1txt = "M1 · " + m1_dirLabel + " · " + m1_phaseCanon
    if na(m1ZoneLbl)
        m1ZoneLbl := label.new(_m1R_near, m1_swH, _m1txt,
             style=label.style_label_left, color=color.new(#10103a, 20),
             textcolor=trace_M1_col, size=size.tiny, textalign=text.align_left)
    else
        label.set_xy  (m1ZoneLbl, _m1R_near, m1_swH)
        label.set_text(m1ZoneLbl, _m1txt)

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PHASE 1-F  AUTOMATIC LABEL STACKING (Section 5 — Visual Clarity Engine)
// Prevents the L2 / L0 / L1 / L3 origin labels from visually overlapping.
// Hierarchy order is enforced top-down: L2 -> L0 -> L1 -> L3. Each label's
// anchor price is read back, and if it sits within a minimum ATR-based
// vertical gap of the label above it in the hierarchy, it is nudged down
// by the remaining distance. No new calculations of wave state are made —
// this only adjusts label.set_xy placement of the four existing labels.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
if showTraceZones and barstate.islast and not na(atr)

    float _stackGap = atr * 1.0   // minimum vertical separation between labels

    // Read current anchor prices (y) for each label, in hierarchy order.
    float _y2 = not na(l2ZoneLbl) ? label.get_y(l2ZoneLbl) : na
    float _y0 = not na(l0ZoneLbl) ? label.get_y(l0ZoneLbl) : na
    float _y1 = not na(l1ZoneLbl) ? label.get_y(l1ZoneLbl) : na
    float _y3 = not na(l3ZoneLbl) ? label.get_y(l3ZoneLbl) : na

    // L0 vs L2
    if not na(_y2) and not na(_y0) and math.abs(_y2 - _y0) < _stackGap
        _y0 := _y0 < _y2 ? _y2 - _stackGap : _y2 + _stackGap
        label.set_xy(l0ZoneLbl, label.get_x(l0ZoneLbl), _y0)

    // L1 vs L0
    if not na(_y0) and not na(_y1) and math.abs(_y0 - _y1) < _stackGap
        _y1 := _y1 < _y0 ? _y0 - _stackGap : _y0 + _stackGap
        label.set_xy(l1ZoneLbl, label.get_x(l1ZoneLbl), _y1)

    // L3 vs L1
    if not na(_y1) and not na(_y3) and math.abs(_y1 - _y3) < _stackGap
        _y3 := _y3 < _y1 ? _y1 - _stackGap : _y1 + _stackGap
        label.set_xy(l3ZoneLbl, label.get_x(l3ZoneLbl), _y3)

    // L3 vs L2 (in case L1 nudge pushed L3 back into L2's space)
    if not na(_y2) and not na(_y3) and math.abs(_y2 - _y3) < _stackGap
        _y3 := _y3 < _y2 ? _y2 - _stackGap : _y2 + _stackGap
        label.set_xy(l3ZoneLbl, label.get_x(l3ZoneLbl), _y3)

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PHASE 1-E  DOMINANT WAVE VISIBILITY
// Drawn ON the dominant structure's zone — not in a detached location.
// Uses existing dominantWaveLevel (from l0/l1/l2/l3 dominance engine).
// No new dominance calculations.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
if showDominantTag and barstate.islast

    // Determine which structure's midpoint to anchor the tag to
    color _domCol  =
         dominantWaveLevel == "L2 HTF"    ? trace_L2_col :
         dominantWaveLevel == "L1 CHILD"    ? trace_L1_col :
         dominantWaveLevel == "L0 PRIMARY" ? trace_L0_col : trace_L3_col

    // Anchor price: mid of the dominant structure's zone
    float _domMid =
         dominantWaveLevel == "L2 HTF"     and not na(l2_zoneHigh) and not na(l2_zoneLow) ?
              f_mid(l2_zoneHigh, l2_zoneLow) :
         dominantWaveLevel == "L1 CHILD"     and not na(l1_zoneHigh) and not na(l1_zoneLow) ?
              f_mid(l1_zoneHigh, l1_zoneLow) :
         dominantWaveLevel == "L0 PRIMARY" and not na(point4OriginHigh) and not na(point4OriginLow) ?
              f_mid(point4OriginHigh, point4OriginLow) :
         not na(l3_zoneHigh) and not na(l3_zoneLow) ?
              f_mid(l3_zoneHigh, l3_zoneLow) : close

    // Anchor bar: right edge of the dominant structure
    int _domBar = bar_index

    string _domTxt = "DOM: " + (dominantWaveLevel == "L2 HTF" ? "H1" : dominantWaveLevel == "L1 CHILD" ? "M15" : dominantWaveLevel == "L0 PRIMARY" ? "M5" : "M3")

    if na(dominantLabel)
        dominantLabel := label.new(_domBar, _domMid, _domTxt,
             style=label.style_label_left,
             color=color.new(#10103a, 5),
             textcolor=_domCol, size=size.normal, textalign=text.align_left)
    else
        label.set_xy       (dominantLabel, _domBar, _domMid)
        label.set_text     (dominantLabel, _domTxt)
        label.set_textcolor(dominantLabel, _domCol)


// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 17 — FUTURE RETURN ZONE ENGINE (FRZ)  [Phase 2]
// Identifies price areas of highest interaction probability BEFORE the return.
// Uses ONLY existing detection variables — no new physics calculations.
//
// Qualification scoring — each component adds 25 points (max 100):
//   Req 1 — FU Candle        : isBullFU_prev / isBearFU_prev (gap-confirmed)
//                              OR isBullFU / isBearFU (same-bar)
//   Req 2 — Imbalance / FVG  : displacement > dispThresh  (void/gap proxy)
//   Req 3 — Liquidity Cleared: liqSweepBull / liqSweepBear / liqVacuum
//                              OR obs_LiquidityScore > 55
//   Req 4 — Displacement     : bullImpulse or bearImpulse
//
// Classification: 0-25 Weak | 26-50 Moderate | 51-75 Strong | 76-100 Exceptional
//
// Section 18 Validation: reject zones where resting liquidity is present
// (liqHeat > 60) AND no sweep has occurred — approve only clean launches.
//
// Spawn guard: one FRZ per bar maximum; dedup by zone overlap with existing zones.
// Lifecycle: Open → Partial (price touched) → Mitigated (full close-inside)
//            → Invalidated (price blew through from wrong side).
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ── FRZ-0: OWNER LAYER MAPPING (Section 19) ──────────────────────────────────
// Determine which wave layer is currently dominant — this becomes the creator tag.
// Uses existing dominantWaveLevel variable (no new logic).
string frz_ownerLayer =
     dominantWaveLevel == "L2 HTF"    ? "L2 HTF"    :
     dominantWaveLevel == "L1 CHILD"  ? "L1 CHILD"  :
     dominantWaveLevel == "L0 PRIMARY"? "L0 PRIMARY" : "L3 MICRO"

// ── FRZ-1: PER-BAR COMPONENT DETECTION ───────────────────────────────────────

// Req 1 — FU candle (gap-confirmed prior bar preferred; same-bar fallback)
bool frz_hasFU_gc   = isBullFU_prev or isBearFU_prev          // gap-confirmed (highest conviction)
bool frz_hasFU_sb   = isBullFU      or isBearFU               // same-bar (lower conviction)
bool frz_hasFU      = frz_hasFU_gc  or frz_hasFU_sb
int  frz_scoreFU    = frz_hasFU ? 25 : 0

// Directional hint from FU type
