bool frz_fuIsBull   = isBullFU_prev or isBullFU
bool frz_fuIsBear   = isBearFU_prev or isBearFU

// Req 2 — Imbalance / FVG / displacement void
// Uses existing displacement variable — values > dispThresh confirm a price void
bool frz_hasImbalance = displacement > dispThresh
int  frz_scoreIMB     = frz_hasImbalance ? 25 : 0

// Req 3 — Liquidity cleared BEFORE the launch
bool frz_hasLiqClear = liqSweepBull or liqSweepBear or liqVacuum or
                       (obs_LiquidityScore > 55.0)
int  frz_scoreLIQ    = frz_hasLiqClear ? 25 : 0

// Req 4 — Displacement impulse (velocity + efficiency + expansion)
bool frz_hasDisp  = bullImpulse or bearImpulse
int  frz_scoreDisp = frz_hasDisp ? 25 : 0

// Raw score 0-100
int frz_rawScore = frz_scoreFU + frz_scoreIMB + frz_scoreLIQ + frz_scoreDisp

// ── FRZ-2: SECTION 18 — LIQUIDITY-FREE VALIDATION ────────────────────────────
// Reject if resting liquidity sits ahead and has NOT been swept yet.
bool frz_liqResting = liqHeat > 60 and not (liqSweepBull or liqSweepBear)
bool frz_approved   = not frz_liqResting

// ── FRZ-3: CLASSIFICATION & TIER STRINGS ─────────────────────────────────────
string frz_class =
     frz_rawScore >= 76 ? "Exceptional" :
     frz_rawScore >= 51 ? "Strong"      :
     frz_rawScore >= 26 ? "Moderate"    : "Weak"

string frz_tier =
     frz_rawScore >= 76                          ? "T1" :
     frz_rawScore >= 51                          ? "T2" :
     frz_rawScore >= 26 and frz_hasFU           ? "T3" :
     frz_rawScore >= 26 and frz_hasImbalance     ? "T4" : "–"

string frz_tierFull =
     frz_rawScore >= 76                          ? "Tier 1 ★★★" :
     frz_rawScore >= 51                          ? "Tier 2 ★★"  :
     frz_rawScore >= 26 and frz_hasFU           ? "Tier 3 ★"   :
     frz_rawScore >= 26 and frz_hasImbalance     ? "Tier 4"     : "–"

string frz_compStr =
     frz_hasFU and frz_hasImbalance and frz_hasLiqClear and frz_hasDisp ? "FU+IMB+LS+DISP" :
     frz_hasFU and frz_hasImbalance and frz_hasLiqClear                  ? "FU+IMB+LS"      :
     frz_hasFU and frz_hasImbalance and frz_hasDisp                      ? "FU+IMB+DISP"    :
     frz_hasFU and frz_hasImbalance                                       ? "FU+IMB"         :
     frz_hasFU and frz_hasLiqClear                                        ? "FU+LS"          :
     frz_hasFU                                                             ? "FU"             :
     frz_hasImbalance and frz_hasLiqClear                                 ? "IMB+LS"         :
     frz_hasImbalance                                                      ? "IMB"            : "–"

// ── FRZ-4: PERSISTENT ZONE STORAGE ───────────────────────────────────────────
// Arrays hold all live FRZs. Index 0 = oldest.

var array<float>  frz_topArr    = array.new_float ()
var array<float>  frz_botArr    = array.new_float ()
var array<int>    frz_barArr    = array.new_int   ()
var array<int>    frz_dirArr    = array.new_int   ()    // 1=bull demand, -1=bear supply
var array<int>    frz_scoreArr  = array.new_int   ()
var array<string> frz_classArr  = array.new_string()
var array<string> frz_tierArr   = array.new_string()
var array<string> frz_tierFArr  = array.new_string()    // full tier string
var array<string> frz_compArr   = array.new_string()
var array<string> frz_ownerArr  = array.new_string()    // Section 19: creator layer
var array<string> frz_statusArr = array.new_string()    // Open / Partial / Mitigated / Invalidated
var array<int>    frz_idxArr    = array.new_int   ()    // sequential FRZ number (display)
var array<box>    frz_boxArr    = array.new<box>  ()
var array<label>  frz_lblArr    = array.new<label>()

var int frz_totalSpawned = 0   // running counter for FRZ #N label

// ── FRZ-5: SPAWN GUARD & DEDUPLICATION ───────────────────────────────────────
// Gate: score >= min threshold, approved by Section 18, at least one primary
// signal present, active wave exists, and score > 0 (i.e. not a blank bar).
// Dedup: do not spawn if an existing live zone overlaps this candle's range.

// Determine zone direction from existing wave + FU signals
bool _frz_isBullSetup = direction == 1 or frz_fuIsBull
bool _frz_isBearSetup = direction == -1 or frz_fuIsBear
int  _frz_spawnDir = _frz_isBullSetup and not _frz_isBearSetup ? 1 : _frz_isBearSetup and not _frz_isBullSetup ? -1 : direction != 0 ? direction : 0

// Zone boundaries: use the triggering candle's range
// Bull demand FRZ → zone = low to close (demand left behind below the launch)
// Bear supply FRZ → zone = close to high (supply left behind above the launch)
float _frz_zTop = _frz_spawnDir == 1 ? math.max(open, close) : high
float _frz_zBot = _frz_spawnDir == 1 ? low                   : math.min(open, close)

// Gap-confirmed FU override: use the FU candle's range (one bar ago)
if frz_hasFU_gc
    _frz_zTop := _frz_spawnDir == 1 ? high[1] : math.max(open[1], close[1])
    _frz_zBot := _frz_spawnDir == 1 ? math.min(open[1], close[1]) : low[1]

// Ensure top > bot (safety guard)
if _frz_zTop <= _frz_zBot
    _frz_zTop := math.max(open, close, high)
    _frz_zBot := math.min(open, close, low)

// Check overlap with existing zones to avoid stacking identical zones
bool _frz_overlaps = false
int  _frzExist = array.size(frz_topArr)
if _frzExist > 0
    for _oi = 0 to _frzExist - 1
        if _oi < array.size(frz_topArr)
            float _ot = array.get(frz_topArr, _oi)
            float _ob = array.get(frz_botArr, _oi)
            // Overlap: zones share > 50% of their combined range
            float _overlapHi = math.min(_frz_zTop, _ot)
            float _overlapLo = math.max(_frz_zBot, _ob)
            float _overlap   = math.max(0.0, _overlapHi - _overlapLo)
            float _thisRange = math.max(_frz_zTop - _frz_zBot, 1e-10)
            if _overlap / _thisRange > 0.5
                _frz_overlaps := true
                break

bool frz_spawn = showFRZ                           and
                 frz_approved                       and
                 frz_rawScore >= frz_minScore       and
                 frz_rawScore > 0                   and
                 (frz_hasFU or frz_hasImbalance)    and
                 _frz_spawnDir != 0                 and
                 not _frz_overlaps

if frz_spawn
    frz_totalSpawned := frz_totalSpawned + 1

    // Color by direction and tier
    color _frzBg =
         frz_rawScore >= 76 ? color.new(_frz_spawnDir == 1 ? #00ffcc : #ff2244, 80) :
         frz_rawScore >= 51 ? color.new(_frz_spawnDir == 1 ? color.teal : color.red, 84) :
                              color.new(_frz_spawnDir == 1 ? color.teal : color.red, 90)
    color _frzBorder =
         frz_rawScore >= 76 ? color.new(_frz_spawnDir == 1 ? #00ffcc : #ff2244, 10) :
         frz_rawScore >= 51 ? color.new(_frz_spawnDir == 1 ? color.teal : color.red, 35) :
                              color.new(_frz_spawnDir == 1 ? color.teal : color.red, 55)
    int _frzBW = frz_rawScore >= 76 ? 2 : 1

    box _frzBox = box.new(
         left         = bar_index,
         top          = _frz_zTop,
         bottom       = _frz_zBot,
         right        = bar_index + frz_maxBarsActive,
         bgcolor      = f_zoneFill(_frzBg),
         border_color = _frzBorder,
         border_width = _frzBW,
         border_style = line.style_dashed)

    array.push(frz_boxArr,   _frzBox)
    array.push(frz_topArr,   _frz_zTop)
    array.push(frz_botArr,   _frz_zBot)
    array.push(frz_barArr,   bar_index)
    array.push(frz_dirArr,   _frz_spawnDir)
    array.push(frz_scoreArr, frz_rawScore)
    array.push(frz_classArr, frz_class)
    array.push(frz_tierArr,  frz_tier)
    array.push(frz_tierFArr, frz_tierFull)
    array.push(frz_compArr,  frz_compStr)
    array.push(frz_ownerArr, frz_ownerLayer)     // Section 19: creator
    array.push(frz_statusArr,"Open")
    array.push(frz_idxArr,   frz_totalSpawned)

    // ── FRZ label — spec format: "FRZ #N\nScore%\nClass\nTier\nComponents\nCreated By\nOwner" ──
    if showFRZ_Labels
        string _frzLblTxt =
             "FRZ #" + str.tostring(frz_totalSpawned) + "\n" +
             str.tostring(frz_rawScore) + "%  " + frz_class + "\n" +
             frz_tierFull + "\n" +
             frz_compStr + "\n" +
             "Created By\n" + frz_ownerLayer
        label _frzLbl = label.new(
             x         = bar_index,
             y         = _frz_spawnDir == 1 ? _frz_zBot - atr * 0.5 : _frz_zTop + atr * 0.5,
             text      = _frzLblTxt,
             style     = _frz_spawnDir == 1 ? label.style_label_up : label.style_label_down,
             color     = color.new(_frz_spawnDir == 1 ? #00ffcc : #ff2244, 12),
             textcolor = _frz_spawnDir == 1 ? color.black : color.white,
             size      = frz_rawScore >= 76 ? size.small : size.tiny,
             textalign = text.align_left)
        array.push(frz_lblArr, _frzLbl)
    else
        array.push(frz_lblArr, na)

// ── FRZ-6: LIFECYCLE ENGINE ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Status transitions:
//   Open       → Partial      (price wicked into zone but close was outside)
//   Open/Partial→ Mitigated   (close inside zone)
//   Open/Partial→ Invalidated (price closed through zone from wrong side)
// Expired zones (age >= frz_maxBarsActive) are also removed.

int _frzN = array.size(frz_topArr)
if _frzN > 0
    for _fi = _frzN - 1 to 0
        if _fi < array.size(frz_topArr)
            float  _ft  = array.get(frz_topArr,   _fi)
            float  _fb  = array.get(frz_botArr,   _fi)
            int    _fbb = array.get(frz_barArr,   _fi)
            int    _fd  = array.get(frz_dirArr,   _fi)
            string _fst = array.get(frz_statusArr,_fi)
            box    _bx  = array.get(frz_boxArr,   _fi)
            int    _age = bar_index - _fbb

            // Skip already-terminal zones waiting for removal
            bool _terminal = _fst == "Mitigated" or _fst == "Invalidated"

            if not _terminal
                // Partial: wick entered zone but close stayed outside
                bool _wickIn  = low  <= _ft and high >= _fb
                bool _closeIn = close >= _fb and close <= _ft

                // Invalidated: bull zone closed BELOW bot, or bear zone closed ABOVE top
                bool _invalid = (_fd == 1 and close < _fb - atr * 0.1) or (_fd == -1 and close > _ft + atr * 0.1)

                string _newStatus = _fst
                if _closeIn
                    _newStatus := "Mitigated"
                else if _invalid
                    _newStatus := "Invalidated"
                else if _wickIn and _fst == "Open"
                    _newStatus := "Partial"

                if _newStatus != _fst
                    array.set(frz_statusArr, _fi, _newStatus)
                    // Update box visual on status change
                    if not na(_bx)
                        color _stCol =
                             _newStatus == "Partial"     ? color.new(color.yellow, 82) :
                             _newStatus == "Mitigated"   ? color.new(color.gray,   88) :
                                                           color.new(color.purple,  88)
                        box.set_bgcolor(_bx, f_zoneFill(_stCol))
                        box.set_border_color(_bx, color.new(color.gray, 50))

// Extend right edge while zone is still Open or Partial
                if not na(_bx) and showFRZ and (_newStatus == "Open" or _newStatus == "Partial")
                    box.set_right(_bx, bar_index + 10)

            // Remove terminal or expired zones
            bool _remove = _terminal or _age >= frz_maxBarsActive
            if _remove
                box   _bx2 = array.get(frz_boxArr, _fi)
                label _lb2 = array.get(frz_lblArr, _fi)
                if not na(_bx2)
                    box.delete(_bx2)
                if not na(_lb2)
                    label.delete(_lb2)
                array.remove(frz_topArr,   _fi)
                array.remove(frz_botArr,   _fi)
                array.remove(frz_barArr,   _fi)
                array.remove(frz_dirArr,   _fi)
                array.remove(frz_scoreArr, _fi)
                array.remove(frz_classArr, _fi)
                array.remove(frz_tierArr,  _fi)
                array.remove(frz_tierFArr, _fi)
                array.remove(frz_compArr,  _fi)
                array.remove(frz_ownerArr, _fi)
                array.remove(frz_statusArr,_fi)
                array.remove(frz_idxArr,   _fi)
                array.remove(frz_boxArr,   _fi)
                array.remove(frz_lblArr,   _fi)

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SECTION 19 — FRZ OWNERSHIP ENGINE  [Phase 2]
// Every FRZ permanently records which wave layer created it (stored above at
// spawn time in frz_ownerArr). The label already shows "Created By / L# LAYER".
// This section derives the live summary statistics used by Section 20.
// No new arrays needed — ownership is already in frz_ownerArr.
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// Tally live zone counts per owner layer (for Section 20 dashboard header)
int frz_ownL0 = 0
int frz_ownL1 = 0
int frz_ownL2 = 0
int frz_ownL3 = 0
int frz_activeCount = 0
int frz_bullCount   = 0
int frz_bearCount   = 0

// Best-zone summary variables
int    frz_bestScore  = 0
string frz_bestClass  = "–"
string frz_bestTier   = "–"
string frz_bestComp   = "–"
string frz_bestOwner  = "–"
string frz_bestStatus = "–"

int _frzN3 = array.size(frz_scoreArr)
if _frzN3 > 0
    for _fk = 0 to _frzN3 - 1
        if _fk < array.size(frz_scoreArr)
            string _own = array.get(frz_ownerArr,  _fk)
            string _st  = array.get(frz_statusArr, _fk)
            int    _sc  = array.get(frz_scoreArr,  _fk)
            int    _fd2 = array.get(frz_dirArr,    _fk)
            bool   _live = _st == "Open" or _st == "Partial"

            if _live
                frz_activeCount := frz_activeCount + 1
                if _fd2 == 1
                    frz_bullCount := frz_bullCount + 1
                else
                    frz_bearCount := frz_bearCount + 1

                if _own == "L0 PRIMARY"
                    frz_ownL0 := frz_ownL0 + 1
                else if _own == "L1 CHILD"
                    frz_ownL1 := frz_ownL1 + 1
                else if _own == "L2 HTF"
                    frz_ownL2 := frz_ownL2 + 1
                else
                    frz_ownL3 := frz_ownL3 + 1

                if _sc > frz_bestScore
                    frz_bestScore  := _sc
                    frz_bestClass  := array.get(frz_classArr,  _fk)
                    frz_bestTier   := array.get(frz_tierFArr,  _fk)
                    frz_bestComp   := array.get(frz_compArr,   _fk)
                    frz_bestOwner  := _own
                    frz_bestStatus := _st





// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// authority; every engine below is a CONSUMER (nothing reassigns ie1a_currentPhase).

// (Pine forbids them inside functions), so they live here. All engine computation,
// the Wave/Delivery registries, and both dashboards are wrapped in f_v72_run(),
// which is called once per bar. Persistent registry state uses `var` locals (valid
// because the call site is singular). This keeps the main body small.

// Bundle tunables into arrays (each array counts as a single external element).
array<float> v72F = array.from(in_frzProximityATR, in_frzConvergenceATR, in_rieW_decay, in_rieW_absorb, in_rieW_convex, in_rieW_stabExp, in_rieW_press, in_rieW_stabInv, in_invOriginBuffer, in_invZoneBuffer, in_teTertiaryATR, in_rrMinimum, in_tqeW_ie1a, in_tqeW_erf, in_tqeW_frz, in_tqeW_mce, in_tqeW_re, in_tqeW_liq, in_tqeGradeA1, in_tqeGradeA, in_tqeGradeB, in_tqeGradeC)
array<int>   v72I = array.from(in_doeCapBase, in_doeCapConv)
array<bool>  v72B = array.from(in_teTertiaryOn, in_dashAdvancedMode, in_showV72Command)
string       v72Sz = dashTextSize == "tiny" ? size.tiny : dashTextSize == "normal" ? size.normal : size.small

// ── MCE TF3/TF4 direction reads (single-value to minimize external elements) ──
// CE limit fix: each request.*() return value counts toward EVERY function's
// 254 external-element budget. Returning only the structural direction (1 int)
// instead of the full 8-value belief tuple keeps that global count low while
// still giving MCE the 4-level direction stack it needs (C15).
f_htfDir(float _open, float _high, float _low, float _close, float _effT, float _dispT, int _obLook) =>
    float _atr_htf = ta.atr(atrLen)
    float _vel_htf = ta.ema(_close - _close[1], 3)
    float _acc_htf = _vel_htf - _vel_htf[1]
    float _move    = math.abs(_close - _close[_obLook])
    float _pathSum = math.sum(math.abs(_close - _close[1]), _obLook)
    float _eff     = _pathSum > 0 ? _move / _pathSum : 0.0
    float _disp    = (_high - _low) / math.max(_atr_htf, 1e-10)
    bool  _bullImp = _eff > _effT and _vel_htf > _vel_htf[1] and _acc_htf > 0 and _close > _open and _disp > _dispT
    bool  _bearImp = _eff > _effT and _vel_htf < _vel_htf[1] and _acc_htf < 0 and _close < _open and _disp > _dispT
    _bullImp ? 1 : _bearImp ? -1 : 0

dir_tf3_raw = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, mce_tf3, f_htfDir(open, high, low, close, effThresh, dispThresh, obLookback), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)
dir_tf4_raw = request.security(syminfo.tickerid, mce_tf4, f_htfDir(open, high, low, close, effThresh, dispThresh, obLookback), lookahead=barmerge.lookahead_off)

// ── Display helper functions (global) ────────────────────────────────────────
f_v72_px(float _v)  => na(_v) ? "–" : str.tostring(math.round_to_mintick(_v))
f_v72_pct(float _v) => na(_v) ? "–" : str.tostring(math.round(_v)) + "%"
f_v72_num(float _v, int _d) => na(_v) ? "–" : str.tostring(math.round(_v, _d))

// (f_fuCoordRow removed in Letra 32 — FU registry panel replaced by route arrows)
f_v72_actionCol(string _a) => _a == "Long" ? #00ff88 : _a == "Short" ? color.red : _a == "No Trade" ? color.maroon : color.gray
f_v72_gradeCol(string _g)  => _g == "A+" ? #00ffcc : _g == "A" ? color.lime : _g == "B" ? color.yellow : _g == "C" ? color.orange : color.red
f_v72_riskCol(string _r)   => _r == "LOW" ? color.lime : _r == "MEDIUM" ? color.yellow : color.red

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// f_v72_run — all V72 engine computation, registries and dashboards.
// Called once per bar (below). Reads global V71 vars + inputs; _dir3/_dir4 are the
// TF3/TF4 structural directions from the security reads above.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
f_v72_run(int _dir3, int _dir4, array<float> _cf, array<int> _ci, array<bool> _cb, string _szCmd) =>
    // Unpack bundled tunables into local names so the engine body below is
    // unchanged. These locals are NOT globals, so there is no shadowing.
    float frzProximityATR   = array.get(_cf, 0)
    float frzConvergenceATR = array.get(_cf, 1)
    float rieW_decay        = array.get(_cf, 2)
    float rieW_absorb       = array.get(_cf, 3)
    float rieW_convex       = array.get(_cf, 4)
    float rieW_stabExp      = array.get(_cf, 5)
    float rieW_press        = array.get(_cf, 6)
    float rieW_stabInv      = array.get(_cf, 7)
    float invOriginBuffer   = array.get(_cf, 8)
    float invZoneBuffer     = array.get(_cf, 9)
    float teTertiaryATR     = array.get(_cf, 10)
    float rrMinimum         = array.get(_cf, 11)
    float tqeW_ie1a         = array.get(_cf, 12)
    float tqeW_erf          = array.get(_cf, 13)
    float tqeW_frz          = array.get(_cf, 14)
    float tqeW_mce          = array.get(_cf, 15)
    float tqeW_re           = array.get(_cf, 16)
    float tqeW_liq          = array.get(_cf, 17)
    float tqeGradeA1        = array.get(_cf, 18)
    float tqeGradeA         = array.get(_cf, 19)
    float tqeGradeB         = array.get(_cf, 20)
    float tqeGradeC         = array.get(_cf, 21)
    int   doeCapBase        = array.get(_ci, 0)
    int   doeCapConv        = array.get(_ci, 1)
    bool  teTertiaryOn      = array.get(_cb, 0)
    bool  dashAdvancedMode  = array.get(_cb, 1)
    bool  showV72Command    = array.get(_cb, 2)
    // ── V72.1 FRZ best-zone index resolution (C1) ────────────────────────────
    int   v72_frzBestIdx = -1
    int   v72_frzBestSc  = -1
    int   _v72_frzN = array.size(frz_scoreArr)
    if _v72_frzN > 0
        for _i = 0 to _v72_frzN - 1
            if _i < array.size(frz_statusArr) and _i < array.size(frz_scoreArr)
                string _stt = array.get(frz_statusArr, _i)
                if _stt == "Open" or _stt == "Partial"
                    int _sc = array.get(frz_scoreArr, _i)
                    if _sc > v72_frzBestSc
                        v72_frzBestSc  := _sc
                        v72_frzBestIdx := _i
    float frz_bestZoneTop = v72_frzBestIdx >= 0 and v72_frzBestIdx < array.size(frz_topArr) ? array.get(frz_topArr, v72_frzBestIdx) : na
    float frz_bestZoneBot = v72_frzBestIdx >= 0 and v72_frzBestIdx < array.size(frz_botArr) ? array.get(frz_botArr, v72_frzBestIdx) : na
    int   frz_bestZoneDir = v72_frzBestIdx >= 0 and v72_frzBestIdx < array.size(frz_dirArr) ? array.get(frz_dirArr, v72_frzBestIdx) : 0
    string frz_bestZoneTier = v72_frzBestIdx >= 0 and v72_frzBestIdx < array.size(frz_tierArr) ? array.get(frz_tierArr, v72_frzBestIdx) : "–"
    float frz_bestZoneMid = (not na(frz_bestZoneTop) and not na(frz_bestZoneBot)) ? (frz_bestZoneTop + frz_bestZoneBot) / 2.0 : na
    float frz_distanceToZone = (frz_activeCount > 0 and not na(frz_bestZoneMid)) ? math.abs(close - frz_bestZoneMid) / math.max(atr, 1e-10) : na
    bool  frz_inProximity = frz_activeCount > 0 and not na(frz_distanceToZone) and frz_distanceToZone < frzProximityATR
    float frz_resolutionScore =
         re_resolutionState == "RESOLVED"           ? 90.0 :
         re_resolutionState == "PARTIALLY RESOLVED" ? 50.0 + re_recursiveCompletionScore * 0.40 :
                                                       20.0 + ede_dissipationProgress * 0.30
    float frz_residualEnergy  = math.max(0.0, 100.0 - frz_resolutionScore)
    float frz_attractorWeight = frz_activeCount > 0 ? math.min(frz_residualEnergy * 0.50 + frz_bestScore * 0.30 + (frz_bestStatus == "Open" ? 20.0 : frz_bestStatus == "Partial" ? 10.0 : 0.0), 100.0) : 0.0
    bool  frz_attractorConvergence = frz_activeCount > 0 and not na(eae_primaryAttractorPrice) and not na(frz_bestZoneMid) and math.abs(eae_primaryAttractorPrice - frz_bestZoneMid) / math.max(atr, 1e-10) < frzConvergenceATR

    // ── V72.2 Rotation Intelligence Engine (C8, C16) ─────────────────────────
    float rot_pressure = math.min(obs_DecayScore * rieW_decay + obs_AbsorptionScore * rieW_absorb + (convexityScore > 40 ? convexityScore * rieW_convex : 0.0) + (obs_LiquidityScore > 50 ? 15.0 : 0.0), 100.0)
    float rot_controlStability = math.min(obs_ExpansionScore * rieW_stabExp + (efficiency > effThresh ? 30.0 : efficiency > effThresh * 0.7 ? 15.0 : 0.0) + (ede_state <= 2 ? 30.0 : ede_state <= 3 ? 15.0 : 0.0), 100.0)
    float rot_transferProbability = math.min(rot_pressure * rieW_press + (100.0 - rot_controlStability) * rieW_stabInv + (re_resolutionState == "UNRESOLVED" ? 20.0 : re_resolutionState == "PARTIALLY RESOLVED" ? 10.0 : 0.0), 100.0)
    string rot_state = rot_transferProbability >= 75 ? "TRANSFER_IMMINENT" : rot_transferProbability >= 50 ? "CONTESTED" : rot_transferProbability >= 25 ? "SOFTENING" : "STABLE"

    // ── V72.3 Multi-TF Consensus Engine (C11, C15) ───────────────────────────
    int   mce_tf1_direction = l1_dir   // M15 FIXED structure (v90: was dir_tf1 belief)
    int   mce_tf2_direction = l2_dir   // H1  FIXED structure (v90: was dir_tf2 belief)
    int   mce_tf3_direction = nz(_dir3)
    int   mce_tf4_direction = nz(_dir4)
    int _mce_agreeAll  = (mce_tf1_direction == displayWaveDir_M5 and displayWaveDir_M5 != 0 ? 1 : 0) + (mce_tf2_direction == displayWaveDir_M5 and displayWaveDir_M5 != 0 ? 1 : 0) + (mce_tf3_direction == displayWaveDir_M5 and displayWaveDir_M5 != 0 ? 1 : 0) + (mce_tf4_direction == displayWaveDir_M5 and displayWaveDir_M5 != 0 ? 1 : 0)
    int _mce_agreeHtf  = (mce_tf3_direction == displayWaveDir_M5 and displayWaveDir_M5 != 0 ? 1 : 0) + (mce_tf4_direction == displayWaveDir_M5 and displayWaveDir_M5 != 0 ? 1 : 0)
    int _mce_agreeExec = (mce_tf1_direction == displayWaveDir_M5 and displayWaveDir_M5 != 0 ? 1 : 0) + (mce_tf2_direction == displayWaveDir_M5 and displayWaveDir_M5 != 0 ? 1 : 0)
    float mce_alignmentScore     = displayWaveDir_M5 == 0 ? 0.0 : _mce_agreeAll  / 4.0 * 100.0
    float mce_htfAlignmentScore  = displayWaveDir_M5 == 0 ? 0.0 : math.min((_mce_agreeHtf / 2.0 * 100.0) * 0.55 + fractalCtxScore * 0.45, 100.0)
    float mce_execAlignmentScore = displayWaveDir_M5 == 0 ? 0.0 : _mce_agreeExec / 2.0 * 100.0
    int mce_lifecycleProgress =
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Point 4 Origin"           ? 5  :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion"                ? 20 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Pre-Convexity"  ? 35 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Induction"      ? 50 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Liquidity"      ? 65 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "New High"                 ? 80 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "New Low"                  ? 80 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Absorption"               ? 70 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement"              ? 55 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Pre-Convexity"? 40 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Induction"    ? 25 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Liquidity"    ? 15 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return"            ? 90 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return"            ? 90 : 0
    string mce_htfAlignmentSummary =
         mce_htfAlignmentScore >= 80 and displayWaveDir_M5 == 1  ? "HTF Bullish Continuation" :
         mce_htfAlignmentScore >= 80 and displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 ? "HTF Bearish Continuation" :
         mce_htfAlignmentScore >= 60 and rot_transferProbability < 40 ? "HTF Trend Intact" :
         mce_htfAlignmentScore >= 50 and rot_transferProbability >= 60 ? "HTF Rotation Developing" :
         mce_htfAlignmentScore < 40 ? "HTF Contested — No Clear Bias" : "HTF Developing"
    string mce_execAlignmentSummary =
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return" and mce_execAlignmentScore >= 60 ? "Execution Aligned — Long Window" :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return" and mce_execAlignmentScore >= 60 ? "Execution Aligned — Short Window" :
         mce_execAlignmentScore < 40 ? "Execution Conflict — Wait" : "Execution Developing"

    // ── V72.4 Narrative Engine (C3) ──────────────────────────────────────────
    bool _ne_phaseExpBull = ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion" or ie1a_currentPhase == "New High"
    bool _ne_phaseExpBear = ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion" or ie1a_currentPhase == "New Low"
    bool _ne_phasePullback = ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Pre-Convexity" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Induction" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Liquidity"
    bool _ne_phaseDemandReturn = ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return"
    bool _ne_phaseSupplyReturn = ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return"
    float _ne_htfScore = mce_htfAlignmentScore > 0 ? mce_htfAlignmentScore : (htfAlign == displayWaveDir_M5 and displayWaveDir_M5 != 0 ? 70.0 : 0.0)
    string ne_dominantNarrative =
         displayWaveDir_M5 == 0 ? "No Clear Narrative" :
         displayWaveDir_M5 == 1  and _ne_phaseExpBull and rot_transferProbability < 40 ? "Bullish Continuation" :
         displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 and _ne_phaseExpBear and rot_transferProbability < 40 ? "Bearish Continuation" :
         displayWaveDir_M5 == 1  and (_ne_phasePullback or _ne_phaseDemandReturn) ? "Bullish Pullback" :
         displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 and (_ne_phasePullback or _ne_phaseSupplyReturn) ? "Bearish Pullback" :
         displayWaveDir_M5 == 1  and (rot_transferProbability >= 55 or ie1a_currentPhase == "Absorption") ? "Bullish Reversal Developing" :
         displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 and (rot_transferProbability >= 55 or ie1a_currentPhase == "Absorption") ? "Bearish Reversal Developing" :
         displayWaveDir_M5 == 1  ? "Bullish Developing" :
         displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 ? "Bearish Developing" : "No Clear Narrative"
    float ne_narrativeStrength = math.min(mce_alignmentScore * 0.40 + rot_controlStability * 0.30 + (re_resolutionState == "RESOLVED" ? 30.0 : re_resolutionState == "PARTIALLY RESOLVED" ? 15.0 : 0.0), 100.0)

    // ── V72.5 Invalidation Engine (C9) ───────────────────────────────────────
    float inv_bullOriginPrice = not na(point4OriginLow)  ? point4OriginLow  - atr * invOriginBuffer : na
    float inv_bearOriginPrice = not na(point4OriginHigh) ? point4OriginHigh + atr * invOriginBuffer : na
    float inv_demandFailPrice = direction == 1  and not na(flipBot) ? flipBot - atr * invZoneBuffer : na
    float inv_supplyFailPrice = direction == -1 and not na(flipTop) ? flipTop + atr * invZoneBuffer : na
    float inv_activeStop = direction == 1 ? nz(inv_demandFailPrice, inv_bullOriginPrice) : direction == -1 ? nz(inv_supplyFailPrice, inv_bearOriginPrice) : na
    bool  inv_invalidated = not na(inv_activeStop) and (direction == 1 ? close < inv_activeStop : direction == -1 ? close > inv_activeStop : false)
    float inv_riskInPts = not na(inv_activeStop) ? math.abs(close - inv_activeStop) : na

    // ── V72.6 Target Engine (C2) ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    float eae_tertiaryAttractorPrice =
         direction == 1  ? math.max(nz(eae_primaryAttractorPrice, close), nz(eae_secondaryAttractorPrice, close)) + atr * teTertiaryATR :
         direction == -1 ? math.min(nz(eae_primaryAttractorPrice, close), nz(eae_secondaryAttractorPrice, close)) - atr * teTertiaryATR : na
    float eae_tertiaryAttractorScore = re_residualEnergyScore * 0.30 + (mce_htfAlignmentScore >= 75 ? 40.0 : mce_htfAlignmentScore * 0.30) + (re_resolutionState == "RESOLVED" ? 30.0 : 10.0)
    float te_tp1 = na
    int   _te_bestSc = -1
    int   _te_n = array.size(frz_scoreArr)
    if _te_n > 0 and direction != 0
        for _j = 0 to _te_n - 1
            if _j < array.size(frz_statusArr) and _j < array.size(frz_dirArr) and _j < array.size(frz_topArr) and _j < array.size(frz_botArr)
                string _st2 = array.get(frz_statusArr, _j)
                int    _fd3 = array.get(frz_dirArr,    _j)
                if (_st2 == "Open" or _st2 == "Partial") and _fd3 == direction
                    float _mid2 = (array.get(frz_topArr, _j) + array.get(frz_botArr, _j)) / 2.0
                    bool  _beyond = direction == 1 ? _mid2 > close : _mid2 < close
                    int   _sc2 = array.get(frz_scoreArr, _j)
                    if _beyond and _sc2 > _te_bestSc
                        _te_bestSc := _sc2
                        te_tp1 := _mid2
    bool  te_tp2_valid = not na(eae_primaryAttractorPrice) and (direction == 1 ? eae_primaryAttractorPrice > close : direction == -1 ? eae_primaryAttractorPrice < close : false)
    float te_tp2 = te_tp2_valid ? eae_primaryAttractorPrice : na
    bool  te_tp3_valid = teTertiaryOn and not na(eae_tertiaryAttractorPrice) and (direction == 1 ? eae_tertiaryAttractorPrice > close : direction == -1 ? eae_tertiaryAttractorPrice < close : false)
    float te_tp3 = te_tp3_valid ? eae_tertiaryAttractorPrice : na
    float te_tp1_quality = math.min(eae_secondaryAttractorScore * 0.40 + (frz_attractorConvergence ? 40.0 : frz_bestScore * 0.25) + re_recursiveCompletionScore * 0.15 + mce_execAlignmentScore * 0.20, 100.0)
    float te_tp2_quality = math.min(eae_primaryAttractorScore * 0.50 + re_residualEnergyScore * 0.30 + mce_htfAlignmentScore * 0.20, 100.0)
    float te_tp3_quality = math.min((eae_tertiaryAttractorScore > 0 ? eae_tertiaryAttractorScore * 0.60 : 20.0) + (mce_htfAlignmentScore >= 80 ? 40.0 : mce_htfAlignmentScore * 0.30), 100.0)
    float te_rr_tp1 = (not na(te_tp1) and not na(inv_riskInPts) and inv_riskInPts > 0) ? math.abs(te_tp1 - close) / inv_riskInPts : na
    bool  te_rrGate = not na(te_rr_tp1) and te_rr_tp1 >= rrMinimum
    string te_expectedPath =
         re_resolutionState == "RESOLVED" and mce_execAlignmentScore >= 70 ? "Direct" :
         (ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return") ? "Direct" :
         rot_transferProbability > 50 ? "Retracement First" :
         re_resolutionState == "UNRESOLVED" ? "Range Then Breakout" : "Direct"

    // ── V72.7 Trade Qualification Engine (C4, C6) ────────────────────────────
    float erf_pureConfidence = math.min(20.0 + (re_resolutionState == "RESOLVED" ? 30.0 : re_resolutionState == "PARTIALLY RESOLVED" ? 20.0 : 10.0) + eae_primaryAttractorScore * 0.30, 100.0)
    float frz_entryBonus = (frz_inProximity and frz_bestZoneDir == direction) ? 15.0 : 0.0
    float tqe_frzQuality = frz_activeCount > 0 ? math.min(frz_bestScore * 0.50 + (frz_bestZoneTier == "T1" ? 40.0 : frz_bestZoneTier == "T2" ? 25.0 : frz_bestZoneTier == "T3" ? 10.0 : 0.0) + (frz_bestStatus == "Open" ? 10.0 : frz_bestStatus == "Partial" ? 5.0 : 0.0) + frz_entryBonus, 100.0) : 0.0
    float tqe_liqQuality = math.min(obs_LiquidityScore * 0.50 + ((liqSweepBull or liqSweepBear) ? 30.0 : 0.0) + (liqVacuum ? 20.0 : 0.0), 100.0)
    float tqe_rawScore = ie1a_phaseConfidence * tqeW_ie1a + erf_pureConfidence * tqeW_erf + tqe_frzQuality * tqeW_frz + mce_htfAlignmentScore * tqeW_mce + re_recursiveCompletionScore * tqeW_re + tqe_liqQuality * tqeW_liq
    string tqe_grade = tqe_rawScore >= tqeGradeA1 ? "A+" : tqe_rawScore >= tqeGradeA ? "A" : tqe_rawScore >= tqeGradeB ? "B" : tqe_rawScore >= tqeGradeC ? "C" : "D"
    string tqe_riskLevel = (rot_transferProbability > 65 or re_resolutionState == "UNRESOLVED") ? "HIGH" : (rot_transferProbability > 35 or tqe_rawScore < 60) ? "MEDIUM" : "LOW"

    // ── V72.8 Decision Output Engine (C1, C6) ────────────────────────────────
    string doe_bias =
         displayWaveDir_M5 == 1  and mce_htfAlignmentScore >= 75 and rot_controlStability >= 65 ? "Strong Bullish" :
         displayWaveDir_M5 == 1  ? "Bullish" :
         displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 and mce_htfAlignmentScore >= 75 and rot_controlStability >= 65 ? "Strong Bearish" :
         displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 ? "Bearish" : "Neutral"
    string doe_action =
         inv_invalidated ? "No Trade" :
         (liqg_active and not (liqg_objArrival and liqg_trueCHoCH)) ? "Wait" :
         not erf_entryGate ? "Wait" :
         not te_rrGate ? "Wait" :
         (ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return" and direction == 1)  ? "Long"  :
         (ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return" and direction == -1) ? "Short" : "Wait"
    float doe_confidence = math.min(modelConfidence * 0.50 + mce_alignmentScore * 0.25 + phaseConfidence * 0.25, frz_attractorConvergence ? doeCapConv : doeCapBase)
    string doe_tradeType =
         (ne_dominantNarrative == "Bullish Continuation" or ne_dominantNarrative == "Bearish Continuation") ? "Continuation" :
         (ne_dominantNarrative == "Bullish Pullback"     or ne_dominantNarrative == "Bearish Pullback")     ? "Pullback" :
         (ne_dominantNarrative == "Bullish Rotation"     or ne_dominantNarrative == "Bearish Rotation")     ? "Rotation" :
         ne_dominantNarrative == "Range Development" ? "Range" :
         (ie1a_currentPhase == "New High" or ie1a_currentPhase == "New Low") ? "Breakout" : "Wait"
    float doe_entryMid =
         (frz_inProximity and frz_bestZoneDir == direction and not na(frz_bestZoneMid)) ? frz_bestZoneMid :
         (ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return" and not na(point4OriginHigh) and not na(point4OriginLow)) ? (point4OriginHigh + point4OriginLow) / 2.0 :
         (ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return" and not na(point4OriginHigh) and not na(point4OriginLow)) ? (point4OriginHigh + point4OriginLow) / 2.0 : close
    float doe_entryHigh = not na(doe_entryMid) ? doe_entryMid + atr * 0.30 : na
    float doe_entryLow  = not na(doe_entryMid) ? doe_entryMid - atr * 0.30 : na
    string doe_entryTrigger = frz_inProximity ? "Limit" : (ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return") ? "LimitOnRetest" : "Market"

    // ── V72.8b OPPORTUNITY PROGRESS ENGINE (Phase 1) ─────────────────────────
    // Direction = displayWaveDir_M5 (single source). Progress SYNTHESIZES engine
    // states; it never decides direction. Hard vetoes (no direction / invalidated)
    // force Stand Down; ERF/HTF/phase/MCE are graded contributors, not vetoes.
    float _opStruct    = displayWaveDir_M5 == 0 ? 0.0 : (direction == displayWaveDir_M5 ? 100.0 : 70.0)
    float _opLifecycle =
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return" ? 100.0 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Absorption" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Pre-Convexity" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Induction" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement Liquidity" ? 70.0 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "New High" or ie1a_currentPhase == "New Low" ? 55.0 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Pre-Convexity" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Induction" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion Liquidity" ? 45.0 :
         ie1a_currentPhase == "Point 4 Origin" ? 25.0 : 0.0
    float _opRotation   = rot_transferProbability
    float _opReturn     = na(frz_distanceToZone) ? (frz_inProximity ? 100.0 : 0.0) : math.max(0.0, 100.0 - frz_distanceToZone * 40.0)
    float _opHtf        = mce_htfAlignmentScore
    float _opDisplace   = math.max(re_recursiveCompletionScore, ede_dissipationProgress)
    float _opConfluence = (frz_attractorConvergence ? 50.0 : 0.0) + ((frz_inProximity and frz_bestZoneDir == displayWaveDir_M5) ? 50.0 : 0.0)
    float oppProgressRaw = _opStruct * 0.25 + _opLifecycle * 0.15 + _opRotation * 0.15 + _opReturn * 0.15 + _opHtf * 0.10 + _opDisplace * 0.10 + _opConfluence * 0.10
    bool  oppVeto     = displayWaveDir_M5 == 0 or inv_invalidated
    float oppProgress = oppVeto ? 0.0 : oppProgressRaw
    bool  _opInZone   = frz_inProximity and frz_bestZoneDir == displayWaveDir_M5
    string oppState =
         oppVeto                                ? "STAND DOWN" :
         oppProgress >= 95 and _opInZone        ? "TRADE ACTIVE" :
         oppProgress >= 85                      ? "PREPARE TO EXECUTE" :
         oppProgress >= 60                      ? "OPPORTUNITY CONFIRMING" :
         oppProgress >= 20                      ? "OPPORTUNITY FORMING" : "STAND DOWN"

    // Synthesized intelligence narrative (consumes displayWaveDir_M5 + lifecycle + rotation)
    string _cmdDirWord = displayWaveDir_M5 == 1 ? "Bullish" : displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 ? "Bearish" : "Neutral"
    string cmd_narrative =
         displayWaveDir_M5 == 0 ? "No directional thesis" :
         inv_invalidated ? _cmdDirWord + " thesis invalidated" :
         (ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return") ? _cmdDirWord + " return-to-zone — execution window" :
         rot_transferProbability >= 55 or ie1a_currentPhase == "Absorption" ? _cmdDirWord + " reversal developing" :
         (_ne_phasePullback or ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement") ? _cmdDirWord + " pullback in progress" :
         (ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion" or ie1a_currentPhase == "New High" or ie1a_currentPhase == "New Low") ? _cmdDirWord + " continuation" :
         _cmdDirWord + " developing"

    // ── V72.9 Wave Registry (C5, C12) — var locals persist (single call site) ─
    var array<int>    wr_waveId          = array.new_int()
    var array<int>    wr_parentWaveId    = array.new_int()
    var array<int>    wr_rootWaveId      = array.new_int()
    var array<int>    wr_birthBar        = array.new_int()
    var array<int>    wr_deathBar        = array.new_int()
    var array<string> wr_spawnPhase      = array.new_string()
    var array<string> wr_deathPhase      = array.new_string()
    var array<float>  wr_peakEnergy      = array.new_float()
    var array<float>  wr_resolutionScore = array.new_float()
    var array<int>    wr_waveDepth       = array.new_int()
    var int wr_nextId         = 1
    var int wr_activeWaveId   = 0
    var int wr_activeParentId = 0
    var int wr_activeRootId   = 0
    int     wr_maxEntries     = 50
    int  _wr_prevDir   = nz(direction[1])
    int  _wr_prevCycle = nz(entryCycle[1])
    bool _wr_died     = direction == 0 and _wr_prevDir != 0
    bool _wr_newRoot  = (direction != 0 and _wr_prevDir == 0) or (direction != 0 and _wr_prevDir != 0 and direction != _wr_prevDir)
    bool _wr_newChild = direction != 0 and entryCycle > _wr_prevCycle and not _wr_newRoot
    if _wr_died and wr_activeWaveId > 0
        int _di = array.indexof(wr_waveId, wr_activeWaveId)
        if _di >= 0
            array.set(wr_deathBar,        _di, bar_index)
            array.set(wr_deathPhase,      _di, ie1a_currentPhase)
            array.set(wr_resolutionScore, _di, re_recursiveCompletionScore)
        wr_activeWaveId   := 0
        wr_activeParentId := 0
        wr_activeRootId   := 0
    if _wr_newRoot or _wr_newChild
        int _newId  = wr_nextId
        wr_nextId  := wr_nextId + 1
        int _parent = _wr_newChild ? wr_activeWaveId : 0
        int _root   = _wr_newChild and wr_activeRootId > 0 ? wr_activeRootId : _newId
        int _depth  = _wr_newChild ? math.max(0, entryCycle) : 0
        array.push(wr_waveId,          _newId)
        array.push(wr_parentWaveId,    _parent)
        array.push(wr_rootWaveId,      _root)
        array.push(wr_birthBar,        bar_index)
        array.push(wr_deathBar,        -1)
        array.push(wr_spawnPhase,      ie1a_currentPhase)
        array.push(wr_deathPhase,      "")
        array.push(wr_peakEnergy,      ede_expansionEnergy)
        array.push(wr_resolutionScore, 0.0)
        array.push(wr_waveDepth,       _depth)
        wr_activeWaveId   := _newId
        wr_activeParentId := _parent
        wr_activeRootId   := _root
        if array.size(wr_waveId) > wr_maxEntries
            array.shift(wr_waveId)
            array.shift(wr_parentWaveId)
            array.shift(wr_rootWaveId)
            array.shift(wr_birthBar)
            array.shift(wr_deathBar)
            array.shift(wr_spawnPhase)
            array.shift(wr_deathPhase)
            array.shift(wr_peakEnergy)
            array.shift(wr_resolutionScore)
            array.shift(wr_waveDepth)
    if wr_activeWaveId > 0
        int _ai = array.indexof(wr_waveId, wr_activeWaveId)
        if _ai >= 0 and ede_expansionEnergy > array.get(wr_peakEnergy, _ai)
            array.set(wr_peakEnergy, _ai, ede_expansionEnergy)
    int _wr_depthDisp = 0
    if wr_activeWaveId > 0
        int _aidx = array.indexof(wr_waveId, wr_activeWaveId)
        if _aidx >= 0
            _wr_depthDisp := array.get(wr_waveDepth, _aidx)

    // ── V72.10 Delivery Wave Registry ────────────────────────────────────────
    var array<int>    dwr_waveId          = array.new_int()
    var array<int>    dwr_rootWaveId      = array.new_int()
    var array<int>    dwr_startBar        = array.new_int()
    var array<int>    dwr_endBar          = array.new_int()
    var array<float>  dwr_energy          = array.new_float()
    var array<string> dwr_resolutionState = array.new_string()
    var array<int>    dwr_entryCycle      = array.new_int()
    var int dwr_nextId     = 1
    var int dwr_activeId   = 0
    int     dwr_maxEntries = 50
    var bool _dwr_prevLBD = false
    bool dwr_shouldSpawn = (ede_state == 4 and nz(ede_state[1]) != 4) or (ede_liquidationBecomingDirectional and not _dwr_prevLBD)
    _dwr_prevLBD := ede_liquidationBecomingDirectional
    if dwr_shouldSpawn
        int _did   = dwr_nextId
        dwr_nextId := dwr_nextId + 1
        array.push(dwr_waveId,          _did)
        array.push(dwr_rootWaveId,      wr_activeRootId)
        array.push(dwr_startBar,        bar_index)
        array.push(dwr_endBar,          -1)
        array.push(dwr_energy,          ede_expansionEnergy)
        array.push(dwr_resolutionState, re_resolutionState)
        array.push(dwr_entryCycle,      entryCycle)
        dwr_activeId := _did
        if array.size(dwr_waveId) > dwr_maxEntries
            array.shift(dwr_waveId)
            array.shift(dwr_rootWaveId)
            array.shift(dwr_startBar)
            array.shift(dwr_endBar)
            array.shift(dwr_energy)
            array.shift(dwr_resolutionState)
            array.shift(dwr_entryCycle)
    if dwr_activeId > 0
        int _dwi = array.indexof(dwr_waveId, dwr_activeId)
        if _dwi >= 0
            array.set(dwr_resolutionState, _dwi, re_resolutionState)
            if re_resolutionState == "RESOLVED" and array.get(dwr_endBar, _dwi) == -1
                array.set(dwr_endBar, _dwi, bar_index)

    // ── V72.11 Traceability strings ──────────────────────────────────────────
    string trc_decisionSource = "IE1A:" + ie1a_currentPhase + " | TQE:" + tqe_grade + " | NE:" + ne_dominantNarrative
    string trc_confidenceBreakdown = "IE1A:" + str.tostring(math.round(ie1a_phaseConfidence)) + " ERF:" + str.tostring(math.round(erf_pureConfidence)) + " FRZ:" + str.tostring(math.round(tqe_frzQuality)) + " MCE:" + str.tostring(math.round(mce_htfAlignmentScore)) + " RE:" + str.tostring(math.round(re_recursiveCompletionScore)) + " LIQ:" + str.tostring(math.round(tqe_liqQuality))
    string trc_waveChain = "Wave#" + str.tostring(wr_activeWaveId) + " (parent #" + str.tostring(wr_activeParentId) + ", root #" + str.tostring(wr_activeRootId) + ")"
    string trc_deliveryChain = "Delivery#" + str.tostring(dwr_activeId)

    // ── V72.11.5 TARGET PROJECTION LAYER (TPL) — single live destination ──────
    // Answers "where is price most likely trying to go right now?" by ranking
    // FRZ / EAE attractor / FU imbalance candidates. Direction is the fixed M5
    // structure (displayWaveDir_M5), so the destination is timeframe-independent.
    int   _tpl_bias = displayWaveDir_M5 != 0 ? displayWaveDir_M5 : fractalStackDir
    // Candidates
    float tpl_attractorTarget = eae_primaryAttractorPrice
    float _tpl_fuTop = array.size(fu_top) > 0 ? array.get(fu_top, array.size(fu_top) - 1) : na
    float _tpl_fuBot = array.size(fu_bot) > 0 ? array.get(fu_bot, array.size(fu_bot) - 1) : na
    bool _tpl_attOK = not na(tpl_attractorTarget) and _tpl_bias != 0 and (_tpl_bias == 1 ? tpl_attractorTarget > close : tpl_attractorTarget < close)
    // Winner
    float  tpl_mainTarget = na
    string tpl_source     = "–"
    float  tpl_confidence = 0.0
    // Winner — HIGHEST SCORE wins (not priority, not closest, not highest residual,
    // not first-found). Each candidate's score already encodes its hierarchy weight;
    // ties resolve FU > Attractor > FRZ to honour the imbalance-first hierarchy.
    // ═══ STRUCTURAL DESTINATION ENGINE V2 — aggressive candidate search ═══
    // Reuses ONLY existing structural objects (FU candles, FRZ zones, liquidity
    // pools, EAE attractor, prior swing extremes). Generates many candidates,
    // scores each, takes the ARGMAX, classifies quality, and SUPPRESSES weak
    // zones (only A+/A++/A+++ become visible).
    array<float>  dc_px = array.new_float()
    array<float>  dc_sc = array.new_float()
    array<string> dc_ty = array.new_string()
    array<string> dc_cl = array.new_string()
    // 1) FU candles (+ FU/imbalance overlap, + residual FU) — top structural tier
    if _tpl_bias != 0 and array.size(fu_top) > 0
        for _i = 0 to array.size(fu_top) - 1
            float  _fmid = (array.get(fu_top, _i) + array.get(fu_bot, _i)) / 2.0
            int    _fdir = array.get(fu_dir, _i)
            string _fst  = array.get(fu_state, _i)
            if _fst != "Invalidated" and (_tpl_bias == 1 ? _fmid > close : _fmid < close)
                float _ov   = (frz_activeCount > 0 and not na(frz_bestZoneMid) and math.abs(_fmid - frz_bestZoneMid) / math.max(atr, 1e-10) < 1.0) ? 12.0 : 0.0
                float _b    = (_fst == "Fresh" or _fst == "Active") ? 82.0 : _fst == "Interacting" ? 76.0 : 70.0
                float _dpen = math.min(math.abs(close - _fmid) / math.max(atr, 1e-10) * 2.0, 22.0)
                float _al   = (_fdir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? 8.0 : 0.0) + (_fdir == liveHtfAlign and liveHtfAlign != 0 ? 6.0 : 0.0)
                array.push(dc_px, _fmid)
                array.push(dc_sc, math.min(_b + _ov + _al + erf_tradeReadiness * 0.06 - _dpen, 100.0))
                array.push(dc_ty, _ov > 0 ? "FU + imbalance overlap" : _fst == "Interacting" ? "Residual FU" : "FU candle")
                array.push(dc_cl, "")
    // 1B) FU WICK AUTHORITY (1A.8/1A.9) — captured left-liquidity pool is the
    //     HIGHEST-priority destination (Priority 1); its induction band Priority 2.
    //     Recursive: the winner is the highest-TF validated FU pool aligned w/ bias.
    if _tpl_bias != 0 and not na(fu_winTarget) and (_tpl_bias == 1 ? fu_winTarget > close : fu_winTarget < close)
        float _fudpen = math.min(math.abs(close - fu_winTarget) / math.max(atr, 1e-10) * 1.5, 14.0)
        array.push(dc_px, fu_winTarget)
        array.push(dc_sc, math.min(96.0 + fu_recursiveAlign * 0.04 - _fudpen, 100.0))
        array.push(dc_ty, fu_winSrc + " (magnet)")
        array.push(dc_cl, "")
    if _tpl_bias != 0 and not na(fu_winBand) and (_tpl_bias == 1 ? fu_winBand > close : fu_winBand < close)
        array.push(dc_px, fu_winBand)
        array.push(dc_sc, 90.0)
        array.push(dc_ty, "FU induction band")
        array.push(dc_cl, "")
    // 2) FRZ zones (curated, pre-scored imbalance / return zones)
    if _tpl_bias != 0 and array.size(frz_topArr) > 0
        for _i = 0 to array.size(frz_topArr) - 1
            string _fzst = array.get(frz_statusArr, _i)
            if _fzst == "Open" or _fzst == "Partial"
                float _zmid = (array.get(frz_topArr, _i) + array.get(frz_botArr, _i)) / 2.0
                int   _zdir = array.get(frz_dirArr, _i)
                if _tpl_bias == 1 ? _zmid > close : _zmid < close
                    float _zsc  = array.get(frz_scoreArr, _i)
                    float _dpen = math.min(math.abs(close - _zmid) / math.max(atr, 1e-10) * 2.0, 22.0)
                    float _al   = (_zdir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? 8.0 : 0.0) + (_zdir == liveHtfAlign and liveHtfAlign != 0 ? 6.0 : 0.0)
                    array.push(dc_px, _zmid)
                    array.push(dc_sc, math.min(_zsc * 0.85 + _al + erf_tradeReadiness * 0.06 - _dpen, 100.0))
                    array.push(dc_ty, "FRZ " + array.get(frz_tierArr, _i))
                    array.push(dc_cl, "")
    // 3) EAE flip / residual attractor (LOW base — the weak candidate to demote)
    if _tpl_attOK
        array.push(dc_px, tpl_attractorTarget)
        array.push(dc_sc, math.min(eae_primaryAttractorScore * 0.45 + (eae_primaryAttractorScore >= 70 ? 6.0 : 0.0), 100.0))
        array.push(dc_ty, "Flip / residual")
        array.push(dc_cl, "")
    // Classify every candidate by quality band
    if array.size(dc_sc) > 0
        for _i = 0 to array.size(dc_sc) - 1
            float _s = array.get(dc_sc, _i)
            array.set(dc_cl, _i, _s >= 92 ? "A+++" : _s >= 85 ? "A++" : _s >= 78 ? "A+" : _s >= 68 ? "A" : _s >= 55 ? "B" : _s >= 40 ? "C" : "Weak")
    // ARGMAX — highest score wins (no priority / first-found / residual default).
    // All array.get calls are guarded by size checks (Pine evaluates both sides of
    // and/ternary, so a -1 index would throw — hence explicit if-blocks).
    int    _dcN            = array.size(dc_sc)
    float  dc_bestScore    = 0.0
    float  dc_bestPrice    = na
    string dc_bestType     = "-"
    float  dc_price2       = na
    float  dc_price3       = na
    string dc_lbl2         = ""
    string dc_lbl3         = ""
    string tpl_winnerClass = "Weak"
    string dc_primaryStr   = "No destination yet"
    string dc_secondaryStr = "-"
    string dc_thirdStr     = "-"
    string dc_scoreboard   = "No structural candidates"
    bool   dc_aClass       = false
    tpl_source     := "RANGEBOUND"
    tpl_confidence := 0.0
    if _dcN > 0
        array<int> dc_order = array.sort_indices(dc_sc, order.descending)
        int _i1 = array.get(dc_order, 0)
        dc_bestScore    := array.get(dc_sc, _i1)
        dc_bestPrice    := array.get(dc_px, _i1)
        dc_bestType     := array.get(dc_ty, _i1)
        tpl_winnerClass := array.get(dc_cl, _i1)
        tpl_confidence  := dc_bestScore
        dc_aClass       := dc_bestScore >= 78
        if dc_bestScore >= 55
            tpl_mainTarget := dc_bestPrice
            tpl_source     := dc_bestType
            dc_primaryStr  := f_v72_px(dc_bestPrice) + "\n" + tpl_winnerClass + " quality\n" + dc_bestType + "\nScore " + str.tostring(math.round(dc_bestScore))
        if _dcN > 1
            int _i2 = array.get(dc_order, 1)
            dc_price2 := array.get(dc_px, _i2)
            dc_lbl2   := array.get(dc_cl, _i2) + " " + array.get(dc_ty, _i2)
            if array.get(dc_sc, _i2) >= 55
                dc_secondaryStr := f_v72_px(array.get(dc_px, _i2)) + "  " + array.get(dc_cl, _i2) + "  " + array.get(dc_ty, _i2) + "  S" + str.tostring(math.round(array.get(dc_sc, _i2)))
        if _dcN > 2
            int _i3 = array.get(dc_order, 2)
            dc_price3 := array.get(dc_px, _i3)
            dc_lbl3   := array.get(dc_cl, _i3) + " " + array.get(dc_ty, _i3)
            if array.get(dc_sc, _i3) >= 55
                dc_thirdStr := f_v72_px(array.get(dc_px, _i3)) + "  " + array.get(dc_cl, _i3) + "  " + array.get(dc_ty, _i3) + "  S" + str.tostring(math.round(array.get(dc_sc, _i3)))
        dc_scoreboard := ""
        for _k = 0 to math.min(_dcN - 1, 4)
            int _oi = array.get(dc_order, _k)
            dc_scoreboard := dc_scoreboard + (_k > 0 ? "\n" : "") + array.get(dc_cl, _oi) + " " + str.tostring(math.round(array.get(dc_sc, _oi))) + "  " + array.get(dc_ty, _oi)
    // No weak fallback: when no A-class structural zone exists, tpl_mainTarget
    // stays na and the panel shows "SCANNING" instead of a low-quality projection.
    // ── Opposite-side destination — where price likely heads if the trade TURNS ──
    float  tpl_revTarget = na
    string tpl_revSource = "off"
    float  tpl_distanceATR = not na(tpl_mainTarget) ? math.abs(close - tpl_mainTarget) / math.max(atr, 1e-10) : na
    string tpl_status = na(tpl_mainTarget) ? "RANGEBOUND" : tpl_winnerClass + " MAGNET"

    // Top-3 most-probable destination zones drawn ON the chart (always visible)
    var line  tpl_line  = na
    var label tpl_label = na
    var line  dc_line2  = na
    var label dc_lab2   = na
    var line  dc_line3  = na
    var label dc_lab3   = na
    if barstate.islast and showV72Destination
        if not na(tpl_line)
            line.delete(tpl_line)
        if not na(tpl_label)
            label.delete(tpl_label)
        if not na(dc_line2)
            line.delete(dc_line2)
        if not na(dc_lab2)
            label.delete(dc_lab2)
        if not na(dc_line3)
            line.delete(dc_line3)
        if not na(dc_lab3)
            label.delete(dc_lab3)
        if not na(dc_bestPrice)
            tpl_line  := line.new(bar_index, dc_bestPrice, bar_index + 60, dc_bestPrice, width=3, color=color.new(#ffd000, 0))
            tpl_label := label.new(bar_index + 60, dc_bestPrice, "1  " + dc_bestType + "  " + tpl_winnerClass + "  " + str.tostring(math.round_to_mintick(dc_bestPrice)), style=label.style_label_left, color=color.new(#0a0a30, 0), textcolor=#ffd000, size=size.small)
        if not na(dc_price2)
            dc_line2 := line.new(bar_index, dc_price2, bar_index + 60, dc_price2, width=2, color=color.new(#00d0ff, 20), style=line.style_dashed)
            dc_lab2  := label.new(bar_index + 60, dc_price2, "2  " + dc_lbl2 + "  " + str.tostring(math.round_to_mintick(dc_price2)), style=label.style_label_left, color=color.new(#0a0a30, 0), textcolor=#00d0ff, size=size.tiny)
        if not na(dc_price3)
            dc_line3 := line.new(bar_index, dc_price3, bar_index + 60, dc_price3, width=1, color=color.new(#a0a0c0, 30), style=line.style_dotted)
            dc_lab3  := label.new(bar_index + 60, dc_price3, "3  " + dc_lbl3 + "  " + str.tostring(math.round_to_mintick(dc_price3)), style=label.style_label_left, color=color.new(#0a0a30, 0), textcolor=#a0a0c0, size=size.tiny)

    // Opposite-side destination line (dotted, dim) — shown only if toggled
    var line  tpl_revLine  = na
    var label tpl_revLabel = na
    if barstate.islast and showV72Destination and showV72RevDest
        if not na(tpl_revLine)
            line.delete(tpl_revLine)
        if not na(tpl_revLabel)
            label.delete(tpl_revLabel)
        if not na(tpl_revTarget)
            tpl_revLine := line.new(bar_index, tpl_revTarget, bar_index + 50, tpl_revTarget, width=1, color=color.new(color.orange, 20), style=line.style_dotted)
            tpl_revLabel := label.new(bar_index + 50, tpl_revTarget,
                 "REV DEST\n" + str.tostring(math.round_to_mintick(tpl_revTarget)) + "\n" + tpl_revSource,
                 style=label.style_label_left, color=color.new(#1a0a00, 0), textcolor=color.orange, size=size.small)

    // ── V72 DESTINATION is rendered inside the V72 COMMAND panel below (the
    //    standalone top_left panel was hidden behind the chart legend). ────────

    // ── V72.11.9 Command-panel + destination EXPLAINABILITY strings (display) ─
    // Intrinsic candidate scores — computed independent of the directional
    // eligibility gate so the scoreboard ALWAYS shows numbers (a candidate shows
    // 0 only when it has no data at all, never a blind dash).
    // V2 diagnostic scoreboard — top structural candidates (proves winner = max).
    string tpl_scoreboard = dc_scoreboard
    // Destination friendly type + letter class (from the winning candidate score).
    string _destClass = tpl_winnerClass
    string _destType  = tpl_source
    // Multi-line winner reasoning (the fallback projection case is fully expanded).
    string tpl_reason = dc_aClass ? (tpl_winnerClass + " structural zone\n" + tpl_source + (mce_htfAlignmentScore >= 60 ? "\nHTF aligned" : "")) : "No A-class zone yet\nExpanding candidate search\nWeak fallbacks suppressed"
    // Per-timeframe stack alignment (multi-line ✓/✗ vs dominant stack direction).
    string _cmdStackPerTf =
           "M1 "  + (m1_dir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? "✓" : "✗")
         + "\nM3 "  + (l3_dir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? "✓" : "✗")
         + "\nM5 "  + (l0_dir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? "✓" : "✗")
         + "\nM15 " + (l1_dir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? "✓" : "✗")
         + "\nH1 "  + (l2_dir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? "✓" : "✗")
         + "\nH4 "  + (l4_dir == fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? "✓" : "✗")
    string _cmdStackSummary = (fractalStackDir == 1 ? "Bullish stack" : fractalStackDir == -1 ? "Bearish stack" : "No stack bias")
         + "\n" + str.tostring(_stackBull) + " Bull   " + str.tostring(_stackBear) + " Bear"
         + "\nAlignment " + str.tostring(math.round(fractalStackScore)) + "%\n" + _cmdStackPerTf
    // HTF Read — multi-line WHY (per-TF wave + consensus verdict + strength %).
    // ROTATION STATE (replaces consensus language) — describes pressure transfer
    // across M15 (l1) -> H1 (l2) -> H4 (l4) in the rotational model.
    string _rotWave1   = l1_dir == 1 ? "Bullish" : l1_dir == -1 ? "Bearish" : "flat"
    string _rotWave2   = l2_dir == 1 ? "Bullish" : l2_dir == -1 ? "Bearish" : "flat"
    string _rotWave4   = l4_dir == 1 ? "Bullish" : l4_dir == -1 ? "Bearish" : "flat"
    bool   _rotCascade = l1_dir != 0 and l1_dir == l2_dir and l2_dir == l4_dir
    bool   _rotMature  = l1_dir != 0 and l1_dir == l2_dir and l2_dir != l4_dir
    bool   _rotActive  = l1_dir != 0 and l2_dir != 0 and l1_dir != l2_dir
    string _rotState   = _rotCascade ? "FULL CASCADE" : _rotMature ? "ROTATION MATURE" : _rotActive ? "ROTATION ACTIVE" : "ROTATION BUILDING"
    string _rotPress   = _rotCascade ? "Full rotational alignment" : _rotMature ? "Pressure transferring upward" : _rotActive ? "Pressure transferring" : "Pressure accumulating"
    string _cmdHtfWhy  = _rotState + "\nM15 " + _rotWave1 + "\nH1 " + _rotWave2 + "\nH4 " + _rotWave4 + "\n" + _rotPress
    // Exec Read — multi-line WHY (M1/M3/M5 words + phase + gate + missing TF).
    string _execMissing =
           (m1_dir != fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? "M1 " : "")
         + (l3_dir != fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? "M3 " : "")
         + (l0_dir != fractalStackDir and fractalStackDir != 0 ? "M5 " : "")
    string _cmdExecWhy = "M1 " + (m1_dir == 1 ? "bullish" : m1_dir == -1 ? "bearish" : "flat")
         + "\nM3 " + (l3_dir == 1 ? "bullish" : l3_dir == -1 ? "bearish" : "flat")
         + "\nM5 " + (l0_dir == 1 ? "bullish" : l0_dir == -1 ? "bearish" : "flat")
         + "\n" + ie1a_currentPhase + " active"
         + (erf_entryGate ? "\nEntry gate armed" : "\nEntry gate not armed")
         + (str.length(_execMissing) > 0 ? "\nMissing: " + _execMissing : "")
    // Opportunity class word.
    string _cmdOppClass = oppProgress >= 85 ? "High quality" : oppProgress >= 60 ? "Confirming" : oppProgress >= 20 ? "Developing" : "Stand down"

    // ══════════ MARKET OPERATING SYSTEM (MOS) — cognition / language layer ══════════
    // Natural-language intelligence composed ONLY from existing engine outputs
    // (Engine 1A phase, rotation state, destination engine, opportunity, threats,
    // stack). No new math — these are sentences, not variables.
    string _mosSide   = displayWaveDir_M5 == 1 ? "buyers" : displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 ? "sellers" : "neither side"
    // Concrete price references so the language names LEVELS, never just "structure".
    string _mosDestPx = na(dc_bestPrice) ? "" : f_v72_px(dc_bestPrice)
    string _mosRetPx  = not na(frz_bestZoneMid) ? f_v72_px(frz_bestZoneMid) : not na(eae_primaryAttractorPrice) ? f_v72_px(eae_primaryAttractorPrice) : not na(point4OriginLow) ? f_v72_px(displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 ? point4OriginHigh : point4OriginLow) : "the return zone"
    string _mosStopPx = na(inv_activeStop) ? "the invalidation level" : f_v72_px(inv_activeStop)
    string story_now    = currentDisplayPhase + " is the active phase and " + _mosSide + " hold the initiative."
    string story_why    = _rotState == "FULL CASCADE"   ? "All timeframes are aligned and pressure flows one way." : _rotState == "ROTATION MATURE" ? "Pressure is transferring up the timeframes; the move is maturing." : _rotState == "ROTATION ACTIVE" ? "Control is rotating between timeframes as pressure transfers." : "Pressure is still accumulating before a clear transfer."
    string story_dest   = not na(dc_bestPrice) ? ("Price is being drawn toward " + _mosDestPx + " - the " + dc_bestType + " (" + tpl_winnerClass + " quality).") : "No destination has formed; the market is rangebound."
    string story_threat = inv_invalidated ? ("Structure is invalidated; a break of " + _mosStopPx + " ends continuation.") : (liqg_active and not (liqg_objArrival and liqg_trueCHoCH)) ? ("Objective at " + (na(liqg_target) ? "target" : f_v72_px(liqg_target)) + " not yet reached - reversal unconfirmed.") : _ep_conflict ? "LTF stack is in conflict with HTF - elevated reversal risk." : (displayWaveDir_H1 != 0 and displayWaveDir_H1 != displayWaveDir_M5) ? "H1 disagrees with the execution wave - the main risk to continuation." : ("Continuation holds while price stays beyond " + _mosStopPx + ".")
    string story_outlook= oppState == "TRADE ACTIVE" ? "A live opportunity is in play." : oppState == "PREPARE TO EXECUTE" ? ("Conditions are lining up for entry near " + _mosRetPx + ".") : oppProgress >= 20 ? "An opportunity is developing but unconfirmed." : "Best to stand aside until structure improves."
    string cop_next     = not na(dc_bestPrice) ? ((displayWaveDir_M5 == 1 ? "Upside" : displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 ? "Downside" : "Movement") + " toward " + _mosDestPx + " stays favoured while " + _mosStopPx + " holds.") : "Direction stays unresolved until a wave takes control."
    string cop_action   = (oppState == "PREPARE TO EXECUTE" or oppState == "TRADE ACTIVE") ? ("Act if price reacts at " + _mosRetPx + "; invalidation at " + _mosStopPx + ".") : ("Wait for price to reach " + _mosRetPx + " before committing.")

    // ── CONTROL MATRIX (who holds authority) ──
    string _ctlArrowM1  = displayWaveDir_M1  == 1 ? "▲ Bulls" : displayWaveDir_M1  == -1 ? "▼ Bears" : "○ Neutral"
    string _ctlArrowM3  = displayWaveDir_M3  == 1 ? "▲ Bulls" : displayWaveDir_M3  == -1 ? "▼ Bears" : "○ Neutral"
    string _ctlArrowM5  = displayWaveDir_M5  == 1 ? "▲ Bulls" : displayWaveDir_M5  == -1 ? "▼ Bears" : "○ Neutral"
    string _ctlArrowM15 = displayWaveDir_M15 == 1 ? "▲ Bulls" : displayWaveDir_M15 == -1 ? "▼ Bears" : "○ Neutral"
    string _ctlArrowH1  = displayWaveDir_H1  == 1 ? "▲ Bulls" : displayWaveDir_H1  == -1 ? "▼ Bears" : "○ Neutral"
    string _ctlArrowH4  = displayWaveDir_H4  == 1 ? "▲ Bulls" : displayWaveDir_H4  == -1 ? "▼ Bears" : "○ Neutral"
    string control_state     = fractalStackScore >= 80 ? "DOMINANT" : fractalStackScore >= 60 ? "STABLE" : fractalStackScore >= 40 ? "CONTESTED" : "FRAGMENTED"
    string control_transfer  = _rotCascade ? "FULL CASCADE" : _rotMature ? "TRANSFER UPWARD" : _rotActive ? "ROTATING" : "FORMING"
    // ── THREAT MATRIX ──
    bool   _thrH1   = displayWaveDir_H1 != 0 and displayWaveDir_H1 != displayWaveDir_M5
    int    _thrCnt  = (inv_invalidated ? 1 : 0) + (_thrH1 ? 1 : 0) + (not erf_entryGate ? 1 : 0) + (_ep_conflict ? 1 : 0)
    string threat_state = _thrCnt == 0 ? "CLEAR" : _thrCnt == 1 ? "CAUTION" : _thrCnt == 2 ? "ELEVATED" : "DANGER"
    string threat_list  = (inv_invalidated ? "⚠ Structure invalidated\n" : "") + (_ep_conflict ? "⚠ HTF/LTF conflict\n" : "") + (_thrH1 ? "⚠ H1 disagreement\n" : "") + (not erf_entryGate ? "⚠ Entry gate closed\n" : "")
    string threat_show  = threat_list == "" ? "✓ Clear - no active threats" : threat_list
    // ── DESTINATION WAR winner state ──
    string war_state = liqg_objArrival ? "OBJECTIVE REACHED" : liqg_active ? "LIQUIDATING" : tpl_winnerClass == "A+++" or tpl_winnerClass == "A++" ? "MAGNET" : tpl_winnerClass == "A+" or tpl_winnerClass == "A" ? "COMPETING" : na(dc_bestPrice) ? "NONE" : "UNSTABLE"
    // ── ENERGY NETWORK / TIMELINE states ──
    string energy_state   = _rotCascade ? "PEAK" : _rotMature ? "TRANSFER" : _rotActive ? "BUILDING" : "DORMANT"
    string timeline_state = liqg_objArrival ? "PEAKING" : liqg_active ? "ACCELERATING" : (ie1a_currentPhase == "Expansion" or ie1a_currentPhase == "New High" or ie1a_currentPhase == "New Low") ? "ACCELERATING" : ie1a_currentPhase == "Absorption" ? "PEAKING" : (ie1a_currentPhase == "Retracement" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Demand Return" or ie1a_currentPhase == "Supply Return") ? "TRANSITIONING" : "CONTINUING"
    string timeline_eta   = na(tpl_distanceATR) ? "target forming" : str.tostring(tpl_distanceATR, "#.0") + " ATR to destination"
    // ── COMMANDER verdict + EXECUTION copilot (the trader) ──
    string mos_commander = oppState == "TRADE ACTIVE" ? "ATTACK" : oppState == "PREPARE TO EXECUTE" ? ("PREPARE " + (displayWaveDir_M5 == 1 ? "LONG" : displayWaveDir_M5 == -1 ? "SHORT" : "")) : inv_invalidated ? "STAND DOWN" : threat_state == "DANGER" ? "REDUCE RISK" : oppProgress >= 20 ? "WAIT" : "STAND DOWN"
    string mos_conf      = oppProgress >= 75 ? "HIGH" : oppProgress >= 45 ? "MEDIUM" : "LOW"
    string mos_operation = oppState == "TRADE ACTIVE" ? "MANAGE THE ACTIVE POSITION." : oppState == "PREPARE TO EXECUTE" ? ("WAIT FOR RETURN INTO " + _mosRetPx + ".") : oppProgress >= 20 ? "LET THE SETUP MATURE." : "NO ACTIONABLE SETUP - STAND ASIDE."
    string exec_trigger  = na(frz_distanceToZone) ? "Return-zone interaction" : ("FRZ proximity - " + str.tostring(frz_distanceToZone, "#.0") + " ATR away")
    string exec_entry    = (na(doe_entryLow) or na(doe_entryHigh)) ? "forming" : (f_v72_px(doe_entryLow) + " - " + f_v72_px(doe_entryHigh))
    string exec_stop     = na(inv_activeStop) ? "n/a" : f_v72_px(inv_activeStop)
    string exec_target   = not na(dc_bestPrice) ? f_v72_px(dc_bestPrice) : na(te_tp1) ? "n/a" : f_v72_px(te_tp1)
    string exec_blocker  = na(tpl_distanceATR) ? "destination forming" : ("Distance to target " + str.tostring(tpl_distanceATR, "#.0") + " ATR")


    // ── V72.12 Dashboards ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    if barstate.islast and showTable and showV72Command
        var table mosStory = table.new(position.top_center, 1, 10, bgcolor=color.new(#0b0b1c, 6), frame_color=color.new(#00e5ff, 25), frame_width=2, border_width=0)
        table.cell(mosStory, 0, 0, "════════  MARKET STORY  ════════", text_color=#00ffcc, text_size=size.normal)
        table.cell(mosStory, 0, 1, liqg_active ? (liqg_title + " — " + liqg_subPhase) : story_now, text_color=(liqg_active ? #ffd000 : color.white), text_size=size.normal)
        table.cell(mosStory, 0, 2, story_why,     text_color=color.silver, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosStory, 0, 3, story_dest,    text_color=color.aqua,   text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosStory, 0, 4, story_threat,  text_color=(inv_invalidated ? color.red : color.orange), text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosStory, 0, 5, story_outlook, text_color=(oppProgress >= 60 ? color.lime : color.yellow), text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosStory, 0, 6, "WAVE   " + cmd_narrative, text_color=#9fb0d8, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosStory, 0, 7, "OPERATION   " + mos_operation, text_color=#ffe05a, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosStory, 0, 8, "COMMANDER   " + mos_commander + "   (conf " + mos_conf + ")", text_color=(mos_commander == "ATTACK" ? #00ff88 : (mos_commander == "STAND DOWN" or mos_commander == "REDUCE RISK") ? #ff5a5a : #ffd000), text_size=size.normal)
        table.cell(mosStory, 0, 9, liqg_readout, text_color=(liqg_active ? #ffd000 : color.gray), text_size=size.small)

        // ── SECTION 2: CONTROL MATRIX (top left) — who holds authority ──
        var table mosCtl = table.new(position.top_left, 1, 9, bgcolor=color.new(#0b0b1c, 6), frame_color=color.new(#00e5ff, 25), frame_width=2, border_width=0)
        table.cell(mosCtl, 0, 0, "═══  CONTROL  ═══", text_color=#00e5ff, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosCtl, 0, 1, "M1   " + _ctlArrowM1,  text_color=(displayWaveDir_M1  == 1 ? #5aff9e : displayWaveDir_M1  == -1 ? #ff5a5a : color.gray), text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosCtl, 0, 2, "M3   " + _ctlArrowM3,  text_color=(displayWaveDir_M3  == 1 ? #5aff9e : displayWaveDir_M3  == -1 ? #ff5a5a : color.gray), text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosCtl, 0, 3, "M5   " + _ctlArrowM5,  text_color=(displayWaveDir_M5  == 1 ? #5aff9e : displayWaveDir_M5  == -1 ? #ff5a5a : color.gray), text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosCtl, 0, 4, "M15  " + _ctlArrowM15, text_color=(displayWaveDir_M15 == 1 ? #5aff9e : displayWaveDir_M15 == -1 ? #ff5a5a : color.gray), text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosCtl, 0, 5, "H1   " + _ctlArrowH1,  text_color=(displayWaveDir_H1  == 1 ? #5aff9e : displayWaveDir_H1  == -1 ? #ff5a5a : color.gray), text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosCtl, 0, 6, "H4   " + _ctlArrowH4,  text_color=(displayWaveDir_H4  == 1 ? #5aff9e : displayWaveDir_H4  == -1 ? #ff5a5a : color.gray), text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosCtl, 0, 7, "Authority " + f_mosBar(fractalStackScore), text_color=(fractalStackScore >= 60 ? #5aff9e : fractalStackScore >= 40 ? #ffe05a : #ff5a5a), text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosCtl, 0, 8, control_state + "  ·  " + control_transfer, text_color=color.white, text_size=size.small)

        // ── SECTION 5: DESTINATION WAR (top right) — candidate competition ──
        var table mosWar = table.new(position.top_right, 1, 6, bgcolor=color.new(#0b0b1c, 6), frame_color=color.new(#00e5ff, 25), frame_width=2, border_width=0)
        table.cell(mosWar, 0, 0, "═══  DESTINATION WAR  ═══", text_color=#00e5ff, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosWar, 0, 1, na(dc_bestPrice) ? "No active competition" : ("WINNER  " + dc_bestType), text_color=#5aff9e, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosWar, 0, 2, na(dc_bestPrice) ? "-" : (_mosDestPx + "   " + tpl_winnerClass + "   " + war_state), text_color=color.white, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosWar, 0, 3, na(dc_bestPrice) ? "" : f_mosBar(dc_bestScore), text_color=#5ad1ff, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosWar, 0, 4, "─ field ─", text_color=#7a86a8, text_size=size.tiny)
        table.cell(mosWar, 0, 5, dc_scoreboard, text_color=#b8c4e0, text_size=size.tiny)


        // ── SECTION 7: THREAT MATRIX (bottom left) ──
        var table mosThr = table.new(position.bottom_left, 1, 3, bgcolor=color.new(#0b0b1c, 6), frame_color=color.new(#00e5ff, 25), frame_width=2, border_width=0)
        table.cell(mosThr, 0, 0, "═══  THREATS  ═══", text_color=#00e5ff, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosThr, 0, 1, threat_state + "   " + f_mosBar(_thrCnt * 33.0), text_color=(_thrCnt == 0 ? #5aff9e : _thrCnt == 1 ? #ffe05a : _thrCnt == 2 ? #ffb347 : #ff5a5a), text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosThr, 0, 2, threat_show, text_color=color.white, text_size=size.small)

        var table mosCop = table.new(position.bottom_right, 1, 6, bgcolor=color.new(#0b0b1c, 6), frame_color=color.new(#00e5ff, 25), frame_width=2, border_width=0)
        table.cell(mosCop, 0, 0, "──────  COPILOT  ──────", text_color=#00ffcc, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosCop, 0, 1, "CURRENT   " + currentDisplayPhase + " remains the dominant behaviour.", text_color=color.white, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosCop, 0, 2, "WHY       " + story_why, text_color=color.silver, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosCop, 0, 3, "NEXT      " + cop_next, text_color=color.aqua, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosCop, 0, 4, "THREAT    " + story_threat, text_color=color.orange, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosCop, 0, 5, "ACTION    " + cop_action, text_color=color.lime, text_size=size.small)

        // ── SECTION 3: ENERGY NETWORK (middle left) — pressure flow ──
        var table mosEng = table.new(position.middle_left, 1, 5, bgcolor=color.new(#0b0b1c, 6), frame_color=color.new(#00e5ff, 25), frame_width=2, border_width=0)
        table.cell(mosEng, 0, 0, "═══  ENERGY  ═══", text_color=#00e5ff, text_size=size.small)

        table.cell(mosEng, 0, 2, "Control  " + f_mosBar(rot_controlStability), text_color=#5ad1ff, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosEng, 0, 3, "Flow  " + control_transfer, text_color=color.white, text_size=size.small)
        table.cell(mosEng, 0, 4, "State " + energy_state, text_color=(_rotCascade or _rotMature ? #5aff9e : #ffe05a), text_size=size.small)

        // ── SECTION 6: OPPORTUNITY REACTOR (middle right) ──
        var table mosRct = table.new(position.middle_right, 1, 5, bgcolor=color.new(#0b0b1c, 6), frame_color=color.new(#00e5ff, 25), frame_width=2, border_width=0)

        // (Timeline now covered by the restored P3 dashboard at bottom_center)

        var table mosExe = table.new(position.middle_center, 1, 9, bgcolor=color.new(#0b0b1c, 4), frame_color=color.new(#ffd000, 25), frame_width=2, border_width=0)
