// ── Run the V72 engine once per bar ──────────────────────────────────────────
f_v72_run(nz(dir_tf3_raw), nz(dir_tf4_raw), v72F, v72I, v72B, v72Sz)

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ENGINE 1A.11 / 1A.12 — FU CONVERSATION ROUTE + AFE ECHO (arrows only).
// Draws the active route as connected arrows through the high-authority validated
// FU nodes on the bias side (W -> D -> H4 -> H1 -> M15 -> M5), nearest-first, only
// when path confidence clears fuRouteMinConf. Nodes below fuAuthMin are noise and
// excluded. AFE echo arrow points to the active flip/FU target.
var array<line> conv_route = array.new<line>()
var label conv_routeLbl    = na
var line  afe_arrow        = na
if barstate.islast
    if array.size(conv_route) > 0
        for _li = 0 to array.size(conv_route) - 1
            line.delete(array.get(conv_route, _li))
        array.clear(conv_route)
    if not na(conv_routeLbl)
        label.delete(conv_routeLbl)
    if not na(afe_arrow)
        line.delete(afe_arrow)
    if showFUConv and conv_bias != 0 and conv_confidence >= fuRouteMinConf
        array<float> _rt = array.new_float()
        if nz(w_fuValid)   == 1 and not na(w_fuTip)   and nz(w_fuScore)   >= fuAuthMin and (conv_bias == 1 ? w_fuTip   > close : w_fuTip   < close)
            array.push(_rt, w_fuTip)
        if nz(d_fuValid)   == 1 and not na(d_fuTip)   and nz(d_fuScore)   >= fuAuthMin and (conv_bias == 1 ? d_fuTip   > close : d_fuTip   < close)
            array.push(_rt, d_fuTip)
        if nz(h4_fuValid)  == 1 and not na(h4_fuTip)  and nz(h4_fuScore)  >= fuAuthMin and (conv_bias == 1 ? h4_fuTip  > close : h4_fuTip  < close)
            array.push(_rt, h4_fuTip)
        if nz(h1_fuValid)  == 1 and not na(h1_fuTip)  and nz(h1_fuScore)  >= fuAuthMin and (conv_bias == 1 ? h1_fuTip  > close : h1_fuTip  < close)
            array.push(_rt, h1_fuTip)
        if nz(m15_fuValid) == 1 and not na(m15_fuTip) and nz(m15_fuScore) >= fuAuthMin and (conv_bias == 1 ? m15_fuTip > close : m15_fuTip < close)
            array.push(_rt, m15_fuTip)
        if nz(m5_fuValid)  == 1 and not na(m5_fuTip)  and nz(m5_fuScore)  >= fuAuthMin and (conv_bias == 1 ? m5_fuTip  > close : m5_fuTip  < close)
            array.push(_rt, m5_fuTip)
        if array.size(_rt) > 0
            array.sort(_rt, conv_bias == 1 ? order.ascending : order.descending)
            int   _rx = bar_index
            float _ry = close
            for _ri = 0 to array.size(_rt) - 1
                float _rn  = array.get(_rt, _ri)
                int   _rx2 = _rx + 9
                array.push(conv_route, line.new(_rx, _ry, _rx2, _rn, color=color.new(#b388ff, 0), width=2, style=line.style_arrow_right))
                _rx := _rx2
                _ry := _rn
            conv_routeLbl := label.new(_rx, _ry, conv_seekTf + " FU  " + str.tostring(math.round(conv_confidence)) + "%", style=label.style_label_left, color=color.new(#7b2fff, 10), textcolor=color.white, size=size.small)
    if showAFE and not na(afe_activeDest)
        afe_arrow := line.new(bar_index, close, bar_index + 18, afe_activeDest, color=color.new(#c9a0ff, 10), width=2, style=line.style_arrow_right)



// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// CONTEXTUAL WAVE ARCS (v90) — restored: L4 (H4) + L2 (H1) big-degree arcs only,
// drawn as curved dashed polylines through each layer's confirmed swing pivots.
// (Finer L1/L0 arcs were dropped to respect Pine's token limit.)
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
showCtxArcs = input.bool(true, "Show Contextual Wave Arcs",   group=GRP_VIS)
ctxArcL4    = input.bool(true, "  Arc: L4 (H4)",              group=GRP_VIS)
ctxArcL2    = input.bool(true, "  Arc: L2 (H1)",              group=GRP_VIS)
ctxArcMax   = input.int (14,   "  Arc Pivot Memory (points)", group=GRP_VIS, minval=3, maxval=40)

f_arcPush(array<chart.point> _pts, float _price, int _maxPts) =>
    array.push(_pts, chart.point.from_time(time, _price))
    if array.size(_pts) > _maxPts
        array.shift(_pts)
    array.size(_pts)

var array<chart.point> arcL4pts = array.new<chart.point>()
var polyline arcL4 = na
var float arcL4_shp = na
var float arcL4_slp = na
if showCtxArcs and ctxArcL4
    bool _nH = not na(se240_sh) and se240_sh != arcL4_shp
    bool _nL = not na(se240_sl) and se240_sl != arcL4_slp
    if _nH
        int _i7 = f_arcPush(arcL4pts, se240_sh, ctxArcMax)
    if _nL
        int _i8 = f_arcPush(arcL4pts, se240_sl, ctxArcMax)
    arcL4_shp := se240_sh
    arcL4_slp := se240_sl
    if (_nH or _nL) and array.size(arcL4pts) >= 2
        if not na(arcL4)
            polyline.delete(arcL4)
        arcL4 := polyline.new(arcL4pts, curved=true, xloc=xloc.bar_time, line_color=color.new(color.orange, 15), line_style=line.style_dashed, line_width=3)

var array<chart.point> arcL2pts = array.new<chart.point>()
var polyline arcL2 = na
var float arcL2_shp = na
var float arcL2_slp = na
if showCtxArcs and ctxArcL2
    bool _nH = not na(se60_sh) and se60_sh != arcL2_shp
    bool _nL = not na(se60_sl) and se60_sl != arcL2_slp
    if _nH
        int _i1 = f_arcPush(arcL2pts, se60_sh, ctxArcMax)
    if _nL
        int _i2 = f_arcPush(arcL2pts, se60_sl, ctxArcMax)
    arcL2_shp := se60_sh
    arcL2_slp := se60_sl
    if (_nH or _nL) and array.size(arcL2pts) >= 2
        if not na(arcL2)
            polyline.delete(arcL2)
        arcL2 := polyline.new(arcL2pts, curved=true, xloc=xloc.bar_time, line_color=color.new(color.yellow, 25), line_style=line.style_dashed, line_width=2)

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// FRACTAL STACK ALERTS (v90) — fire when the fixed-layer stack flips or fully aligns.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
bool stackFlippedBull  = fractalStackDir == 1  and fractalStackDir[1] != 1
bool stackFlippedBear  = fractalStackDir == -1 and fractalStackDir[1] != -1
bool stackFullyAligned = fractalStackScore >= 100.0 and fractalStackScore[1] < 100.0
alertcondition(stackFlippedBull,  title="Fractal Stack flip BULL", message="Fractal stack flipped bullish")
alertcondition(stackFlippedBear,  title="Fractal Stack flip BEAR", message="Fractal stack flipped bearish")
alertcondition(stackFullyAligned, title="All Layers Aligned",      message="All fixed layers aligned (100% stack)")
